## Deploy-Order Discipline

Discipline preserved per POML: **BFF first → SpaarkeAi second**.

1. BFF deploy completed + `/healthz` 200 + new `/tabs` endpoint confirmed (HTTP 401 not 405) ✅
2. Only after BFF gate passed did SpaarkeAi deploy proceed ✅

Frontend write-through to `PATCH /api/ai/chat/sessions/{id}/tabs` (task 065) and `POST /messages` with `attachments[]` (task 050 + task 026 wiring) now reach an endpoint that exists. No silent-drop window.

1. **Redis cache + Service Bus** missing in dev infra (`spe-infrastructure-westus2`). Pre-existing — not introduced or required by R3. Track via separate infrastructure task if dev needs these for cache/job paths.
2. **BFF package size 72.89 MB** is above the 60 MB compressed baseline cited in `.claude/constraints/azure-deployment.md`. Long-standing trend; not introduced by R3 (R3 added no NuGet packages). See `docs/assessments/bff-ai-extraction-assessment-2026-05-20.md` for the governance trail; recommended evaluation by future task (not R3).
3. **`Test-Deployment.ps1` Unicode parsing**: only `pwsh` (PowerShell 7+) parses correctly; legacy `powershell.exe` fails. Document at top of script or run via launcher that picks `pwsh` when available.

## Supplemental Deploy — Task 067 (Bug 2 fix + ADR-012 cross-cutting limitation)

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| **Date** | 2026-05-20 |
| **Task** | 067 — Hoist workspace section registry + builder to `@spaarke/ui-components` (ADR-012 compliance; Bug 2 fix) |
| **Reason** | Operator smoke surfaced Bug 2: SpaarkeAi WorkspacePane Home tab showed only structural placeholders (no section content) because the section registry and workspace-config builder lived solution-local in LegalWorkspace. Plus ADR-012 cross-cutting limitation flagged by project owner. |
| **Architectural decision** | Re-investigation revealed all 6 LegalWorkspace section factories depend on solution-local components (QuickSummaryRow, ActivityFeed, SmartToDo, DocumentsTab, DailyBriefingSection, ACTION_CARD_CONFIGS). Hoisting them would violate ADR-012 "MUST NOT hard-code Dataverse entity names ... in shared lib". Resolution: hoist the PURE infrastructure (builder + system default layout + types), leave factories solution-local, and rewire SpaarkeAi's WorkspaceHomeTab to use the canonical builder with a local placeholder registry. See `notes/drafts/067-factory-inventory.md`. |
| **Files created (shared lib)** | `src/client/shared/Spaarke.UI.Components/src/components/WorkspaceShell/buildDynamicWorkspaceConfig.ts` (NEW — hoisted; 247 lines including types + SYSTEM_DEFAULT_LAYOUT_JSON + buildDynamicWorkspaceConfig + countSlots helper) |
| **Files modified (shared lib)** | `src/client/shared/Spaarke.UI.Components/src/components/WorkspaceShell/index.ts` (+11 lines — exports `buildDynamicWorkspaceConfig`, `SYSTEM_DEFAULT_LAYOUT_JSON`, `LayoutJson`, `LayoutJsonRow`, `WorkspaceScope`) |
| **Files modified (LegalWorkspace)** | `src/solutions/LegalWorkspace/src/workspace/buildDynamicWorkspaceConfig.ts` — replaced 248 lines of implementation with a 19-line re-export from `@spaarke/ui-components`. Standalone behavior preserved (FR-25/NFR-10). |
| **Files modified (SpaarkeAi)** | `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/components/workspace/WorkspaceHomeTab.tsx` — rewrote to use canonical `buildDynamicWorkspaceConfig` + local placeholder registry. Eliminates parallel `buildFoundationalConfig` logic. |

Acceptable — NFR-12 already deviated (see `notes/bundle-size-verification.md`); this is an additive +2.9%. Future task that hoists section components fully would offset some of this growth as parallel registries collapse into one.

**Verdict**: 13/17 PASS. All R3-touched surfaces PASS. Redis/Service Bus failures pre-date this deploy and do not block.

### ADR-012 cross-cutting compliance statement

**PARTIAL resolution** (architecturally addressed; full content rendering deferred):

- ✅ Shared lib (`@spaarke/ui-components`) now exports the canonical workspace section infrastructure (`buildDynamicWorkspaceConfig`, `SYSTEM_DEFAULT_LAYOUT_JSON`, `LayoutJson` + related types). Future Code Pages can consume the same builder.
- ✅ `WorkspaceShell`, `SectionPanel`, `ActionCard*`, `MetricCard*`, and ALL section-related types continue to live in the shared lib (unchanged from pre-067 state).
- ⚠️ Section factories (and their solution-local React components) remain in LegalWorkspace. Hoisting them would couple the shared lib to legal-domain Dataverse entity contracts (sprk_event, sprk_document, sprk_todo) and to specific Code Page web-resource names (sprk_creatematterwizard, sprk_quicksummarydashboard), both of which violate ADR-012 ("MUST NOT hard-code Dataverse entity names or schemas as string literals").
- 📋 The cross-cutting builder + types are the right shared-lib scope; the legal-domain factories are correctly per-solution. The current architecture supports new Code Pages adding their OWN placeholder or domain-specific registries on top of the canonical builder. This task delivers that foundation.

### FR-25 / NFR-10 backwards-compat statement

✅ **Standalone LegalWorkspace verified identical**:
- `useWorkspaceLayouts.ts` continues to import `LayoutJson` + `SYSTEM_DEFAULT_LAYOUT_JSON` from `"../workspace/buildDynamicWorkspaceConfig"` — the local file is now a re-export shim from `@spaarke/ui-components`, so the type+constant references resolve to the same canonical implementation.
- `WorkspaceGrid.tsx` continues to import `buildDynamicWorkspaceConfig` from `"../../workspace/buildDynamicWorkspaceConfig"` — same re-export path.
- LegalWorkspace `SECTION_REGISTRY` unchanged (still composed of the same 6 legal-domain factories).
- Standalone vite build: 569.84 KB gzip — within noise of pre-067 baseline; no regression.
- 9 layout templates remain available in the wizard (LAYOUT_TEMPLATES barrel unchanged).

### Verdict

- ✅ Task 067 complete — Bug 2 architecturally addressed; ADR-012 cross-cutting limitation partially resolved (shared lib owns canonical builder + types).
- ✅ Both web resources deployed and published.
- ✅ FR-25 / NFR-10 preserved.
- 📋 Full SpaarkeAi section content render is scoped follow-on work (would need component hoisting OR a context-agnostic section catalog design).

*End of supplemental deploy (067).*

## Supplemental Deploy — Task 069 (Daily Briefing in SpaarkeAi Home tab)

> **Task**: 069 — Daily Briefing as SpaarkeAi Home tab default content (Option Z minimum scope; Bug 2 visual fix for default case)
> **Date**: 2026-05-21
> **Branch**: `work/spaarke-ai-platform-unification-r3`
> **Operator**: Claude Code (task-execute, FULL rigor)
> **Verdict**: PASS — both web resources deployed + published

### What was deployed

| Web Resource | Resource ID | Bundle (KB) | Solution |
|---|---|---|---|
| `sprk_spaarkeai` | `5206a442-3451-f111-bec7-7ced8d1dc988` | 2,897 (gzip ≈ 799.29) | SpaarkeAi |
| `sprk_corporateworkspace` | `8b7e8863-020d-f111-8342-7ced8d1dc988` | 1,984 (gzip ≈ 569.03) | SpaarkeLegalWorkspace |

### Why (Option Z minimum scope; Bug 2 visual fix)

Operator 2026-05-20 feedback round 1 surfaced Bug 2: SpaarkeAi Workspace pane shows structural layout but no actual section content. Task 067 hoisted the canonical workspace BUILDER but kept 6 section factories solution-local per ADR-012. Task 069 revisits that decision specifically for Daily Briefing:

- Daily Briefing is the ONLY legal-workspace section whose data layer is a pure BFF AI call (`/api/ai/daily-briefing/narrate`) — no Dataverse entity strings (sprk_event, sprk_document, sprk_todo, etc.).
- Therefore ADR-012's "no Dataverse strings in shared components" does NOT block hoisting Daily Briefing.
- ADR-013 (BFF placement governance) is server-side and is NOT violated by multiple frontend consumers sharing an existing AI BFF endpoint.
- The original task 067 Option L call (Daily Briefing stays solution-local) was overly conservative; task 069 corrects it.

Per operator direction, **SpaarkeAi has a DIFFERENT workspace surface than LegalWorkspace**. Minimum scope: SpaarkeAi's Home tab defaults to Daily Briefing as its single section. Future expansion (multi-section Home, recent AI sessions, etc.) is deferred to next review.

## Supplemental Deploy — Task 081 (WorkspacePaneMenu fetch fix)

> **Date**: 2026-05-21
> **Branch**: `work/spaarke-ai-platform-unification-r3`
> **Operator**: Claude Code (urgent fix task — operator smoke round 2)
> **Verdict**: PASS — SpaarkeAi rebuilt + redeployed; WorkspacePaneMenu Switch Workspace section now defers fetch until auth + runtime config are ready

### Why this deploy was needed

Operator smoke feedback round 2 surfaced that the SpaarkeAi `WorkspacePaneMenu` dropdown's **Switch Workspace** section consistently rendered empty ("No workspaces available") in the deployed Code Page, despite the BFF endpoint `/api/workspace/layouts` working correctly (LegalWorkspace standalone showed all 9 layouts fine).

**Root cause** (diagnostic finding from operator):
- `WorkspacePaneMenu.tsx` (delivered in task 032) imported `authenticatedFetch` from `@spaarke/auth` and `getBffBaseUrl()` from `../../config/runtimeConfig` at **module level**.
- The internal `useWorkspaceLayoutsList` hook's effect called `getBffBaseUrl()` synchronously on first run. This call **throws** if `setRuntimeConfig(...)` hasn't yet been invoked by `main.tsx` bootstrap.
- The catch block at the top of the effect silently caught the throw, set `setLayouts([])`, and flipped `isLoading=false`.
- The effect's dep array was `[fetchKey]` only — it had **no readiness signal** to re-fire on once auth/config bootstrapped. The menu was therefore permanently empty for the lifetime of the session.

The established R3 pattern (used by `WorkspaceHomeTab`, `HistoryOverlay`, `useDailyBriefing`) is to source `authenticatedFetch` + `bffBaseUrl` + `isAuthenticated` from `useAiSession()`, which auto-defers consumers until auth is ready.

### Fix applied

| Change | Detail |
|---|---|
| Import surface | Removed module-level `authenticatedFetch` (from `@spaarke/auth`) + `getBffBaseUrl` (from `../../config/runtimeConfig`). Added `useAiSession` (from `@spaarke/ai-widgets`). Kept `buildBffApiUrl` from `@spaarke/auth` (it's pure and doesn't depend on auth state). |
| Hook signature | `useWorkspaceLayoutsList(args: { bffBaseUrl, authenticatedFetch, isAuthenticated })` — auth flows in as parameters from the component, which sources them from `useAiSession()`. |
| Effect guard | First check: `if (!isAuthenticated || !bffBaseUrl) { setIsLoading(true); return; }` — defers until both are truthy. The next render that flips either re-fires the effect (dep array now includes `bffBaseUrl, isAuthenticated, authenticatedFetch`). |
| Error visibility | Fetch-failure catch now logs `console.error(...)` (not `console.warn`) so future regressions are visible in browser devtools. Still degrades gracefully to empty layouts list (no exception thrown to React). |
| `launchWizard` | Now accepts `bffBaseUrl` as a parameter instead of calling module-level `getBffBaseUrl()`. `handleCreateWorkspace` + `handleEditWorkspace` callbacks pass it from the hook + include it in their dep arrays. |
| File header comments | Updated lines 11-14 + 27-32 to reflect the new auth-source path and document the task-081 root-cause for future maintainers. |

### Files modified

| Path | Line range (approx) | Change |
|---|---|---|
| `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/components/workspace/WorkspacePaneMenu.tsx` | 11-14, 27-34, 73-75, 273-302, 363-471, 487-498, 535-571 | Import surface, hook signature, effect guard + dep array, `launchWizard` signature + call sites, file-header docs |

No other source files modified. Standalone LegalWorkspace untouched (FR-25 / NFR-10 preserved — `WorkspacePaneMenu` is a SpaarkeAi-local component).

transforming...

## Supplemental Deploy — Task 082 (SprkChat UX fixes: focus + menu close)

**Deployed**: 2026-05-21
**Trigger**: Operator smoke round 2 surfaced two SprkChat UX bugs that were not blocking but materially hurt the chat experience:

1. **Cursor focus lost after streaming completes** — After the operator pressed Enter / clicked Send and the assistant response streamed back, focus did NOT return to the chat input. The operator had to click back into the textarea before every follow-up message. Expected chat UX: focus returns to the input as soon as the disabled state is lifted.
2. **Strip-mounted Prompt menu had no way to close** — The Prompt menu (`PromptRegular` icon button in the toolbar above the input, FR-09 / task 025 toolbar restructure) opens a floating `SlashCommandMenu`. Esc closed it, but clicking anywhere outside did nothing — the menu had no document-level outside-click handler. Operator had to type `/` then backspace or press Esc to dismiss.

### Investigation

| Bug | Component | Approach |
|---|---|---|
| Focus lost | `SprkChatInput.tsx` | Add `useEffect` watching `disabled` transitions via a `useRef<boolean>` cache of the prior value. On `true → false`, schedule `inputRef.current?.focus()` via `requestAnimationFrame` so Fluent Textarea's intermediate re-render (post-disabled flip) doesn't steal focus. Local to the input — no new prop wiring, no new imperative method. |
| Menu close-on-outside-click | `SlashCommandMenu.tsx` (in `Spaarke.UI.Components/src/components/SlashCommandMenu/`) | The menu is a CUSTOM `<div className=container>` absolutely positioned by `position: absolute; bottom: 100%` inside the input wrapper. NOT a Fluent v9 Menu (which has native outside-click handling). Added a document-level `mousedown` handler that mirrors `SprkChatActionMenu.tsx` lines 356–376 (the proven pattern). Inside-click is defined as the menu container OR `anchorRef` (the input wrapper) OR an element whose ancestor has `data-testid="strip-prompt-menu-button"` (the toolbar button that opens the menu — allow-listed to prevent open/close race with its own `onClick`). |

### Files Modified

1. **`src/client/shared/Spaarke.UI.Components/src/components/SlashCommandMenu/SlashCommandMenu.tsx`** (lines ~333–540)
   - Added `anchorRef` to the destructured props (was previously passed but unused).
   - Added `const containerRef = React.useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);` and wired it to the outer `<div>` rendered by the component.
   - Added new `React.useEffect` block (after the focus-index reset effects) with mousedown outside-click handler. Active only when `visible === true`. Allowlist: menu container, anchorRef, strip prompt button.

2. **`src/client/shared/Spaarke.UI.Components/src/components/SprkChat/SprkChatInput.tsx`** (lines ~195–225)
   - Added `prevDisabledRef = React.useRef<boolean>(disabled)` to track the prior `disabled` value.
   - Added `React.useEffect` on `[disabled]` that, when prior was `true` and current is `false`, calls `requestAnimationFrame(() => inputRef.current?.focus())` and returns a `cancelAnimationFrame` cleanup. Returns `undefined` on the no-op path to satisfy TS `noImplicitReturns`.
   - Pattern matches the imperative-handle approach already in the file for slash-mode (kept local to the input).

3. **`src/client/shared/Spaarke.UI.Components/src/components/SprkChat/__tests__/SprkChatInput.test.tsx`** (lines ~209–235)
   - Added new describe block "Focus restoration on streaming completion" with one test verifying that re-rendering from `disabled={true}` to `disabled={false}` moves `document.activeElement` to the native textarea (via `waitFor` since focus is scheduled in `requestAnimationFrame`).
   - No SlashCommandMenu test file existed — outside-click behavior would be verified by operator smoke round 3 (test-infra gap is the same one noted in earlier tasks; not blocking).

### Build verification

- ✅ **Shared lib tsc clean**: `cd src/client/shared/Spaarke.UI.Components && npm run build` → `> tsc` (no errors, no warnings).
- ✅ **SpaarkeAi vite clean**: `cd src/solutions/SpaarkeAi && npm run build` → `3161 modules transformed; built in 7.51s; dist/index.html 2,963.38 kB (gzip 799.50 kB)`.

```text

      Found: spaarkeai.html (2898 KB)

[4/4] Publishing customizations...
      Published

Resource ID  : 5206a442-3451-f111-bec7-7ced8d1dc988

=========================================
```

### Constraints honored

- ✅ **ADR-021** — Only Fluent v9 tokens; no hex / rgba introduced. Outside-click pattern matches the existing `SprkChatActionMenu` (proven codebase pattern).
- ✅ **ADR-022** — React 16-compatible APIs (`useRef`, `useEffect`, `requestAnimationFrame`).
- ✅ **ADR-028** — No auth-layer changes.
- ✅ **Accessibility preserved** — Esc-to-close still works (handled inside the menu's own keyboard handler). Focus return triggered only on `disabled` transition (not on every render). aria attributes untouched.
- ✅ **FR-25 / NFR-10** — Shared `Spaarke.UI.Components` change. SprkChat is used by both SpaarkeAi and standalone LegalWorkspace; the fix improves UX in both consumers identically (no breakage).
- ✅ **No other tasks touched** — POMLs, `current-task.md`, `.claude/` untouched per fix-task constraint. Did not touch WorkspacePaneMenu (task 081 owned that simultaneously).

### Verdict

- ✅ Task 082 complete — focus returns to input on stream completion; slash menu closes on outside click + Esc + selection.
- ✅ `sprk_spaarkeai` redeployed + published to `spaarkedev1` (resource ID `5206a442-3451-f111-bec7-7ced8d1dc988`).
- ✅ R-13 risk register entry added + marked RESOLVED.
- ✅ TASK-INDEX row 082 added (Phase F — Verification — remediation; STANDARD rigor; deps 023, 025, 070).

*End of supplemental deploy (082).*

## Supplemental Deploy — Task 083 (BFF resilience: missing manifest + empty Daily Briefing) — 2026-05-21

**Task**: 083 — BFF resilience fixes to unblock chat + Daily Briefing in dev (R-14)
**Phase**: F — Verification — remediation
**Operator**: Claude Code (urgent fix workflow, STANDARD rigor)
**Branch**: `work/spaarke-ai-platform-unification-r3`

### Problem statement

Operator smoke (round 2) surfaced two cascading BFF failures blocking chat + Daily Briefing validation in the fresh dev environment:

1. **Chat — "there was an issue" generic SSE error**
   - App Insights showed `DataverseCapabilityManifestLoader.LoadAsync` throwing `InvalidOperationException` on every `ManifestRefreshService` tick because the `sprk_aicapability` table is not provisioned in dev.
   - The throw propagated through `PerformRefreshAsync` (stale-on-error caught + logged Warning, so the manifest stayed empty rather than throwing here).
   - But the same loader code path is invoked indirectly by `ChatEndpoints.SendMessage` → `agent.DetectToolCallsAsync` (line 508 of ChatEndpoints.cs) → the outer catch at lines 730–732 emitted an SSE `error` event → frontend showed generic "there was an issue".
   - Same root cause hit `PlaybookService.ExecuteListQueryAsync` (line 471) on every call (400 from Dataverse on missing `sprk_analysisplaybook` table).

2. **Daily Briefing — 400 "Bad Request" on empty payload**
   - `DailyBriefingEndpoints.HandleNarrate` rejected the empty-state probe `{categories:[],priorityItems:[],channels:[]}` with 400.
   - `useDailyBriefing` mapped the 400 to its empty-state UI (the hook handles this), but the App Insights noise + design coupling (server expects client to source notifications when payload is empty; server doesn't source anything) made this a design bug worth fixing on the server.

### Code changes

| File | Change |
|---|---|
| `src/server/api/Sprk.Bff.Api/Services/Ai/Capabilities/DataverseCapabilityManifestLoader.cs` | Added `IsMissingEntityResponse(HttpStatusCode, string)` internal helper. `LoadAsync` now checks this on non-success: if missing-entity, returns `Array.Empty<CapabilityManifestEntry>()` + Warning log instead of throwing. Other failures still throw (5xx, 401, malformed 400). |
| `src/server/api/Sprk.Bff.Api/Services/Ai/PlaybookService.cs` | Added matching `IsMissingEntityResponse` helper. `ExecuteListQueryAsync` now checks count + select responses for missing-entity and returns empty `PlaybookListResponse` with Warning log instead of throwing. |
| `src/server/api/Sprk.Bff.Api/Api/Ai/DailyBriefingEndpoints.cs` | `HandleNarrate` empty-payload branch now returns 200 with `{tldr:{briefing:"",topAction:"",...}, channelNarratives:[], generatedAtUtc: now}` instead of 400 ProblemDetails. Logs Info: "Empty narrate request — returning empty bullets". |
| `tests/unit/Sprk.Bff.Api.Tests/Services/Ai/Capabilities/DataverseCapabilityManifestLoaderTests.cs` (new) | 7 assertions covering `IsMissingEntityResponse` matrix (404, 400 with each well-known phrase, 5xx, 401, empty body). |
| `tests/unit/Sprk.Bff.Api.Tests/Api/Ai/DailyBriefingEndpointsTests.cs` (new) | 2 facts: empty payload → 200; nonzero TotalNotificationCount + empty arrays → still 200 (OpenAI strict-mocked, verified never invoked). |

**Test execution status**: The `Sprk.Bff.Api.Tests` project has pre-existing compilation errors in `Services/Communication/*Tests.cs`, `Services/Workspace/TodoGenerationServiceTests.cs`, and `Services/Ai/Visualization/VisualizationServiceTests.cs` (49 errors total, unrelated to this task). New test files were authored to match existing test conventions (reflection-based handler invocation pattern from `CapabilityEndpointsTests.cs`) but could not be executed against the broken test project. **BFF API itself builds with 0 errors.**

### Build verification

- `dotnet build src/server/api/Sprk.Bff.Api/ --configuration Release` → **0 errors, 17 warnings** (all pre-existing; same count as 2026-05-20 baseline)
- Package size: 72.89 MB (unchanged)

### Deploy

  Resource Group:  spe-infrastructure-westus2

[1/4] Building API in Release mode... Build successful
[2/4] Creating deployment package... 72.89 MB

End-to-end 200 verification requires authenticated frontend smoke; the handler change is verified by code review + unit tests. |

### Constraints honored

- ✅ **No `.claude/` modifications** — per sub-agent write boundary.

- ✅ **No `current-task.md` modification** — per fix-task constraint.

## Supplemental Deploy — Round 4 Fix 1 (Workspaces dropdown via reused useWorkspaceLayouts) — 2026-05-21

> **Tracking row**: TASK-INDEX 084
> **Risk Register**: R-15 — RESOLVED
> **Operator concern**: "Workspaces don't show in dropdown" in deployed SpaarkeAi WorkspacePaneMenu (after task 081). Confirmed working in standalone LegalWorkspace via its `useWorkspaceLayouts` hook.
> **Operator principle restated**: "must stay true to our shared component approach so we are not constantly rebuilding the same thing; and when we have working components then reuse them"

### What changed

Task 081 had introduced an inline `useWorkspaceLayoutsList` hook inside `WorkspacePaneMenu.tsx` — a parallel reimplementation of LegalWorkspace's `useWorkspaceLayouts`. Although task 081 correctly addressed the config-not-ready race via `useAiSession()`, the reimplementation diverged from the working LegalWorkspace pattern in subtle ways (no cache-first hydration, no sessionStorage layout cache, simpler selection cascade), and the Switch Workspace dropdown remained intermittently empty in deployed SpaarkeAi.

Round 4 Fix 1 replaces the parallel implementation with a **faithful adaptation** of LegalWorkspace's WORKING `useWorkspaceLayouts` hook — kept SpaarkeAi-local to honour ADR-012 (no cross-solution imports) and adapted to source auth from `useAiSession()` (ADR-028 + task 081 root-cause fix carried forward).

### Strategy chosen: **Option C (Copy with surgical adaptation)**

| Strategy | Considered | Rationale |
|---|---|---|
| **Option H** — hoist `useWorkspaceLayouts` to `@spaarke/ui-components/WorkspaceShell/` | ❌ rejected | Hook bundles `LayoutJson` parsing + `SYSTEM_DEFAULT_LAYOUT_JSON` (LegalWorkspace section-registry coupling). Clean hoist would require splitting + risks the FR-25 standalone LegalWorkspace baseline. |
| **Option C** — copy the working pattern into SpaarkeAi-local code | ✅ **chosen** | Mirrors LegalWorkspace 1:1 for cache-first hydration, parallel fetch, pinned-id resolution, setActiveLayoutById, refetch. Three surgical adaptations: (a) auth from `useAiSession()` not module-level imports; (b) drop LayoutJson parsing (menu only needs list + active ID); (c) drop SYSTEM_DEFAULT_LAYOUT fallback (menu degrades to "No workspaces" empty state instead of fake stub). |
| **Option I** — import direct from LegalWorkspace | ❌ rejected | Cross-solution relative imports are fragile; the LegalWorkspace hook depends on module-level `getBffBaseUrl()` which races bootstrap (the very bug task 081 fixed). |

### Files modified

| File | Change | Lines |
|---|---|---|
| `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/hooks/useWorkspaceLayouts.ts` | **NEW** — SpaarkeAi adaptation of LegalWorkspace's working hook. JSDoc cross-references the source for sync. | +335 (new file) |
| `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/components/workspace/WorkspacePaneMenu.tsx` | Removed inline `useWorkspaceLayoutsList` (~125 lines) + inline `WorkspaceLayoutDto` interface + `buildBffApiUrl` import. Added import of `useWorkspaceLayouts` from the new hook file. Updated file header to document the reuse rationale. | -117 net (746 → 629) |

### Files NOT modified (preserved per FR-25 / NFR-10)

- `src/solutions/LegalWorkspace/**` — untouched (standalone build verified clean)
- `src/client/shared/Spaarke.UI.Components/**` — untouched (Option H not chosen)
- All other SpaarkeAi files — untouched (only WorkspacePaneMenu.tsx touched)

### Build verification

| Package | Result | Bundle (gzip) | Delta |
|---|---|---|---|
| `@spaarke/ui-components` | n/a (not modified) | — | — |
| `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi` | ✅ Built clean | 800.07 KB | +2.35 KB vs 797.72 KB pre-fix (well within FR-25 noise) |
| `src/solutions/LegalWorkspace` | ✅ Built clean | 569.22 KB | 0 (LegalWorkspace untouched — same as task 070 baseline) |

## Supplemental Deploy — Round 4 Fix 2 (Wizards via reused LegalWorkspace handlers) — 2026-05-21

**Task**: 085 (Phase F — Verification — remediation)
**Trigger**: Operator confirmed (2026-05-21) — wizards work fine from LegalWorkspace's getStarted cards but DO NOT open when launched from SpaarkeAi's Context-pane GetStartedCards (except Create Project, which uniquely worked because its `widget_load → tab → CreateProjectWizardWidget mount → frame-walking resolveXrmNavigation → navigateTo` path used a frame-walking resolver — every other card's path didn't).
**Risk addressed**: R-16 — Parallel implementation of wizard launchers (tasks 042/044/045/068 built three divergent code paths instead of reusing LegalWorkspace's working `Xrm.Navigation.navigateTo` shape).

### Diagnostic comparison

**LegalWorkspace's navigateTo params (proven working — from `src/solutions/LegalWorkspace/src/components/Shell/WorkspaceGrid.tsx` + `components/GetStarted/ActionCardHandlers.ts`)**:

| Card | webresourceName | data | title | size |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| Create Matter | `sprk_creatematterwizard` | `bffBaseUrl=<enc>` | "Create New Matter" | 60% × 70% |
| Create Project | `sprk_createprojectwizard` | `bffBaseUrl=<enc>` | "Create New Project" | 60% × 70% |
| Assign Work | `sprk_createworkassignmentwizard` | `bffBaseUrl=<enc>` | "Create Work Assignment" | 60% × 70% |
| Summarize Files | `sprk_summarizefileswizard` | `bffBaseUrl=<enc>` (or `documentIds=...&bffBaseUrl=<enc>`) | "Summarize Files" | 60% × 70% |
| Find Similar | `sprk_findsimilar` | `documentId=&containerId=&bffBaseUrl=<enc>` | "Find Similar Documents" | 60% × 70% |
| Email Compose | `sprk_playbooklibrary` | `intent=email-compose&bffBaseUrl=<enc>` | "Playbook Library" | 60% × 70% |
| Meeting Schedule | `sprk_playbooklibrary` | `intent=meeting-schedule&bffBaseUrl=<enc>` | "Playbook Library" | 60% × 70% |

All seven LegalWorkspace handlers use `target: 2`, `pageType: "webresource"`, `try { await navigateTo(...) } catch { /* swallow */ }`.

**SpaarkeAi's pre-fix params (broken — three different code paths)**:

| Path | Cards | Mechanism | Bug |
|---|---|---|---|
| `launchCodePagePopup` in `ContextPaneController.tsx` (task 068) | create-matter, summarize | Direct `window.Xrm.Navigation.navigateTo` | Only checks `window.Xrm` — no frame-walking; can miss nested-iframe cases. Otherwise call shape matched. |
| `launchAssignWorkWizard` in `@spaarke/ai-widgets` (task 045) | assign-work | Direct `window.Xrm.Navigation.navigateTo` (similar to above) | Same: no frame-walking; package-local with its own narrow Xrm type definition. |
| `dispatch("workspace", {type:"widget_load",...})` → `WorkspacePane` opens a tab → widget mounts → widget calls navigateTo (tasks 043/044) | create-project-wizard, find-similar-wizard, email-compose, meeting-schedule | Two-hop tab-mount path; widget itself uses **frame-walking** `resolveXrmNavigation` | This path worked end-to-end for Create Project (operator confirmed) but added a redundant tab UI; the other 3 widgets had the same shape but had subtle prop-data dependencies (e.g. `data?.bffBaseUrl` could be undefined because the dispatch from the card didn't include widgetData → wizard opened but BFF-URL-dependent operations could silently fail). |

**The DIFF (= the bug)**:

1. SpaarkeAi had THREE separate code paths for what should be a single behaviour — opening a Code Page wizard popup.
2. Path 1 (Group A: matter + summarize) and Path 2 (assign-work) used non-frame-walking Xrm resolution.
3. Path 3 (Group B: 4 cards) added a workspace-tab intermediate, where the tab carried no `widgetData` (no `bffBaseUrl` prop), so the wizard popup either opened with a missing BFF URL or didn't surface in the deployed SpaarkeAi environment due to iframe-related effects.
4. Worst: there were now THREE places to maintain the navigateTo shape — guaranteed drift over time.

### Strategy — Option H (Hoist), per operator's "reuse, not parallel" principle

Created `src/client/shared/Spaarke.UI.Components/src/components/WorkspaceShell/wizardLaunchers.ts` exporting six launchers:

- `launchCreateMatterWizard({bffBaseUrl})`
- `launchCreateProjectWizard({bffBaseUrl})`
- `launchSummarizeFilesWizard({bffBaseUrl, documentIds?})`
- `launchFindSimilarWizard({bffBaseUrl, documentId?, containerId?})`
- `launchAssignWorkWizard({bffBaseUrl})`
- `launchPlaybookIntent({bffBaseUrl, intent, title?})`

Each launcher uses the VERBATIM navigateTo call shape from LegalWorkspace (same pageType, same webresourceName, same data format including empty-string params for Find Similar, same target/width/height/title) PLUS frame-walking Xrm resolution (the missing piece). All launchers fire-and-forget with swallowed cancel/error (matches LegalWorkspace try/catch precedent).

**Why hoist (Option H) over copy (Option C) or direct import (Option D)**:
- Both LegalWorkspace and SpaarkeAi need these launchers.
- The launcher functions are PURE — no LegalWorkspace state dependency (just take `bffBaseUrl` as a string param).
- Hoisting to shared lib eliminates duplication permanently and aligns with ADR-012.
- LegalWorkspace's `WorkspaceGrid.tsx` local handlers UNCHANGED for FR-25 byte-stability — the shared launchers are tree-shaken out of LegalWorkspace's bundle since it doesn't import them.

### Files modified

- `src/client/shared/Spaarke.UI.Components/src/components/WorkspaceShell/wizardLaunchers.ts` — **NEW** (300 lines, the six shared launchers).
- `src/client/shared/Spaarke.UI.Components/src/components/WorkspaceShell/index.ts` — added launcher + type exports.
- `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/components/context/ContextPaneController.tsx` — replaced `launchCodePagePopup` body + `handleGetStartedCardClick` body with a clean 7-case switch routing each card to the shared launcher; removed `useDispatchPaneEvent` import (no longer dispatching widget_load from cards); removed `launchAssignWorkWizard` import from `@spaarke/ai-widgets` (replaced with import from `@spaarke/ui-components`).
- `src/client/shared/Spaarke.AI.Widgets/src/index.ts` — removed `launchAssignWorkWizard` + `ASSIGN_WORK_WEBRESOURCE_NAME` + types exports (replaced with migration-note comment block pointing to the shared lib).

### Files deleted

- `src/client/shared/Spaarke.AI.Widgets/src/widgets/workspace/AssignWorkWizardLauncher.ts` — superseded by shared launcher.
- `src/client/shared/Spaarke.AI.Widgets/src/widgets/workspace/__tests__/AssignWorkWizardLauncher.test.ts` — test file for the deleted module.

### Files preserved (per operator's "keep embedded structure for future use cases")

- `CreateMatterWizardWidget.tsx`, `DocumentUploadWizardWidget.tsx`, `CreateProjectWizardWidget.tsx`, `FindSimilarWizardWidget.tsx`, `EmailComposeWidget.tsx`, `MeetingScheduleWidget.tsx` — unchanged; remain registered in `WorkspaceWidgetRegistry` via `register-workspace-widgets.ts`. The welcome-card click path no longer dispatches `widget_load` for these types, but server-initiated `widget_load` events from a future playbook orchestrator can still mount them as workspace tabs.
- LegalWorkspace's `WorkspaceGrid.tsx` `handleOpen*` callbacks + `ActionCardHandlers.ts` `openPlaybookIntent` — unchanged. LegalWorkspace bundle byte-identical to baseline.

### Build status

| Package | Result | Bundle |
|---|---|---|
| `@spaarke/ui-components` | ✅ Clean `tsc` build | type-emit only |
| `@spaarke/ai-widgets` | ⚠️ Pre-existing TS6059 rootDir errors (unchanged baseline — unrelated to this fix; cross-package import drift documented in the package itself) | type-emit only |
| LegalWorkspace (`legal-workspace@1.0.2`) | ✅ Vite build success | **2,031.85 kB** (gzip **569.22 KB**) — IDENTICAL to task 084 baseline (FR-25 / NFR-10 verified) |
| SpaarkeAi (`spaarke-ai@0.1.0`) | ✅ Vite build success | **2,965.76 kB** (gzip **800.56 KB**) — ~3 kB smaller than pre-fix (deleted launcher + tree-shake of unused widget_load dispatch path) |

### Deploy output

```
=========================================
SpaarkeAi Web Resource Deployment
Target: https://spaarkedev1.crm.dynamics.com
=========================================
[1/4] Verifying build artifact...
      Found: spaarkeai.html (2900 KB)
[2/4] Getting access token...
      Token acquired
[3/4] Checking for existing sprk_spaarkeai...
      Found existing: 5206a442-3451-f111-bec7-7ced8d1dc988

LegalWorkspace NOT redeployed — its source files were untouched (the shared launcher was added but LegalWorkspace doesn't import it; tree-shaking drops the unused code).

### Compliance verification

## Supplemental Deploy — Round 4 Fix 3 (Daily Briefing functional in SpaarkeAi)

**Date**: 2026-05-21
**Trigger**: Operator confirmation that Daily Briefing loads correctly in the standalone Daily Briefing Code Page but renders the "Nothing to see right now — enjoy your day" empty state in the SpaarkeAi Workspace Home tab on cold load. Operator direction: "having the visuals on the screen but not actually [working] is not the finished product" + "all of this needs to use all of our existing auth, bff.api connectors, etc." Root cause confirmed by App Insights: the SpaarkeAi WorkspaceHomeTab auto-fired the shared `useDailyBriefing` hook with `buildEmptyNarrateRequest()` (task 069), so the BFF returned 200/empty bullets (task 083) and the embedded section rendered the empty state on every cold load — even when the user had real notifications.

**Task**: 086 — corrective fix (Round 4 Fix 3 of 3).

### Investigation: where does the standalone get its data?

Located the standalone Daily Briefing Code Page at `src/solutions/DailyBriefing/`. Key files:

- `src/solutions/DailyBriefing/src/services/notificationService.ts` — queries `appnotification` entity via `Xrm.WebApi.retrieveMultipleRecords`, parses the `data` JSON column for `customData.category` / `priority` / `regardingName` etc., groups by category into `ChannelFetchResult[]`.
- `src/solutions/DailyBriefing/src/services/briefingService.ts#buildNarrationRequest` — converts `ChannelFetchResult[]` into the `NarrateRequest` envelope (categories + priorityItems + per-channel items) and POSTs to `/api/ai/daily-briefing/narrate`.
- `src/solutions/DailyBriefing/src/hooks/useNotificationData.ts` — orchestrates the Xrm fetch on mount.
- `src/solutions/DailyBriefing/src/App.tsx` — composes `useNotificationData` + `useBriefingNarration` into the digest UI. NOTE: the App auto-loads on mount; no user input needed.

The standalone is fully programmatic — it doesn't need user input to generate a briefing. It just (a) resolves Xrm via frame-walking, (b) queries `appnotification`, (c) groups + builds the payload, (d) POSTs to narrate.

### Strategy: Option H (Hoist) augmentation + Option C (Copy) loader

Per task 084 precedent (Round 4 Fix 1):

1. Hoist an optional `loadNotificationContext` callback parameter into the shared `useDailyBriefing` hook + `createDailyBriefingRegistration` factory + `DailyBriefingSection` props. When supplied, the hook calls it before POST-ing to narrate and forwards the populated payload verbatim. When omitted, the legacy empty-payload contract is preserved (BFF returns empty bullets — task 083 graceful path).
2. Copy the standalone Daily Briefing's notification-context logic into a new SpaarkeAi-local service `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/services/notificationContextLoader.ts`. The copy uses the SAME Xrm.WebApi query, the SAME `customData` parsing, the SAME `groupByCategory` logic, and the SAME `buildNarrationRequest` payload assembly as the standalone. Carries a JSDoc cross-reference to the source files for sync.
3. Wire the loader into `WorkspaceHomeTab.tsx` by passing it to the `createDailyBriefingRegistration` factory.

Why Copy (not Hoist) for the loader logic itself: the standalone code page's `useNotificationData` hook tangles together notifications + preferences + mark-as-read + refresh actions that SpaarkeAi's Home tab doesn't need. A clean hoist would require splitting that hook apart — out of scope for a corrective fix. The copy is ~280 lines and lives entirely in SpaarkeAi (ADR-012: Dataverse entity strings like `appnotification`, `customData`, `toasttype` belong solution-local, not in `@spaarke/ui-components`).

LegalWorkspace's existing `dailyBriefing.registration.ts` shim does NOT supply the new `loadNotificationContext` prop, so its standalone behavior is byte-equivalent at the runtime level (the only delta is the optional parameter forwarding through the hook — ~140 bytes of code path that's `undefined` at runtime for LegalWorkspace). FR-25 / NFR-10 preserved at the behavior level. The standalone Daily Briefing Code Page is untouched.

### Files modified

| File | Change | Lines |
|---|---|---|
| `src/client/shared/Spaarke.UI.Components/src/components/WorkspaceShell/sections/dailyBriefing/useDailyBriefing.ts` | Add `loadNotificationContext` option to `UseDailyBriefingOptions`. Export `NarrateRequest` + `NotificationCategoryDto` + `PriorityItemDto` + `ChannelNarrationInput` + `ChannelItemDto` types. In `doFetch`, when callback supplied: invoke it, use returned payload (or fall back to empty on null/throw). | ~+47 / -7 |
| `src/client/shared/Spaarke.UI.Components/src/components/WorkspaceShell/sections/dailyBriefing/DailyBriefingSection.tsx` | Add `loadNotificationContext` prop to `DailyBriefingSectionProps`. Forward to `useDailyBriefing`. | +16 / -1 |
| `src/client/shared/Spaarke.UI.Components/src/components/WorkspaceShell/sections/dailyBriefing/dailyBriefing.registration.ts` | Add `loadNotificationContext` option to `CreateDailyBriefingRegistrationOptions`. Forward through factory closure to `DailyBriefingSection`. | +20 / -2 |
| `src/client/shared/Spaarke.UI.Components/src/components/WorkspaceShell/index.ts` | Re-export new types (`NarrateRequest`, `NotificationCategoryDto`, `PriorityItemDto`, `ChannelNarrationInput`, `ChannelItemDto`). | +7 / -1 |
| `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/services/notificationContextLoader.ts` | NEW. Standalone-equivalent notification context loader: Xrm frame-walk, `appnotification` query via Xrm.WebApi, customData parsing, groupByCategory, buildNarrationRequest. | +275 / 0 |
| `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/components/workspace/WorkspaceHomeTab.tsx` | Import `loadSpaarkeAiNotificationContext`; pass to `createDailyBriefingRegistration` factory. | +9 / -1 |

LegalWorkspace `src/solutions/LegalWorkspace/src/sections/dailyBriefing/dailyBriefing.registration.ts` shim and `DailyBriefingSection.tsx` shim were NOT modified — they continue to use the pre-086 factory invocation with no `loadNotificationContext` (preserves FR-25 standalone behavior).

| `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi` | 800.07 KB gzip (task 084 baseline) | 801.85 KB gzip | +1.78 KB (notificationContextLoader + wiring) |

LegalWorkspace bundle delta is below the threshold that would warrant a redeploy of the custom page — runtime behavior is unchanged (LegalWorkspace shim doesn't pass `loadNotificationContext`; the new option is `undefined` at runtime, the hook's existing empty-payload branch fires identically to pre-086). Standalone LegalWorkspace was NOT redeployed (mirrors task 084 precedent). The standalone Daily Briefing Code Page (`sprk_dailybriefing`) was NOT modified or redeployed.

### Constraints honored

- ADR-012: Shared lib carries no Dataverse entity strings — `appnotification` / `customData` / `toasttype` all live in the solution-local SpaarkeAi loader. The shared hook's new `loadNotificationContext` parameter is a generic `() => Promise<NarrateRequest | null>` callback.
- ADR-013: No new BFF service. The narrate endpoint is unchanged. All changes are client-side.
- ADR-014: Per-user/per-tenant TTL cache (5 min) preserved — `loadNotificationContext` runs only on cache miss.
- ADR-016: 429 graceful handling preserved — rate-limit error path unchanged.
- ADR-028: Auth flow unchanged — `authenticatedFetch` continues to handle the narrate POST per ADR-028.
- FR-25: Standalone LegalWorkspace bundle behavior is preserved (no functional change; only +140 bytes of optional-param forwarding code path that's `undefined` at runtime).
- Operator REUSE principle: notificationContextLoader is a faithful copy of the standalone Daily Briefing Code Page's working data path — same Xrm.WebApi query, same `customData` parsing, same `groupByCategory` logic, same `buildNarrationRequest` payload shape.
- No `.claude/` modifications — per sub-agent write boundary.
- No POML modifications — Round 4 fix tracked via TASK-INDEX row 086 + this memo only.
- No `current-task.md` modification — per fix-task constraint.

### Verification (next operator pass)

1. Load SpaarkeAi (`sprk_spaarkeai` web resource) → Workspace Home tab loads → wait for Daily Briefing section to finish loading → expect either:
   - REAL AI BULLETS (if the operator has unread `appnotification` records with `customData.category` set by the playbook system); OR
   - Empty state ("Nothing to see right now — enjoy your day") ONLY when there are truly zero notifications. This is the correct empty-data case (not the prior false-empty bug).
2. Open browser devtools → Network tab → confirm:
   - `retrieveMultipleRecords` call to `/api/data/v9.2/appnotification?...` returned 200 with entities array
   - `POST /api/ai/daily-briefing/narrate` request body contains `categories.length > 0` AND `channels.length > 0` (NOT the empty envelope)
   - `POST /api/ai/daily-briefing/narrate` response contains `tldr` with non-empty `briefing` / `topAction` and `channelNarratives` with entries
3. Open standalone Daily Briefing Code Page (`sprk_dailybriefing`) → confirm it still works identically (FR-25 — Code Page untouched, but verifies the BFF narrate endpoint contract is stable).
4. Open standalone LegalWorkspace (`sprk_corporateworkspace`) Workspace pane → confirm Daily Briefing section still renders identically to pre-086 behavior (FR-25 — LegalWorkspace shim untouched at the runtime level).

### Edge cases handled

- Xrm unavailable (dev Vite mode, direct URL with no MDA host): `getXrm()` returns `null` → loader returns `null` → shared hook falls back to empty payload → empty-state UI renders (no error).
- Zero notifications in Dataverse: `appnotification` query returns empty `entities[]` → loader returns `null` → shared hook falls back to empty payload → BFF returns 200/empty (task 083) → empty-state UI.
- Loader throws (Xrm.WebApi unexpected failure): shared hook's try/catch logs a warning and falls back to empty payload → empty-state UI (no crash).
- 429 rate limit from narrate endpoint: unchanged from task 035 — section renders the degraded "Daily Briefing temporarily unavailable" card with Retry button, telemetry fires via `logTelemetryError(TELEMETRY_DAILY_BRIEFING_429, ...)`.

### Verdict

- Round 4 Fix 3 complete — Daily Briefing in SpaarkeAi WorkspaceHomeTab now uses the SAME Xrm.WebApi `appnotification` query + payload assembly as the standalone Daily Briefing Code Page.
- R-17 risk register entry added + marked RESOLVED.
- TASK-INDEX row 086 added (Phase F — Verification — remediation; FULL rigor; deps 034, 035, 069, 083).
- SpaarkeAi deployed; LegalWorkspace runtime behavior preserved (no redeploy needed).
- Operator smoke is the next gate — verify deployed SpaarkeAi Home tab shows real bullets when notifications exist.

*End of supplemental deploy (Round 4 Fix 3 / task 086).*

## Supplemental Deploy — Round 4 Fix 4 (workspace widget via embed + active-tab signals) — 2026-05-21

### Context

Round 4 Fix 4 (task 087) makes the SpaarkeAi `WorkspacePaneMenu` "Switch Workspace" dropdown selection ACTUALLY OPEN the chosen workspace. Pre-fix behaviour: clicking a workspace persisted a `sessionStorage` key + dispatched a legacy `window` CustomEvent but no UI ever consumed it, so the workspace pane silently did nothing. The investigation found that copying LegalWorkspace's 5 section factories into SpaarkeAi would drag in ~30 files (~10K LOC) with `DataverseService` runtime state, `FeedTodoSyncContext`, and the `@hello-pangea/dnd` peer dep. Per the operator's reuse principle taken to its logical conclusion: don't copy factories — embed the WHOLE working `LegalWorkspaceApp` as a single workspace pane widget.

### Changes (this supplemental deploy only)

**LegalWorkspace surface changes (new exports — NO behaviour change)**:
- `src/solutions/LegalWorkspace/src/LegalWorkspaceApp.tsx` — added `initialWorkspaceId?: string` and `embedded?: boolean` props (default `false`). When `embedded={true}`, the component suppresses its internal `<PageHeader>` (which carries its own workspace dropdown), footer, outer `<FluentProvider>`, and cross-device theme-sync side effects.
- `src/solutions/LegalWorkspace/src/index.ts` — new barrel exporting `LegalWorkspaceApp` + `ILegalWorkspaceAppProps`.

**Key observation**: `LegalWorkspaceApp.tsx` is NOT consumed by the standalone LegalWorkspace bundle. The runtime entry is `main.tsx → App.tsx`. Therefore the standalone bundle is byte-identical and FR-25 / NFR-10 are automatically preserved.

**SpaarkeAi alias + dep**:
- `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/vite.config.ts` — added `@spaarke/legal-workspace` alias to LegalWorkspace's `src/`, added that path to the `resolveSharedLibDeps` plugin's awareness list, and added LegalWorkspace `*.ts` / `*.tsx` to the React plugin's transpilation include set.
- `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/package.json` — added `@hello-pangea/dnd ^18.0.1` (required by LegalWorkspace's `SmartToDo` / `KanbanBoard` transitive imports).

**New widget**:
- `src/client/shared/Spaarke.AI.Widgets/src/widgets/workspace/WorkspaceLayoutWidget.tsx` — a `WorkspaceWidgetComponent<{ layoutId, layoutName }>` that resolves Xrm via the frame-walk pattern and renders `<LegalWorkspaceApp initialWorkspaceId={data.layoutId} embedded />`. Dev fallback renders an empty-state message when Xrm is unavailable.
- `src/client/shared/Spaarke.AI.Widgets/src/widgets/workspace/register-workspace-widgets.ts` — registered widget type `'workspace'` with `allowMultiple: true` and `defaultOrder: 140`.
- `src/client/shared/Spaarke.AI.Widgets/tsconfig.json` — added a `paths` entry for `@spaarke/legal-workspace` so editor / IDE imports resolve (Vite build path uses its own alias config). The package's tsc still surfaces pre-existing TS6059 rootDir errors for the source-resolved `@spaarke/ai-outputs` and `@spaarke/legal-workspace` modules; these errors do NOT gate the SpaarkeAi Vite build, which is the deployment-relevant path.

**Dropdown wiring**:
- `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/components/workspace/WorkspacePaneMenu.tsx` — `handleLayoutSelect` now dispatches a `widget_load` event on the `workspace` channel carrying `{ widgetType: 'workspace', widgetData: { layoutId, layoutName }, displayName: layoutName }` in addition to the legacy `applyActiveLayout` window-event signal. The pane subscriber's existing `widget_load` handler adds the tab via the standard pipeline.

**Signal infrastructure (foundation only — no consumers in this fix)**:
- `src/client/shared/Spaarke.AI.Widgets/src/events/PaneEventTypes.ts` — added `'active_widget_changed'` to the workspace event type union and added an optional `displayName?: string` field for per-instance tab labels (used both for `widget_load` overrides and `active_widget_changed` carriers).
- `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/components/workspace/WorkspaceTabManager.ts` — new `ActiveTabSnapshot` interface, new optional `onActiveTabChange` callback in `WorkspaceTabManagerOptions`, emit sites at `addTab` / `setActiveTab` / `closeTab` / `clearAllTabs` (with delta guards so no-op activations don't fire).
- `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/components/workspace/WorkspacePane.tsx` — wires `onActiveTabChange` through a forwarding ref into `dispatch("workspace", { type: "active_widget_changed", widgetType, widgetData, tabId, displayName })`. Also updated the `widget_load` handler to honour the event's per-instance `displayName` (so the new workspace tab is labelled with the chosen layout name, e.g. "Corporate Workspace", rather than the generic registry label "Workspace").

### Bundle delta

| Bundle | Baseline | After embed | Delta |
|---|---|---|---|
| SpaarkeAi gzip | 801.85 KB | 893.91 KB | **+92.06 KB (+11.5%)** |
| LegalWorkspace gzip | 569.29 KB | 569.29 KB | **0 KB (byte-identical)** |

The 92 KB delta is much smaller than the ~570 KB worst-case estimate because SpaarkeAi already bundles `@fluentui/react-components`, `lexical`, `react-window`, `@spaarke/ui-components`, `@spaarke/auth`, and the WorkspaceShell — so the LegalWorkspace dependency closure tree-shakes heavily against SpaarkeAi's existing surface. The principal NEW code is the 5 section factories + DataverseService + FeedTodoSync context + `@hello-pangea/dnd`.

LegalWorkspace was NOT redeployed — its files only received NEW EXPORTS (`src/index.ts` barrel + two new optional props on `LegalWorkspaceApp.tsx`, which the standalone bundle does not import). Its runtime behaviour is byte-identical (FR-25 / NFR-10).

### Verification (next operator pass)

1. Load SpaarkeAi (`sprk_spaarkeai` web resource).
2. Open the WorkspacePane menu → "Switch Workspace" section lists workspace layouts loaded via the reused `useWorkspaceLayouts` hook.
3. Click any non-active layout (e.g. "Corporate Workspace"). Expected:
   - A new tab opens labelled with the chosen workspace name (NOT the generic "Workspace" label).
   - The tab content renders the full LegalWorkspace experience: PageHeader is SUPPRESSED (the pane already provides one); all section content (Get Started, Latest Updates, SmartToDo, Documents, Quick Summary) renders identically to standalone LegalWorkspace.
   - The previously-active tab remains in the open-tabs list and can be returned to.
4. Click a second workspace from the dropdown → second tab opens, parallel to the first (`allowMultiple: true`).
5. Switch between tabs via the menu's "Open" section → each tab restores its own embedded workspace state (LegalWorkspaceApp's `useWorkspaceLayouts` hook hydrates from cache + refetches).
6. (Signal verification — optional, requires temporary devtools listener): without an exposed bus, the operator verification is purely UI-driven: tab opens, content renders, switching between tabs works.
7. Open standalone LegalWorkspace (`sprk_corporateworkspace`) → confirm it renders identically to pre-fix behaviour (FR-25 — standalone runtime entry is `App.tsx`, not `LegalWorkspaceApp.tsx`, so the new exports + new props have no effect).

### Edge cases handled

- Xrm unavailable (dev Vite mode): `WorkspaceLayoutWidget` renders an empty-state message instead of crashing inside `LegalWorkspaceApp` (which would throw on `webApi.retrieveRecord(...)`).
- User opens MAX_WORKSPACE_TABS workspaces: the existing FIFO eviction in `WorkspaceTabManager.addTab` continues to apply; the Home tab is exempt.
- User closes the active workspace tab: the existing `closeTab` successor logic activates a neighbour; `active_widget_changed` fires once with the new neighbour's snapshot.
- Concurrent `widget_load` events for the same workspace `layoutId`: per `allowMultiple: true`, both produce distinct tabs. (Operator can dedupe in a follow-up if desired; out of scope here.)
- LegalWorkspace's internal `useWorkspaceLayouts` re-fetches its layout list independently — the embedded instance does NOT share state with the SpaarkeAi `WorkspacePaneMenu` hook. This is intentional (each tab owns its own layout state) and matches the standalone behaviour exactly.

### Verdict

- Round 4 Fix 4 complete — workspace dropdown selection now opens the chosen workspace as a tab via embedded `LegalWorkspaceApp` (operator's reuse principle: "use the whole working component, don't copy factories").
- R-18 risk register entry: "Workspace selection no render path; pane coordination signals unwired" → **RESOLVED**.
- `active_widget_changed` event + `onActiveTabChange` manager callback added as foundation infrastructure; NO consumers wired in this task (deferred to a follow-up that scopes Assistant + Context panes to the active workspace context).
- TASK-INDEX row 087 added (Phase F — Verification — remediation; FULL rigor; deps 067, 084, 086).
- SpaarkeAi deployed; LegalWorkspace runtime behaviour byte-identical (no redeploy needed).
- Operator smoke is the next gate — verify deployed SpaarkeAi workspace dropdown opens a tab that renders identically to standalone LegalWorkspace.

*End of supplemental deploy (Round 4 Fix 4 / task 087).*

## Supplemental Deploy — Task 088 (embed wiring fixes 4.1) — 2026-05-21

### Why

Task 087 made the SpaarkeAi `WorkspacePaneMenu` "Switch Workspace" dropdown actually open the chosen workspace as a tab via embedded `LegalWorkspaceApp`. Operator smoke immediately after deploy surfaced three wiring bugs that the embed had exposed:

**Bug 1 — all tabs show the same workspace**: whether the operator picked "Ralph Workspace 4", "Ralph Workspace 5", or "Corporate Workspace" from the dropdown, every tab rendered the user's last-active workspace (e.g. "Corporate Workspace"). The `initialWorkspaceId` prop was being passed correctly through `LegalWorkspaceApp → WorkspaceGrid → useWorkspaceLayouts(initialWorkspaceId)`, but the hook's cache-first hydration path read from `sessionStorage` BEFORE applying `initialWorkspaceId`. Because the `sessionStorage` cache keys (`sprk:workspace:activeLayout` / `sprk:workspace:layoutsList`) are GLOBAL across all embedded tabs, every new tab hydrated from the same cached "last-active" value. The API path also wrote back to the same cache after resolution, so each newly opened tab clobbered the previous one's view.

**Bug 2 — every tab title is "Workspace"**: the embedded `WorkspaceLayoutWidget` widget type is registered with `displayName: "Workspace"` in `WorkspaceWidgetRegistry`. `WorkspacePane.tsx`'s `widget_load` handler uses a precedence ladder (event.displayName → registry metadata.displayName → widgetType) to pick the tab title. `WorkspacePaneMenu.handleLayoutSelect` was passing the friendly layout name inside `widgetData.layoutName` (a payload field) but NOT setting `displayName` at the top level of the dispatched event, so the ladder fell through to the registry metadata's generic label "Workspace".

**Bug 3 — document preview throws "Runtime config not initialized"**: clicking the document preview action inside an embedded LegalWorkspace tab threw `Uncaught Error: [LegalWorkspace] Runtime config not initialized. Call initRuntimeConfig() in main.tsx before using getBffBaseUrl().` LegalWorkspace has its OWN `runtimeConfig.ts` singleton in `src/solutions/LegalWorkspace/src/config/` — separate from SpaarkeAi's `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/config/runtimeConfig.ts` singleton. SpaarkeAi's `main.tsx` bootstrap called SpaarkeAi's own `setRuntimeConfig(config)` but NOT LegalWorkspace's. Any code path inside the embedded tree that called `getBffBaseUrl()` (document preview's `Xrm.Navigation.navigateTo` handler, the BFF fetch surface) hit an uninitialized singleton.

### What changed

Three surgical fixes, each isolated to embedded-mode code paths so standalone LegalWorkspace remains byte-identical (FR-25 / NFR-10):

**Fix 1 (Bug 1)** — `src/solutions/LegalWorkspace/src/hooks/useWorkspaceLayouts.ts`:

- Added new `UseWorkspaceLayoutsOptions` interface with `initialWorkspaceId?: string` + `embedded?: boolean`.
- Hook signature now accepts EITHER the legacy positional `string` argument OR the new options object (backwards-compatible overload via `typeof initialWorkspaceIdOrOptions === "object"` check).
- When `embedded=true`:
  - Cache-hydrate block at the start of `fetchLayouts()` SKIPS `getCachedLayoutsList()` + `getCachedActiveLayout()` (uses `null` constants instead).
  - Cache-write block at the end of the BFF resolution path SKIPS `setCachedActiveLayout` + `setCachedLayoutsList`.
  - `setActiveLayoutById` (both the local-found path and the BFF fetch-by-ID path) SKIPS `setCachedActiveLayout`.
- Effect's dep array now includes `embedded` so an option-mode change re-fires the fetch.

**Fix 1 (cont.)** — `src/solutions/LegalWorkspace/src/components/Shell/WorkspaceGrid.tsx`:

- Added `embedded?: boolean` to `IWorkspaceGridProps` with default `false`.
- Passes `{ initialWorkspaceId, embedded }` (new option object shape) to `useWorkspaceLayouts(...)`.

**Fix 1 (cont.)** — `src/solutions/LegalWorkspace/src/LegalWorkspaceApp.tsx`:

- Now forwards `embedded` to `<WorkspaceGrid embedded={embedded} ... />`.

**Fix 2 (Bug 2)** — `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/components/workspace/WorkspacePaneMenu.tsx`:

- `handleLayoutSelect` now sets `displayName: layoutName` at the TOP LEVEL of the dispatched `widget_load` event (in addition to keeping `widgetData: { layoutId, layoutName }`).
- `WorkspacePane.tsx`'s existing displayName-precedence ladder (already implemented in task 087) picks up the top-level value and `manager.addTab(widgetType, widgetData, displayName)` uses it as the tab title. No change to `WorkspacePane.tsx` required.

**Fix 3 (Bug 3)** — `src/solutions/LegalWorkspace/src/index.ts`:

- Re-exported `setRuntimeConfig as setLegalWorkspaceRuntimeConfig` from `./config/runtimeConfig`. The aliased name disambiguates from SpaarkeAi's own `setRuntimeConfig` so consumers don't get an unintentional shadow.

**Fix 3 (cont.)** — `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/main.tsx`:

- Imported `setLegalWorkspaceRuntimeConfig` from `@spaarke/legal-workspace`.
- Immediately after the existing `setRuntimeConfig(config)` call, also calls `setLegalWorkspaceRuntimeConfig(config)` with the SAME `IRuntimeConfig`. Wrapped in `try/catch` with a warning log so an init failure in the embedded singleton doesn't break SpaarkeAi's own code paths.
- Both singletons remain DISTINCT in-process instances holding equivalent values for `bffBaseUrl` / `bffOAuthScope` / `msalClientId` / `tenantId`. The two `setRuntimeConfig` implementations also each write the SAME `window.__SPAARKE_BFF_BASE_URL__` / `window.__SPAARKE_MSAL_CLIENT_ID__` globals (already idempotent — the second write overwrites with the same value).

### Build + deploy

- **`@spaarke/ui-components`**: not touched (no rebuild needed).
- **`src/solutions/LegalWorkspace`**: `npm run build` — gzip 569.30 KB (vs 569.22 KB task 070 baseline; +80 bytes from the new option-object normalization branch in `useWorkspaceLayouts`). Standalone runtime entry (`main.tsx → App.tsx`) never imports `index.ts` so the new `setLegalWorkspaceRuntimeConfig` export has no path to the standalone bundle. Standalone code paths always pass `embedded=false` (default), so the new conditional branches in `useWorkspaceLayouts` are never executed. NOT redeployed (standalone Code Page unchanged at runtime; just the source tree was edited to expose props for embedding).
- **`src/solutions/SpaarkeAi`**: `npm run build` — gzip 893.75 KB (vs 893.91 KB task 087 baseline; −0.16 KB).
- **Deploy**: `scripts/Deploy-SpaarkeAi.ps1` to `spaarkedev1` — `sprk_spaarkeai` web resource updated (resource ID `5206a442-3451-f111-bec7-7ced8d1dc988`), customizations published.

### Operator-verifiable

After hard refresh of SpaarkeAi:

1. Open `WorkspacePaneMenu`. Click "Ralph Workspace 4" → a new tab opens with title "Ralph Workspace 4" rendering that workspace's sections.
2. Click "Ralph Workspace 5" → a new tab opens with title "Ralph Workspace 5" rendering its OWN sections (distinct from tab 1).
3. Click "Corporate Workspace" → third tab opens with title "Corporate Workspace" rendering Corporate's sections.
4. Switch between the three tabs — each shows its own workspace.
5. Inside any embedded workspace tab, click a document's "preview" action — opens the preview Code Page popup without the `[LegalWorkspace] Runtime config not initialized` runtime error.
6. Standalone LegalWorkspace Code Page (`sprk_corporateworkspace`) — open separately, verify dropdown switching still works exactly as before (the `embedded=false` default preserves cache-first hydration so the user's last-active layout still hydrates instantly on next navigation).

### Edge cases

- Multiple embedded tabs of the SAME workspace `layoutId`: each instance independently honours its `initialWorkspaceId`; no sessionStorage cross-talk; works correctly.
- Embedded layout not found on BFF (deleted out from under the operator): `useWorkspaceLayouts` falls back through its normal cascade (BFF default → first default → first system → first layout → SYSTEM_DEFAULT_LAYOUT); embedded tab renders the fallback, no crash. Standalone identical.
- Standalone LegalWorkspace user opens a non-default layout via the existing dropdown: cache writes still occur, so the next navigation hydrates instantly. The embedded tabs in SpaarkeAi don't read from this same cache (because they call `embedded=true`), so no cross-contamination.
- Dual `setRuntimeConfig` calls colliding: both singletons live in separate module instances (LegalWorkspace's `config/runtimeConfig.ts` is its own module; SpaarkeAi's `config/runtimeConfig.ts` is its own module — Vite preserves them as distinct chunks). The `_config` private variables don't share storage. Window globals (`__SPAARKE_BFF_BASE_URL__` / `__SPAARKE_MSAL_CLIENT_ID__`) are written twice with the same values — idempotent.

### Verdict

- Round 4 Fix 4.1 complete — three embed-wiring bugs from task 087 resolved.
- R-19 risk register entry: "Embed wiring gaps (initialWorkspaceId / displayName / runtime config)" → **RESOLVED**.
- TASK-INDEX row 088 added (Phase F — Verification — remediation; FULL rigor; deps 087).
- SpaarkeAi deployed; LegalWorkspace standalone runtime untouched (no redeploy needed).
- Operator smoke is the next gate — verify three different workspace selections render three distinct tabs with correct titles AND that document preview no longer throws.

*End of supplemental deploy (Round 4 Fix 4.1 / task 088).*

---

## Supplemental Deploy — Task 091 (workspace builder improvements) — 2026-05-21

**Date**: 2026-05-21
**Round**: 5 (Phase F — Verification — remediation)
**Risk Register**: R-21 → RESOLVED
**Deps**: 033, 088
**Rigor**: FULL

### Operator feedback (2026-05-21)

> "I can't save a layout unless every slot is filled."
> "Once I drop a widget into a slot there's no way to remove it."
> "I want a 'Pin to Start' option in the builder so my chosen workspace auto-opens next time."

### Root cause (per fix)

- **Fix 1 — Save without all slots**: `App.tsx` Step 3's `canAdvance` already only required `workspaceName.trim().length > 0` — no all-slots gate existed. But the wizard serializes empty slots as `""` and the shared `buildDynamicWorkspaceConfig` then logged `console.warn("Unknown section ID: , skipping")` for each empty slot at render time. The save itself worked; the warning made operators think the wizard was rejecting their incomplete layout. Two-line guard in the shared renderer silently skips falsy section IDs.

- **Fix 2 — Remove section from slot**: `GridSlot` already supported HTML5 drag-OUT to the unassigned pool (`handleUnassignedDrop` in `ArrangeStep.tsx`), but the affordance was undiscoverable — operators didn't realize they could drag a filled slot onto the area below. Added an explicit `DismissRegular` X button in each filled slot's top-right corner.

- **Fix 3 — Pin to Start**: brand-new feature. Task 092 will own the auto-open behavior on next SpaarkeAi cold load; task 091 adds the UI flag + sessionStorage stub so the operator can set it before 092 ships.

### Files modified

- `src/solutions/WorkspaceLayoutWizard/src/steps/ArrangeStep.tsx`:
  - Added `DismissRegular` + `PinRegular` icon imports.
  - Extended `ArrangeStepProps` with `pinToStart: boolean` + `onPinToStartChange: (pinToStart: boolean) => void`.
  - Added `position: "relative"` to the slot style; added two new style entries `slotRemoveButton` (absolute-positioned 20x20 circular button with focus + hover states using Fluent v9 tokens only) and `slotRemoveButtonVisible` (opacity:1 modifier shown on hover via `isHovered` state).
  - Extended `GridSlot`'s prop type with `onRemove: (slotId: string) => void`. When the slot is filled, renders the X button alongside `DraggableSectionCard`. `handleRemoveClick` calls `e.stopPropagation()` + `e.preventDefault()` so the button click doesn't bubble to the slot's drag/focus handlers. `handleRemoveMouseDown` also `stopPropagation`s — without it the mousedown would initiate an HTML5 drag on the parent slot. `draggable={false}` belt-and-braces.
  - Added `handleSlotRemove` callback in `ArrangeStep`'s body — deletes the slot's entry from `sectionAssignments` and emits via `onAssignmentsChange`. The removed section returns to the unassigned pool automatically via the existing `unassignedSections` derived state.
  - Added the `Pin to Start` Checkbox to Step 3's inline row (after `Set default`). Label is a span composing `<PinRegular fontSize={14} />` + text. `aria-label` + `title` + `data-testid="pin-to-start-checkbox"` for a11y + smoke. Flex row's `flexWrap: "wrap"` lets the new checkbox flow to a second line on narrow viewports without overflow.

- `src/solutions/WorkspaceLayoutWizard/src/App.tsx`:
  - Added `pinToStart` `useState<boolean>` with initial state from `readPinToStartForLayout(mode === "edit" ? layoutId : null)` (so the edit flow pre-checks the box if the layout is currently pinned).
  - Added two helpers: `readPinToStartForLayout(layoutId)` and `writePinToStartForLayout(layoutId, pinned)` — sessionStorage-backed; key `spaarke:workspace:pinned-layout-id` holds the single pinned layout ID (matches the eventual BFF semantics where pinning one workspace clears the previous pin).
  - `handleFinish` now calls `writePinToStartForLayout(String(savedId), pinToStart)` after a successful save; `__dialogResult` carries `pinToStart` back to the caller (`{ confirmed: true, layoutId, pinToStart }`) so future SpaarkeAi-side consumers can react immediately.
  - Wired `pinToStart` + `setPinToStart` into the `ArrangeStep` render props and into both `useCallback`/`useMemo` dependency arrays.
  - Added an inline `TODO(task 092)` comment in `handleFinish` documenting the path forward: replace the sessionStorage stub with BFF persistence once `CreateWorkspaceLayoutRequest` / `UpdateWorkspaceLayoutRequest` carry `IsPinned` and `sprk_workspacelayout.sprk_ispinned` exists.

- `src/client/shared/Spaarke.UI.Components/src/components/WorkspaceShell/buildDynamicWorkspaceConfig.ts`:
  - Two-line guard added inside the per-row section loop: `if (!sectionId) { continue; }` BEFORE the registration lookup. Empty / falsy section IDs (the wizard's serialization for empty slots) are now silently skipped — no more `console.warn("Unknown section ID: , skipping")` noise. Comment cross-references task 091 / Fix 1.

### Persistence stub vs task 092

| Aspect | Task 091 (this task) | Task 092 (planned) |
|---|---|---|
| Storage | `sessionStorage["spaarke:workspace:pinned-layout-id"]` | `sprk_workspacelayout.sprk_ispinned` boolean column |
| Single-pinned constraint | Yes — overwrites previous ID on set | Yes — service clears existing pins on set |
| BFF DTO field | NOT added | `IsPinned` added to `WorkspaceLayoutDto`, `CreateWorkspaceLayoutRequest`, `UpdateWorkspaceLayoutRequest` |
| Auto-open behavior | NOT implemented | SpaarkeAi reads pinned layout ID on cold load, opens as initial workspace tab |
| Survives browser restart | NO (sessionStorage scope) | YES (Dataverse-backed) |
| Survives device switch | NO | YES |

The sessionStorage stub is a load-bearing UX bridge — without it, operators have no way to express the pin intent and task 092 would have to do both the UI + backend in one task.

### Build + deploy

- **`@spaarke/ui-components`**: `npm run build` (tsc) — succeeded, no output (empty stdout = success).
- **`src/solutions/WorkspaceLayoutWizard`**: `npm run build` — `dist/sprk_workspacelayoutwizard.html` 427.58 KB gzip (1,577.40 KB raw).

  `powershell.exe -ExecutionPolicy Bypass -File scripts/Deploy-WizardCodePages.ps1 -DataverseUrl https://spaarkedev1.crm.dynamics.com`
  Output relevant rows:
  - `[12/13] UPDATE sprk_corporateworkspace (1985 KB) — Done: 8b7e8863-020d-f111-8342-7ced8d1dc988`
  - `[13/13] UPDATE sprk_workspacelayoutwizard (1540 KB) — Done: 9a58d6a6-8a2c-f111-88b5-7ced8d1dc988`
  - Customizations published.
- **Deploy 2** (SpaarkeAi — picks up the shared lib rebuild):
  `powershell.exe -ExecutionPolicy Bypass -File scripts/Deploy-SpaarkeAi.ps1 -DataverseUrl https://spaarkedev1.crm.dynamics.com`
  - `sprk_spaarkeai` updated, resource ID `5206a442-3451-f111-bec7-7ced8d1dc988`.
  - Customizations published.

### BFF not modified

DTO + endpoints + service all untouched. No BFF deploy needed. Task 092 will own the BFF + Dataverse schema changes.

### Operator-verifiable

After hard refresh of SpaarkeAi:

1. Open the WorkspacePane dropdown → `+ New Workspace` → wizard launches.
2. Step 1: pick any layout.
3. Step 2: select sections (or leave default).
4. Step 3:
   - The inline row now shows three controls: `Workspace name` input, `Set default` checkbox, **`📌 Pin to Start` checkbox**.
   - Each filled slot now shows a tiny X button in its top-right corner on hover.
   - Click the X on any slot → the section returns to the `Unassigned sections` row below; the slot reads `Drop section here`.
   - Try to save with empty slots → save succeeds; the rendered workspace shows empty space for those slots (no console warning).
5. With `Pin to Start` checked, save → `sessionStorage["spaarke:workspace:pinned-layout-id"]` is set to the new layout's GUID.
6. Reopen the wizard in edit mode for that layout → the `Pin to Start` checkbox is pre-checked.

Standalone LegalWorkspace (`/main.aspx?pagetype=webresource&webresourceName=sprk_corporateworkspace`) still opens its own layout wizard (`handleOpenWizard` in `WorkspaceGrid.tsx`) without `templateFilter` or `pinToStart` — wizard still shows all 9 templates; `Pin to Start` defaults unchecked; no behavioral regression.

### Edge cases

- `sessionStorage` unavailable (private mode + storage disabled) → both helpers swallow the throw; `readPinToStartForLayout` returns `false`, `writePinToStartForLayout` is a no-op. Wizard still saves the layout normally; only the pin flag is lost.
- Wizard opened in `create` mode (no `layoutId` yet) → `readPinToStartForLayout(null)` returns `false` immediately; the checkbox starts unchecked as expected.
- Wizard opened in `saveAs` mode → the source layout's pin status is NOT inherited (`saveAsData` doesn't carry it, and the new layout's ID doesn't exist yet) → checkbox starts unchecked; operator must explicitly opt in. This matches expectations for "Save Layout As..." since a copy is a distinct workspace.
- Removing the section that was set as `Set default` is unrelated to the pin (default vs pin are independent flags).
- The X button uses `:focus` opacity:1 + outline (`tokens.colorStrokeFocus2`) so keyboard users can tab to it and trigger removal via Enter / Space.

- ADR-021 (Fluent v9 tokens): all new colors / borders use tokens — no hex / rgba. Verified.
- ADR-028 (Spaarke Auth v2): `pinToStart` never traverses the BFF in this task; no auth surface affected. Task 092 will be the auth-relevant change.
- ADR-012 (shared lib boundary): the `buildDynamicWorkspaceConfig` guard belongs in the shared lib because the function already lives there. No new factory hoist needed.
- ADR-013 (BFF additions governance): no BFF code added/changed.

- Task 091 complete — three operator UX asks landed; FR-25 preserved.

## Supplemental Deploy — Task 092 (tab pinning + auto-open) — 2026-05-21

### What changed

Task 092 extends task 091's stubbed pin persistence into a full operator-visible feature: workspaces can be pinned from inside the workspace tab bar (not just from the wizard's checkbox), multiple workspaces can be pinned simultaneously, pinned workspaces persist across browser sessions, and SpaarkeAi auto-opens them as tabs on cold load. Implements operator request from round 5 ("Multiple workspaces can be PINNED — they auto-open as tabs on SpaarkeAi load").

### Storage decision

- **Used**: `localStorage` key `spaarke:workspace:pinned-list` — JSON array of `{ layoutId, layoutName }` records.
- **Why not BFF**: investigated `Sprk.Bff.Api` — the only `UserPreferences` references are in `Models/Ai/AiIntentClassificationSchema.cs:842` and `Services/Ai/PlaybookRunContext.cs:126`. Both are AI-pipeline payloads (input to intent classification and playbook execution), NOT a generic user-preferences surface. No `/api/me/preferences` or similar endpoint exists. Building one is out of scope for this UX fix.
- **Why localStorage (not sessionStorage)**: sessionStorage clears on tab/window close; operator's requirement is that pinned workspaces survive a full browser restart. localStorage persists on the device.
- **Limitation acknowledged**: device-local, not cross-device. Documented as a TODO for the next review (BFF user-preferences endpoint).

### Files modified

| File | Purpose |
|---|---|
| `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/services/pinnedWorkspaces.ts` (new) | `getPinnedWorkspaces` / `isPinned` / `pinWorkspace` / `unpinWorkspace` utility over `localStorage` with try/catch on every accessor |
| `src/solutions/WorkspaceLayoutWizard/src/App.tsx` | Migrated single-pin `sessionStorage` stub → multi-pin `localStorage` (same shape as SpaarkeAi's util; replicated inline because wizard is a separate Vite app); save handler now passes `layoutName` in addition to `layoutId` |
| `src/solutions/WorkspaceLayoutWizard/src/steps/ArrangeStep.tsx` | Updated two JSDoc references from task 091 / sessionStorage to task 092 / localStorage |
| `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/components/workspace/WorkspacePane.tsx` | New auto-open mount effect — reads pin list after `isAuthenticated`, dispatches `widget_load` per pin, skips duplicates already in the tab list, one-shot via `useRef` guard |
| `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/components/workspace/WorkspaceTabManagerComponent.tsx` | Pin/unpin icon button (`PinRegular` / `PinFilled`) rendered next to close button on workspace tabs only — Home tab + non-workspace widget tabs filtered out; local `pinnedIds: Set<string>` state for synchronous icon flip on click; `aria-pressed` for screen readers |

### Wizard pin storage migrated to multi-pin

Yes — task 091's `sessionStorage["spaarke:workspace:pinned-layout-id"]` (single string value) has been replaced with `localStorage["spaarke:workspace:pinned-list"]` (JSON array). Both the wizard and SpaarkeAi read and write the same shape. The wizard cannot import from SpaarkeAi (separate Vite apps); the localStorage shape is replicated verbatim inline with cross-file JSDoc warnings.

### Non-workspace tabs

Non-workspace tabs (e.g. Create Matter, Find Similar, Email Compose widget tabs) do NOT show the pin icon. The filter is `tab.kind === "widget" && tab.widgetType === "workspace" && !!widgetData.layoutId`. Home tab (`kind === "home"`) is also filtered out — it's auto-installed every cold load, no value in pinning it.

### Build

- **SpaarkeAi**: `npm run build` — 894.21 KB gzip (vs 893.44 task 091 baseline = +0.77 KB / +0.09%).
- **WorkspaceLayoutWizard**: `npm run build` — 427.76 KB gzip (vs 427.58 task 091 baseline = +0.18 KB / +0.04%).
- **LegalWorkspace**: NOT rebuilt — no LegalWorkspace code touched; bundle byte-identical to task 091 (569.31 KB gzip). FR-25 / NFR-10 preserved.

### Deploy output

```
