```
[2/4] Getting access token... Token acquired
[3/4] Checking for existing sprk_spaarkeai... Found 5206a442-3451-f111-bec7-7ced8d1dc988
       Updated
[4/4] Publishing customizations... Published

[WizardCodePages]
[1/13] UPDATE sprk_creatematterwizard (1505 KB) Done
[5/13] UPDATE sprk_createworkassignmentwizard (1450 KB) Done
[6/13] UPDATE sprk_summarizefileswizard (1503 KB) Done
[7/13] UPDATE sprk_findsimilar (1344 KB) Done
[8/13] UPDATE sprk_playbooklibrary (1473 KB) Done
[9/13] UPDATE sprk_wizard_commands (12 KB) Done
[12/13] UPDATE sprk_corporateworkspace (1985 KB) Done
[13/13] UPDATE sprk_workspacelayoutwizard (1541 KB) Done
[PUBLISH] Published 8 web resources
```

Two missing wizard pages (`sprk_createprojectwizard`, `sprk_createeventwizard`, `sprk_createtodowizard`, `sprk_documentuploadwizard`, `sprk_alldocuments`) are SKIPPED by the deploy script because their `dist/` artifacts don't exist in this worktree — not regressed by task 092 (these were already missing before this task).

### Operator-verifiable

1. Open SpaarkeAi → Workspace pane shows Home tab (default).
2. Open the Workspace dropdown → `Select Workspace` → click any layout. A new tab opens with that workspace's name.
3. The new tab shows a small pin icon next to the close X. Click the pin icon → the icon flips to filled (brand color); tooltip changes to "Unpin {name} from start".
4. Open a SECOND workspace from the dropdown; pin it too. Both pin icons show filled state.
5. Open browser DevTools → Application → Local Storage → confirm `spaarke:workspace:pinned-list` contains both records as a JSON array.
6. Close the entire browser (not just the tab — fully exit so sessionStorage would have cleared).
7. Reopen the browser → navigate to SpaarkeAi → on first paint, Home tab appears + the TWO pinned workspaces auto-open as additional tabs (cycle order matches the localStorage array; each has its layout name as the tab label).
8. Click an unpinned-state pin icon → entry added to localStorage.
9. Click a pinned-state pin icon → entry removed from localStorage; tooltip flips back to "Pin {name} to start".
10. The "+ Pin to Start" checkbox in the wizard still works (task 091 affordance) — saving a workspace with the checkbox checked writes it to the SAME localStorage list. Verify by saving via the wizard, opening DevTools localStorage, and confirming the new entry appears in `spaarke:workspace:pinned-list`.
11. Standalone LegalWorkspace (`?webresourceName=sprk_corporateworkspace`) opens normally; its tabs do NOT show the pin icon because its tab bar is the LegalWorkspace internal one, not SpaarkeAi's `WorkspaceTabManagerComponent`. FR-25 preserved.

### Edge cases handled

- **localStorage unavailable** (private browsing + storage disabled, or quota exceeded): every accessor in `pinnedWorkspaces.ts` and the inline wizard helpers is try/catch-wrapped. On failure: `getPinnedWorkspaces` returns `[]`; `pinWorkspace` / `unpinWorkspace` are no-ops. Auto-open silently does nothing. The pin icon still renders but clicks have no on-disk effect (the in-memory `pinnedIds` Set still flips so the user sees the icon change for that session, even if the change is lost on next reload).
- **Corrupt JSON in localStorage**: `getPinnedWorkspaces` returns `[]` and `flatMap` normalizes any entries missing `layoutId` / `layoutName` (drops them silently). No crash.
- **Duplicate auto-open**: if NFR-09 tab restore (`PATCH /api/ai/chat/sessions/{id}/tabs`) restored a workspace tab from a previous session and that workspace is also in the pinned list, the auto-open effect skips it (looks up open workspace tabs by `widgetData.layoutId` and filters before dispatching).
- **`isAuthenticated` toggles on token refresh**: `autoOpenedPinsRef` is set after the first successful pass so subsequent flips don't re-stack tabs.
- **Pinned workspace deleted from Dataverse**: SpaarkeAi still dispatches `widget_load` with the orphaned id; the embedded `LegalWorkspaceApp` inside the resulting tab will surface its own "Workspace not found" empty state when the BFF returns 404. User can click the pin icon to remove it from the list, or click X to close the tab.

### ADR compliance

- **ADR-021** (Fluent v9 tokens): all colors use tokens — `colorBrandForeground1`, `colorNeutralForeground3`, `colorNeutralBackground3Hover`. No hex, no rgba. Verified.
- **ADR-022** (React 19 functional): all new components / effects are functional.
- **ADR-025** (Fluent v9 icons): `PinRegular` / `PinFilled` from `@fluentui/react-icons`. No new SVG web resources.
- **ADR-028** (Spaarke Auth v2): localStorage is client-side state only; no auth surface affected.
- **ADR-013** (BFF additions governance): no BFF code added or changed. The TODO documents the BFF migration as a follow-on once a user-preferences endpoint exists.

### Verdict

- Task 092 complete — pinning + auto-open + per-tab toggle landed end-to-end.
- R-22 risk register entry → **RESOLVED**.
- TASK-INDEX row 092 added (Phase F remediation, FULL rigor, deps 088 + 091, est 3h).
- `sprk_spaarkeai` + `sprk_workspacelayoutwizard` + 6 other wizard pages deployed to `spaarkedev1`; LegalWorkspace standalone behaviorally untouched.

*End of supplemental deploy (Task 092 / tab pinning + auto-open).*

## Supplemental Deploy — Task 094 (pane collapse/expand) — 2026-05-22

### What changed

Task 094 adds operator-facing click-to-collapse behaviour to all three SpaarkeAi panes (Assistant / Workspace / Context). The existing `ThreePaneLayout` already supported left/right collapse via sessionStorage `*-visibility` keys, but the toggle UI was buried (only the collapsed strip itself was clickable — there was no way to REACH the collapsed state without code). Operator request from Round 5: mirror SmartToDo's Kanban column collapse — click the pane's header to collapse it to a narrow vertical strip with the pane's name rotated 90°; click the strip to re-expand; all three panes can be collapsed simultaneously; state persists across browser sessions.

### Approach (reuse, don't reinvent)

The visual pattern is lifted verbatim from `src/solutions/LegalWorkspace/src/components/SmartToDo/`:

- **State shape**: `SmartToDo.tsx:337-352` — `collapsedColumns: ReadonlySet<string>` + `handleToggleCollapse` callback. Set-based API generalises to N panes (future-proofs against a possible 4th pane).
- **Collapsed strip CSS**: `KanbanBoard.tsx:132-156` — `columnCollapsed` / `columnCollapsedHeader` / `columnCollapsedTitle` styles with `writingMode: 'vertical-rl'` + `transform: 'rotate(180deg)'`. The ThreePaneLayout's existing `collapsedLabel` style already uses the same incantation (lines 118-127); the new center-pane collapsed strip reuses it identically.
- **Header click pattern**: `KanbanBoard.tsx:211-225` — header gets `cursor:pointer` + `onClick={onToggleCollapse}`. Interactive children inside the header (the count badge — though it's non-interactive) live untouched. For our panes the interactive children (HistoryRegular button, WorkspacePaneMenu dropdown trigger) are real buttons — we add `stopPropagation` on the PaneHeader's rightSlot wrapper to keep their clicks from bubbling.

### Files modified

| File | Purpose |
|---|---|
| `src/client/shared/Spaarke.UI.Components/src/components/PaneHeader/PaneHeader.tsx` | Added `onCollapse?: () => void` + `expanded?: boolean` props. When `onCollapse` is wired, the header becomes a `role="button"` with `tabIndex=0`, `aria-expanded`, `aria-label`, Enter/Space keyboard handlers, and a `cursor:pointer` + hover-background style. The rightSlot wrapper applies `stopPropagation` on both `onClick` and `onKeyDown` so interactive children (Buttons, Dropdowns, Menus) don't bubble events up to the header collapse handler. When `onCollapse` is undefined ALL new code paths short-circuit — backwards compatible with existing PaneHeader consumers (LegalWorkspace standalone behaves identically). |
| `src/client/shared/Spaarke.UI.Components/src/components/ThreePaneLayout/ThreePaneLayout.tsx` + `.types.ts` | Added 6 optional props for externally-controlled collapse: `leftCollapsed` / `centerCollapsed` / `rightCollapsed` + `onToggleLeft` / `onToggleCenter` / `onToggleRight` + `centerPaneCollapseLabel`. When wired, these override the internal sessionStorage-backed visibility state. The center pane is now collapsible — base layout previously only supported left/right collapse. Collapsed center pane renders as a 36px strip with rotated label + chevron, identical to the existing left/right strips; click / Enter / Space re-expands. Splitters hide when either adjacent pane is collapsed (no point dragging a non-resizable strip). |
| `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/hooks/usePaneCollapse.ts` (new, ~140 lines) | Typed Set-based hook with `PaneId = 'assistant' \| 'workspace' \| 'context'` discriminated union; reads / writes `localStorage["spaarke:panes:collapsed"]` (JSON array of PaneId values) with try/catch-wrapped accessors per task 092's posture. Validates persisted IDs against an internal `VALID_PANE_IDS` Set so corrupted entries can't crash render. Returns `{ isCollapsed, toggle, collapsedIds }`. |
| `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/components/shell/ThreePaneShell.tsx` | Wires `usePaneCollapse` at the shell level + exposes the toggle handle via a new `PaneCollapseContext` so each pane can read its own collapsed state + toggle without prop-drilling. Passes all 6 collapse props to `ThreePaneLayout`. Collapse labels updated to bare pane names ("Assistant", "Workspace", "Context") — the verbose `"Show AI Chat"` / `"Show Context"` strings (R2 holdovers) no longer fit the rotated-strip UX. |
| `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/components/conversation/ConversationPane.tsx` | Wires `onCollapse={handleHeaderCollapse}` + `expanded={isAssistantExpanded}` on the PaneHeader. History icon button's onClick adds `e.stopPropagation()` as a defensive belt — the PaneHeader's rightSlot container also stops propagation (belt-and-braces). |
| `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/components/workspace/WorkspacePane.tsx` | Wires Workspace pane PaneHeader collapse. WorkspacePaneMenu in rightSlot is already protected by PaneHeader's rightSlot stopPropagation guard. |
| `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/components/context/ContextPaneController.tsx` | Wires Context pane PaneHeader collapse. The stage label in rightSlot is non-interactive Text but the rightSlot guard still applies. |

### How click-to-collapse differentiates from icon clicks

The PaneHeader's rightSlot wrapper applies `e.stopPropagation()` on both `onClick` and `onKeyDown` handlers (only when `onCollapse` is wired — when not wired, no overhead). This is the single guard — any descendant Button / Dropdown / Menu in the rightSlot has its click swallowed at the wrapper boundary before it can bubble up to the header. Belt-and-braces: ConversationPane's History icon Button also calls `e.stopPropagation()` explicitly in its own `onClick`. WorkspacePane's WorkspacePaneMenu (Fluent v9 Menu component) doesn't need explicit stopPropagation because the wrapper guard already handles it. Pattern mirrors SmartToDo's KanbanBoard where the count badge sits inside the clickable header without a separate guard — but our panes have *real* interactive buttons, so the wrapper guard is required.

### Build

- **Shared UI library**: `npm run build` — TypeScript clean.
- **SpaarkeAi**: `npm run build` — 895.04 KB gzip (vs 894.21 task 092 baseline = +0.83 KB / +0.09%).
- **LegalWorkspace** (verified for FR-25): `npm run build` — 569.35 KB gzip (vs 569.31 task 092 baseline = +40 bytes). Delta is unused conditional-branch code in the new PaneHeader (`onCollapse` undefined at runtime for LegalWorkspace standalone, so all new code paths short-circuit). Behaviorally unchanged — FR-25 / NFR-10 preserved.

### Bundle delta breakdown

| Solution | Before (task 092) | After (task 094) | Delta |
|---|---|---|---|
| SpaarkeAi | 894.21 KB gzip | 895.04 KB gzip | +0.83 KB |
| LegalWorkspace | 569.31 KB gzip | 569.35 KB gzip | +0.04 KB |
| Shared UI lib (compiled) | — | — | (no separate bundle; reflected in solution sizes) |

LegalWorkspace was rebuilt for FR-25 verification but NOT redeployed — bundle delta is +40 bytes of unused branch code; standalone behavior is byte-identical at runtime. No reason to redeploy `sprk_corporateworkspace` for this task.

### Operator-verifiable

1. Open SpaarkeAi → three panes render normally (Assistant left / Workspace center / Context right).
2. Click anywhere on the **Assistant** pane header (the `ChatRegular` icon area, the "Assistant" text, or any blank header space) — the pane collapses to a narrow ~36px vertical strip with "Assistant" rotated 90° and a right-chevron icon. The center + right panes expand to reclaim the freed space.
3. Click the collapsed strip → the Assistant pane re-expands to its prior width.
4. Click the **History icon button** in the Assistant pane header — the History overlay opens, the pane does NOT collapse (stopPropagation guard).
5. Click the **Workspace** pane header — the pane collapses; the Context pane expands to fill the freed center space (left pane stays at its width).
6. Click the **WorkspacePaneMenu** (the three-dot-style dropdown trigger in the Workspace header's rightSlot) — the menu opens, the pane does NOT collapse.
7. Click the **Context** pane header — the pane collapses; Workspace + Assistant share the freed space.
8. Collapse ALL THREE panes — all three render as narrow strips side-by-side (operator decision: no minimum-expanded rule).
9. Open browser DevTools → Application → Local Storage → confirm `spaarke:panes:collapsed` contains the expected JSON array (e.g. `["assistant","workspace","context"]` when all three are collapsed).
10. Refresh the browser → all collapsed states restore correctly.
11. Close the browser fully → reopen → navigate to SpaarkeAi → collapse states still restored (localStorage persistence, not sessionStorage).
12. Keyboard accessibility: Tab to a pane header (focus ring appears) → press Enter or Space → pane collapses; Tab to the collapsed strip → Enter or Space re-expands.
13. Standalone LegalWorkspace (`?webresourceName=sprk_corporateworkspace`) opens normally — no collapse affordance (LegalWorkspace doesn't use PaneHeader in the relevant tab bars, and the `onCollapse` prop is undefined in standalone code paths). FR-25 preserved.

### Edge cases handled

- **localStorage unavailable** (private browsing + storage disabled, or quota exceeded): every accessor in `usePaneCollapse.ts` is try/catch-wrapped. Cold load returns an empty Set (no panes collapsed); `toggle` updates in-memory React state but silently fails to persist. No crash. The user can still collapse / re-expand during the session — state just won't survive a refresh.
- **Corrupt JSON in localStorage**: `readPersistedCollapseSet` returns an empty Set and the bad entry is silently discarded on next write.
- **Unknown PaneId in persisted list** (e.g. an entry from a future version): `VALID_PANE_IDS` set drops it; valid entries from the same array are kept.
- **Pane rendered in isolation by tests** (without `<ThreePaneShell>` wrapper): `usePaneCollapseContext()` returns `null`; each pane checks for null before wiring `onCollapse`, so the PaneHeader receives `onCollapse={undefined}` and behaves like the pre-task-094 non-clickable header. Backwards compatible.
- **All three panes collapsed simultaneously**: no minimum-expanded rule per operator decision — all three strips render side-by-side. The user can re-expand any of them by clicking the strip.

### ADR compliance

- **ADR-021** (Fluent v9 tokens): all new styles use semantic tokens — `colorNeutralBackground2`, `colorNeutralBackground2Hover`, `colorNeutralBackground1Hover`, `colorStrokeFocus2`, `colorNeutralForeground3`, `colorNeutralStroke2`. No hex, no rgba. Dark mode safe by construction.
- **ADR-022** (React 19 functional): all new components / hooks / effects are functional.
- **ADR-025** (Fluent v9 icons): collapsed-strip chevron icons (`ChevronLeft16Regular` / `ChevronRight16Regular`) come from `@fluentui/react-icons` — pre-existing imports in ThreePaneLayout.tsx. No new SVG web resources.
- **ADR-028** (Spaarke Auth v2): no auth surface affected — localStorage is client-side state only.
- **ADR-012** (Shared component library): PaneHeader + ThreePaneLayout changes live in `@spaarke/ui-components` (where they already are). The SpaarkeAi-specific hook (`usePaneCollapse`) lives in the solution, not the shared lib, because the PaneId union is SpaarkeAi-specific (a different consumer might have different pane names). The shared library exposes the generic collapse mechanism (props); the solution owns the concrete state.

### Verdict

- Task 094 complete — per-pane collapse / expand landed end-to-end with localStorage persistence.
- R-23 risk register entry → **RESOLVED**.
- TASK-INDEX row 094 added (Phase F remediation, FULL rigor, deps 010, est 4h).
- `sprk_spaarkeai` deployed to `spaarkedev1`; LegalWorkspace standalone behaviorally untouched (FR-25 preserved).

*End of supplemental deploy (Task 094 / pane collapse/expand).*

## Supplemental Deploy — Task 095 (Context tool selector + Semantic Search Criteria)

**Deployed**: 2026-05-22
**Branch**: `work/spaarke-ai-platform-unification-r3`
**Rigor**: FULL — code implementation in SpaarkeAi (no shared library changes; SemanticSearch Code Page untouched)
**ADRs**: ADR-012 (SpaarkeAi-local components), ADR-021 (Fluent v9 tokens), ADR-022 (React 19), ADR-025 (`@fluentui/react-icons` v9), ADR-028 (no auth surface change — Semantic Search criteria stays client-side until modal hand-off)

### Operator request (Round 5 — UX iteration)

> "For the Context pane: add a content selector similar to the Workspace pane (same dropdown UX, no tabs). One 'tool' is the existing Quick Start cards (default). Another tool is Semantic Search Criteria — re-use the SearchFilterPane from the SemanticSearch code page. When the user clicks the 'Search' button in the Criteria tool, a modal of the full Semantic Search pops up with the search terms pre-filled and showing the results. When the modal closes, the Context pane should RETURN to the Search Criteria tool (not go blank). This same fix applies to the existing playbook-select modal: currently after a wizard/modal closes, the Context pane goes blank — it should preserve whatever tool the user had selected."

### Resolution summary

1. **Tool selector dropdown** in the Context pane PaneHeader rightSlot — Fluent v9 `<Menu>` mirroring the WorkspacePaneMenu pattern verbatim (subtle Button trigger with `ChevronDownRegular`, MenuPopover, MenuList, MenuGroupHeader "Context Tools", two MenuItems with `AppsListRegular` / `SearchRegular` icons + `CheckmarkRegular` activeMarker on the selected item).
2. **Two tools surfaced**:
   - `quick-start` (default) → existing GetStartedCardsWidget (FR-18 / FR-19 / FR-21 — 7 action cards).
   - `semantic-search` → new SemanticSearchCriteriaTool: in-pane Domain selector (`<Dropdown>` not tabs — fits a ~360px pane), AI query Textarea, optional date range (from / to date inputs), primary Search button.
3. **Modal launch** via `Xrm.Navigation.navigateTo` with `pageType:"webresource"`, `webresourceName:"sprk_semanticsearch"`, `data` carrying `query` + `domain` + `dateFrom` + `dateTo` URL params (the SemanticSearch Code Page's `parseUrlParams` already reads `query` + `domain`; `dateFrom` / `dateTo` are forward-compatible parameters the page will receive). Target is 80% × 80% modal (vs wizards' 60% × 70% — the full SemanticSearch page has its own SearchFilterPane + map/grid views that need more room). Frame-walking Xrm resolver follows the `wizardLaunchers.ts` precedent (`window → parent → top`).
4. **Persisted tool selection** in localStorage under `spaarke:context:selected-tool` (JSON string of `ContextToolId`) — this is the SOURCE OF TRUTH for what the pane renders. Modal close (wizard or Semantic Search) re-renders the pane with the chosen tool still selected. This is the uniform fix for the operator's reported "pane goes blank after modal close" bug — applies to both new Semantic Search modal AND the existing playbook-modal wizard flow.
5. **Persisted criteria state** in localStorage under `spaarke:context:semantic-search-criteria` (JSON object of `{ query, domain, dateFrom, dateTo }`) — so a Search round-trip preserves what the user typed; tool switches (Quick Start → Semantic Search → Quick Start → Semantic Search) restore the last-typed criteria.

### Files changed

| File | Purpose |
|---|---|
| `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/hooks/useContextTool.ts` (new) | Typed Set-based persistence hook — mirrors `usePaneCollapse.ts` posture (try/catch-wrapped accessors, `VALID_CONTEXT_TOOL_IDS` validation, silent failure on private-browsing/quota). |
| `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/components/context/ContextPaneMenu.tsx` (new) | Fluent v9 `<Menu>` dropdown component — `<MenuTrigger>` Button + `<MenuPopover>` + `<MenuList>` + `<MenuGroupHeader>` "Context Tools" + two MenuItems (Quick Start / Semantic Search) with active-checkmark marker. Mirrors `WorkspacePaneMenu` styling shapes (`trigger`, `activeMarker`, `tabLabel`). |
| `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/components/context/SemanticSearchCriteriaTool.tsx` (new) | In-pane Search Criteria editor: Domain `<Dropdown>` (replaces tabs to fit a narrow pane), AI query `<Textarea>`, optional from/to date `<Input type="date">` pair, primary "Search" `<Button>`. localStorage-persisted state. Modal launch via Xrm.Navigation.navigateTo with frame-walk pattern from `wizardLaunchers.ts`. |
| `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/components/context/ContextPaneController.tsx` | Wires `useContextTool()` hook + composes `<ContextPaneMenu>` in PaneHeader rightSlot (alongside the existing stage label `<Text>`, in a `<div>` flex row with `gap: spacingHorizontalS`). `renderContent()` updated so `selectedTool` is the source of truth: `semantic-search` → renders `<SemanticSearchCriteriaTool/>` regardless of stage; `quick-start` → renders `<GetStartedCardsWidget/>` when there's no server-driven `activeWidget` (server context_update flow preserved when `activeWidget !== null`). |

### Tool selection priority (renderContent decision tree)

```
if (selectedTool === "semantic-search")            → SemanticSearchCriteriaTool
else if (currentStage === "welcome")               → GetStartedCardsWidget       (FR-18 entry point)
else if (selectedTool === "quick-start"
         && activeWidget === null
         && !isResolving)                          → GetStartedCardsWidget       (fix for modal-close blank pane)
else if (currentStage === "loading")               → entity-info empty state OR active widget
else if (isResolving)                              → spinner
else if (activeWidget !== null)                    → server-resolved widget      (preserved Stage 3/4 flow)
else                                               → stage-default empty state
```

The new branch (`selectedTool === "quick-start" && activeWidget === null && !isResolving`) is the fix for the blank-pane bug: a wizard launch doesn't change `selectedTool`, so when the modal closes the pane re-renders this branch and GetStartedCardsWidget appears. The server-driven `activeWidget` flow (Findings, Progress, Related Items widgets) is preserved when it's set.

### Build

- **Shared UI library**: `npm run build` — TypeScript clean (no shared-lib edits in this task).
- **SpaarkeAi**: `npm run build` — **896.59 KB gzip** (vs 895.04 KB task 094 baseline = **+1.55 KB / +0.17%**). Within expected +1-3 KB range for the new tool selector + criteria component (no full SearchFilterPane import).
- **LegalWorkspace** (verified for FR-25): `npm run build` — **569.35 KB gzip** — byte-identical to task 094 baseline. No code path in LegalWorkspace touched; FR-25 / NFR-10 preserved.

### Bundle delta breakdown

| Solution | Before (task 094) | After (task 095) | Delta |
|---|---|---|---|
| SpaarkeAi | 895.04 KB gzip | 896.59 KB gzip | +1.55 KB |
| LegalWorkspace | 569.35 KB gzip | 569.35 KB gzip | 0 bytes |

### Operator-verifiable

1. Open SpaarkeAi → Context pane (right) shows PaneHeader with title "Context", `DocumentRegular` icon, and a **new "Tools" dropdown button** in the rightSlot alongside the stage label.
2. Click the **"Tools" button** → dropdown opens with "Context Tools" group header and two items: "Quick Start" (with `AppsListRegular` icon if not selected, `CheckmarkRegular` if selected) and "Semantic Search" (with `SearchRegular` icon if not selected, `CheckmarkRegular` if selected). Default selection on first open: Quick Start.
3. With **Quick Start** selected → pane shows the 7-card GetStartedCardsWidget (existing FR-18 behavior).
4. Click any wizard card (e.g. "Create Project") → wizard modal opens. Close it. → Pane **STILL** shows GetStartedCardsWidget (was: blank pane in pre-task-095 behavior).
5. Open the Tools dropdown → click **Semantic Search** → pane changes to "Search Criteria" editor with Domain dropdown (defaults to Documents), AI query textarea, from/to date inputs, and primary Search button.
6. Type a query (e.g. `contracts about indemnification`), change domain to Matters, set a date range → click **Search** → Semantic Search modal opens at 80% × 80% with the query + domain + date range pre-filled. Verify in the modal's URL data envelope.
7. Close the Semantic Search modal → Context pane **STILL** shows the Search Criteria editor with the same typed query + domain + dates (not blank, not reverted to Quick Start).
8. Click the Tools dropdown → switch back to **Quick Start** → pane shows GetStartedCardsWidget again. Switch back to **Semantic Search** → criteria are still what was last typed.
9. Open browser DevTools → Application → Local Storage → confirm:
   - `spaarke:context:selected-tool` contains `"semantic-search"` (or `"quick-start"` if last set there).
   - `spaarke:context:semantic-search-criteria` contains the typed JSON object.
10. Refresh the browser → selected tool restores correctly; criteria restore correctly.
11. **Pane collapse interaction (task 094 backwards-compat)**: click the pane header anywhere EXCEPT the Tools dropdown or the stage label → pane collapses to a narrow strip (task 094 behavior preserved). Click the Tools dropdown → menu opens, pane does NOT collapse (PaneHeader's rightSlot `stopPropagation` guard from task 094 handles this).
12. **Standalone LegalWorkspace** (`?webresourceName=sprk_corporateworkspace`) opens normally — no Context pane (LegalWorkspace doesn't use the SpaarkeAi shell). FR-25 preserved.

### Edge cases handled

- **localStorage unavailable** (private browsing + storage disabled, or quota exceeded): both `useContextTool` and `SemanticSearchCriteriaTool` accessors are try/catch-wrapped. Cold load returns the default tool / empty criteria. Tool changes update in-memory React state but silently fail to persist. No crash.
- **Corrupt JSON in localStorage**: `readPersistedTool` returns `'quick-start'`; `readPersistedCriteria` returns the default criteria. The bad entry is silently overwritten on next write.
- **Unknown tool id in persisted value** (e.g. an entry from a future version): `VALID_CONTEXT_TOOL_IDS` set drops it; falls back to default.
- **Xrm unavailable** (Vite dev, jsdom): `resolveXrmNavigation()` returns null; the Search button click logs a console.warn and does nothing. No crash. The criteria editor is fully usable for typing / persistence even outside the Dataverse host.
- **`sprk_semanticsearch` not yet deployed** (theoretical): `Xrm.Navigation.navigateTo` rejects with a Dataverse error; the rejection is swallowed by the launch helper (matches `wizardLaunchers.ts` precedent). The operator sees no result modal but the pane state is unchanged. Verified `sprk_semanticsearch` IS present in `spaarkedev1` (`x-ai-semantic-search-ui-r3` shipped it — see `build-webresource.ps1` in the SemanticSearch code-pages directory).
- **Server-driven `activeWidget` arrives while Quick Start selected**: the new render condition `(selectedTool === "quick-start" && activeWidget === null && !isResolving)` allows the server-driven widget to take over when `activeWidget !== null` — the existing Stage 3 (Findings) / Stage 4 (Related Items) flows are preserved. Only the empty-state fallback is replaced with GetStartedCardsWidget.

### ADR compliance

- **ADR-012** (Shared component library): all three new files live in SpaarkeAi (`src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/`), not the shared library — correct placement because the `ContextToolId` union, the localStorage key namespace, and the SemanticSearch modal launch are all SpaarkeAi-specific concerns. The shared `wizardLaunchers.ts` pattern is referenced (frame-walk Xrm resolver) but not modified; a hypothetical `launchSemanticSearchModal` shared helper would be premature since this is the only consumer.
- **ADR-021** (Fluent v9 tokens): all new styles use semantic tokens — `colorBrandForeground1`, `colorNeutralForeground1/2/3`, `colorNeutralBackground1`, `colorNeutralStroke2`, `spacingHorizontalS/M`, `spacingVerticalXXS/XS/S/M`, `borderRadiusMedium`, `fontWeightSemibold`, `fontSizeBase200/400`. No hex, no rgba. Dark mode safe by construction.
- **ADR-022** (React 19 functional): all new components / hooks are functional; `React.useState` / `React.useCallback` / `React.useRef` patterns used throughout.
- **ADR-025** (Fluent v9 icons): all icons (`ChevronDownRegular`, `AppsListRegular`, `SearchRegular`, `CheckmarkRegular`) imported from `@fluentui/react-icons` v9. No new SVG web resources.
- **ADR-028** (Spaarke Auth v2): no auth surface affected — criteria are client-side state until the modal launch hands off to `sprk_semanticsearch`, which has its own MSAL bootstrap (`initializeAuth()` in `src/client/code-pages/SemanticSearch/src/index.tsx`). No token snapshots, no access tokens crossing the SpaarkeAi/SemanticSearch boundary.

### What this does NOT change

- **FR-25 / NFR-10** (standalone LegalWorkspace identical): no LegalWorkspace files touched; LegalWorkspace bundle byte-identical (569.35 KB gzip = task 094 baseline).
- **Task 094 pane collapse**: ContextPaneController still wires `paneCollapse?.toggle("context")` via the shared PaneHeader `onCollapse` / `expanded` props. The new `<ContextPaneMenu>` lives in the rightSlot alongside the existing stage label `<Text>`; both are protected by the PaneHeader rightSlot stopPropagation guard from task 094. Click on the pane header (anywhere except the Tools dropdown or the stage label) still collapses the pane.
- **Existing GetStartedCardsWidget card clicks**: all seven `handleGetStartedCardClick` cases still route through the shared `launch*Wizard` helpers from `@spaarke/ui-components`. The handlers are unchanged. The fix is that AFTER the wizard modal closes, the pane re-renders with `selectedTool === "quick-start"` (the default for first-time users + remembered for returning users) so GetStartedCardsWidget appears again — instead of the pane going blank because ShellStage had advanced away from `"welcome"`.
- **Server-driven context_update events**: the `usePaneEvent("context", ...)` subscriber still resolves widgets from the registry on `context_update`, sets `activeWidget`, and the render decision honors `activeWidget` when `selectedTool === "quick-start"`. Phase 3 / 4 (Findings, Progress, Related Items) flows are preserved.

### Verdict

- Task 095 complete — Context pane tool selector + Semantic Search Criteria editor + persisted tool selection landed end-to-end.
- R-24 risk register entry → **RESOLVED**.
- TASK-INDEX row 095 added (Phase F remediation, FULL rigor, deps 094, est 3h).
- `sprk_spaarkeai` deployed to `spaarkedev1`; LegalWorkspace standalone byte-identical (FR-25 preserved); SemanticSearch Code Page untouched.

*End of supplemental deploy (Task 095 / Context tool selector + Semantic Search Criteria).*

## Supplemental Deploy — Task 096 (shared pane foundation polish)

> **Date**: 2026-05-22
> **Task**: 096 — Shared pane foundation polish (title +2px, MDA-width collapse strip, icon-only identifier prop)
> **Phase**: F (Verification — remediation, Round 6 operator smoke)
> **Driver**: Operator feedback 2026-05-22 — three foundational shared-lib changes consumed by all three SpaarkeAi panes; foundation commit for Wave 2 (tasks 097-099 — Assistant / Workspace / Context pane revisions to be created)
> **Verdict**: **PASS — shared lib API surface + visual change landed; Wave 2 unblocked**

### Operator feedback (Round 6, 2026-05-22)

1. "Make the collapse pane wider — too narrow currently. The width should mirror the model-driven app left nav pane collapse" (≈48px).
2. "In collapse mode, use the icon only as the pane identifier — not the words."
3. Across all three panes: "In the pane title, increase the title size font by 2px equivalent."

The widened, icon-only collapsed strip + larger title text are foundational shared-library changes. Each pane's specific updates (Assistant history dropdown, Workspace tab/dropdown changes, Context tool dropdown polish + pin) will land in Wave 2 sub-agents AFTER this foundation commits.

### Files modified

| File | Change |
|---|---|
| `src/client/shared/Spaarke.UI.Components/src/components/PaneHeader/PaneHeader.tsx` | Bump title `<Text>` from `size={300}` → `size={400}` (one Fluent v9 size step up; ≈ 14px → 16px); inline comment documents the bump |
| `src/client/shared/Spaarke.UI.Components/src/components/ThreePaneLayout/ThreePaneLayout.tsx` | (a) Add `COLLAPSED_STRIP_PX = 48` constant near top of file; apply to `leftPaneCollapsed` (was 28) / `rightPaneCollapsed` (was 28) / `centerPaneCollapsed` (was 36) flex-basis + minWidth. (b) Add new `collapsedIcon` style — centered, `tokens.fontSizeBase400`, `tokens.colorNeutralForeground2` → `tokens.colorNeutralForeground1` on hover. (c) Accept new optional props `leftCollapsedIcon` / `centerCollapsedIcon` / `rightCollapsedIcon`. (d) Each collapsed-strip JSX now branches: when icon prop is provided → render icon inside `<span className={styles.collapsedIcon}>` (no rotated text, no chevron); when omitted → fall through to legacy `<ChevronXXX>` + rotated `<span className={styles.collapsedLabel}>` rendering (backwards compatible). |
| `src/client/shared/Spaarke.UI.Components/src/components/ThreePaneLayout/ThreePaneLayout.types.ts` | Add three new optional props: `leftCollapsedIcon?: React.ReactElement`, `centerCollapsedIcon?: React.ReactElement`, `rightCollapsedIcon?: React.ReactElement`. JSDoc references task 096 + documents backwards-compat fallback + aria-label retention via existing `*PaneCollapseLabel` props. |

### Token / dimension changes

| Surface | Before | After | Rationale |
|---|---|---|---|
| PaneHeader title `<Text>` size prop | `size={300}` (`tokens.fontSizeBase300` ≈ 14px) | `size={400}` (`tokens.fontSizeBase400` ≈ 16px) | Operator request: +2px equivalent; stronger visual hierarchy. Fluent v9 token only (ADR-021). |
| Left collapsed strip width | 28px | 48px | Mirrors MDA left-nav collapsed width per operator feedback |
| Right collapsed strip width | 28px | 48px | Same |
| Center collapsed strip width | 36px (task 094) | 48px | Same (uniform across all three for visual consistency) |
| Collapsed identifier (when icon prop provided) | Chevron + rotated label text | Icon only, centered | Operator request: icon-only identifier |
| Collapsed identifier (when icon prop OMITTED) | Chevron + rotated label text | UNCHANGED — legacy rendering preserved | Backwards-compat for standalone LegalWorkspace + any caller that hasn't been updated |

### Backwards compatibility

The new `*CollapsedIcon` props are OPTIONAL. When a caller passes NO icon (the current state of all three SpaarkeAi panes + LegalWorkspace standalone), the rendering falls through to the legacy `<ChevronXXX>` + rotated-text rendering — visually identical to task 094 + 095 behavior (modulo the new 48px width). LegalWorkspace doesn't import `ThreePaneLayout` at runtime, so the strip-width change has no effect there; the `+30 bytes` LegalWorkspace bundle delta is purely the PaneHeader `size={400}` token-reference change.

### Wave 2 wiring deferred

This task DELIBERATELY does NOT modify any SpaarkeAi pane component (`ConversationPane.tsx` / `WorkspacePane.tsx` / `ContextPaneController.tsx` / `ThreePaneShell.tsx`). The Wave 2 agents (tasks 097-099, to be created) will:
- Task 097 (Assistant pane): wire `leftCollapsedIcon={<ChatRegular />}` on `ThreePaneShell`'s ThreePaneLayout instance; add Assistant history dropdown polish.
- Task 098 (Workspace pane): wire `centerCollapsedIcon={<AppsListRegular />}` (or whatever icon WorkspacePane uses in its PaneHeader); apply Workspace tab/dropdown changes.
- Task 099 (Context pane): wire `rightCollapsedIcon={<DocumentRegular />}` (the icon Context pane already passes to PaneHeader); apply Context tool dropdown polish + pin.

Until Wave 2 lands, all three panes continue rendering the rotated-text identifier — operator will see the widened 48px strip + larger title font on first deploy of this task, but the icon-only behavior arrives with Wave 2.

### Build

- **Shared UI library**: `npm run build` — TypeScript clean. PaneHeader.tsx + ThreePaneLayout.tsx + ThreePaneLayout.types.ts all transpile without errors. No new test files added (existing PaneHeader / ThreePaneLayout tests still pass at the props-shape level — adding `*CollapsedIcon` props doesn't change any existing contract).
- **SpaarkeAi**: `npm run build` — **896.67 KB gzip** (vs 896.59 KB task 095 baseline = **+0.08 KB / +80 bytes / +0.009%**). Near-zero delta as expected — only the PaneHeader `size={400}` token reference + the new ThreePaneLayout conditional-branch code execute through the bundle; SpaarkeAi doesn't yet pass the new icon props (Wave 2).
- **LegalWorkspace** (verified for FR-25): `npm run build` — **569.38 KB gzip** (vs 569.35 KB task 095 baseline = **+0.03 KB / +30 bytes**). LegalWorkspace doesn't import `ThreePaneLayout` at runtime; the entire delta is the PaneHeader `size={400}` token reference. Well within the +0.5 KB tolerance band specified by the task. FR-25 / NFR-10 preserved behaviorally — visual rendering identical to task 094/095 modulo the slightly larger PaneHeader title font (applies wherever LegalWorkspace renders a PaneHeader; visually identical to standalone PaneHeader callers).

### Operator-verifiable

1. Open SpaarkeAi → all three panes (Assistant left, Workspace center, Context right) display their PaneHeader title in a noticeably larger font (≈ 16px vs the previous ≈ 14px). Visual hierarchy improvement — title is the strongest element in each pane's header band.
2. Click any pane's header to collapse it (task 094 behavior preserved) → collapsed strip is now **48px wide** (previously 28px for left/right, 36px for center). The wider strip is comfortable to read and easier to click.
3. Inside the collapsed strip, the **legacy rotated-text identifier is STILL shown** in this task — task 096 only adds the icon-only API; Wave 2 (tasks 097-099) wires the icons on each pane. This is INTENTIONAL — operator's icon-only treatment lands once all three panes pass their respective icon props.
4. Backwards-compat sanity check: Open standalone LegalWorkspace (`?webresourceName=sprk_corporateworkspace`) → PaneHeader titles inside LegalWorkspace are also ~2px larger. No `ThreePaneLayout` collapsed-strip rendering occurs in standalone LegalWorkspace (LegalWorkspace uses its own grid layout, not `ThreePaneLayout`).
5. Verify nothing regressed: collapse interactions, splitter drags, keyboard ArrowLeft/Right resize, sessionStorage persistence — all still work (task 094 behavior 100% preserved; this task added optional props + a px constant, no functional removals).

### Edge cases handled

- **Caller passes no `*CollapsedIcon` prop**: render path falls through to the existing `<ChevronXXX>` + rotated-text rendering. ZERO behavioral change vs task 095. This is the state of all current callers (SpaarkeAi + LegalWorkspace). Wave 2 will add the icon props per pane.
- **Caller passes ONE icon prop but leaves the other two omitted**: the wired pane renders icon-only; the others fall through to legacy. Per-pane opt-in works correctly because each conditional branch is independent.
- **`Text size={400}` accessibility**: Fluent v9 `<Text>` honors the user's browser zoom + OS font-size preferences; bumping the size prop one step up does NOT break any of the pane's keyboard / aria-label / tab-order behavior. The PaneHeader's `role="button"` + `aria-expanded` wiring from task 094 is unchanged.
- **Color contrast**: `tokens.colorNeutralForeground2` (collapsed icon at rest) → `tokens.colorNeutralForeground1` (hover) — both pass WCAG AA against `colorNeutralBackground2` in both light and dark Fluent themes (ADR-021 dark-mode safety preserved).

### ADR compliance

- **ADR-012** (Shared component library): all three files modified are in the shared library (`@spaarke/ui-components`). The `COLLAPSED_STRIP_PX = 48` constant is a layout-dimension literal (Fluent has no token for this); the rationale is documented in the inline comment. All other style values use Fluent v9 tokens.
- **ADR-021** (Fluent v9 tokens only): no new hex / rgba literals introduced. Title font size moves between `tokens.fontSizeBase300` → `tokens.fontSizeBase400` (semantic token-based). Collapsed-icon color uses `tokens.colorNeutralForeground2` + `tokens.colorNeutralForeground1`. Dark-mode safe.
- **ADR-022** (React 19): all changes are functional-component / token-prop edits; no new hooks, no class components, no React 16 fallbacks.

### What this does NOT change

- **FR-25 / NFR-10** (standalone LegalWorkspace identical): no LegalWorkspace files touched; PaneHeader title font bump applies wherever LegalWorkspace renders a PaneHeader (a visual improvement, not a behavioral change). LegalWorkspace doesn't import `ThreePaneLayout` so the strip-width + icon-prop changes are no-ops for LegalWorkspace standalone.
- **Task 094 pane collapse**: the `onCollapse` / `expanded` props on PaneHeader, the `*Collapsed` / `onToggle*` props on ThreePaneLayout, and SpaarkeAi's `usePaneCollapse` hook are all unchanged. Click-the-header-to-collapse + localStorage persistence + center-pane collapse all work identically.
- **Task 095 Context tool selector + Semantic Search Criteria**: ContextPaneController's `<ContextPaneMenu>` rightSlot dropdown + Semantic Search criteria editor + `selectedTool` persistence are all unchanged.

### Verdict

- Task 096 complete — shared-lib foundation for Round 6 operator polish landed.

## Task 097 — Assistant pane: History as dropdown

> **Date**: 2026-05-22
> **Task**: 097 — Assistant pane revisions: History trigger becomes a Fluent v9 dropdown matching Workspace/Context UX; collapsed Assistant strip renders the `ChatRegular` icon via task 096's new `leftCollapsedIcon` prop
> **Phase**: F (Verification — remediation, Round 6 operator smoke — Wave 2 of 3)
> **Driver**: Operator feedback 2026-05-22 — Assistant pane's History affordance was an icon-only button opening a slide-in `OverlayDrawer`; this read as a Model-Driven Apps far-right side-pane pattern and was visually inconsistent with the Workspace ("Workspace ▾") + Context ("Tools ▾") dropdowns. Wave 2 commit 1 of 3 (siblings: task 098 = Workspace, task 099 = Context).
> **Verdict**: **PASS — Assistant pane trigger + surface now match Workspace/Context UX; collapsed strip icon wired; LegalWorkspace untouched**

### Operator feedback addressed (Assistant pane block, Round 6)

> "Assistant pane:
> - In the pane title, increase the title font size by equivalent 2px [DONE in Wave 1 task 096 — automatic via PaneHeader `size={400}`]
> - The current history uses the model-driven app far-right side pane pattern; this is probably because this is pulling a Dataverse table; but this pattern is different than for the Workspace pane or Context pane — unusual pattern for the user. Does it have to be this way? if not then make it a dropdown like the Workspace pane and Context pane dropdown
> - Replace the 'History' icon with words 'History' and dropdown arrow so looks consistent to Workspace pane and Context pane"

### Rendering pattern finding (investigation)

**The operator's MDA-pattern hypothesis was incorrect, but the UX problem they flagged was real.** The previous `HistoryOverlay` (task 022) was a Fluent v9 `<OverlayDrawer>` (a frontend slide-in overlay) — NOT an MDA-driven `Xrm.Navigation.navigateTo` to a Dataverse table view. Data is sourced from the BFF endpoint `GET /api/ai/chat/sessions?limit=50` via `authenticatedFetch` (see `HistoryOverlay.tsx` task-022 implementation lines 327–391). The reason it FELT like the MDA side-pane pattern was the combination of (a) icon-only trigger button in the PaneHeader, (b) slide-in surface from the trailing edge, (c) no text label on the trigger — which collectively echoes the MDA "far-right side pane" affordance even though the implementation is pure Fluent v9 React. Converting to a dropdown is therefore **straightforward** — no data-source plumbing is needed; only the trigger surface + the list surface change.

### Path A vs Path B decision

**Path A chosen.** The 50-item ceiling fits comfortably inside a scrollable `<MenuPopover>` (max-height 360px, ~10 items visible, scroll for the rest), so we replace BOTH the trigger AND the surface with a single Fluent v9 `<Menu>` — matching the WorkspacePaneMenu + ContextPaneMenu pattern verbatim. Path B (keep the OverlayDrawer surface, swap only the trigger) was considered but would leave the Assistant pane with a surface mismatched against Workspace + Context (which render their lists inline in MenuPopover) — partial consistency only. Path A delivers full consistency.

### Files modified

| File | Change |
|---|---|
| `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/components/conversation/HistoryOverlay.tsx` | Wholly rewritten as `HistoryMenu` — a self-contained `<Menu>` + `<MenuTrigger>` (subtle Button with text "History" + `<ChevronDownRegular />` icon, `iconPosition="after"`, mirroring WorkspacePaneMenu lines 492–505 + ContextPaneMenu lines 141–155) + `<MenuPopover>` with `max-height: 360px` + `overflow-y: auto` for scrolling. List items are `<MenuItem>` elements with a two-line layout (title semibold + relative timestamp meta) and the same selection handler (`onSelectSession` ➜ `setChatSessionId`). Loading / error / empty states render inline inside the MenuPopover (`statusRow` style). BFF fetch path unchanged — same URL, same `authenticatedFetch`, same telemetry constant `TELEMETRY_HISTORY_OVERLAY_LOAD_FAILURE`. Legacy `HistoryOverlay` named export kept as `export const HistoryOverlay = HistoryMenu` alias for grep-safe migration. |
| `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/components/conversation/ConversationPane.tsx` | (a) Removed `HistoryRegular` icon import — no longer used. (b) Renamed import `HistoryOverlay` → `HistoryMenu`. (c) Removed `historyOpen` state + `handleOpenHistory` + `handleCloseHistory` handlers (Menu manages its own open/close). (d) Removed the `<Tooltip>` + `<Button icon={<HistoryRegular />}>` wrapper from the `PaneHeader.rightSlot` prop; replaced with `<HistoryMenu onSelectSession={setChatSessionId} bffBaseUrl={...} authenticatedFetch={...} />` directly. (e) Removed the separate `<HistoryOverlay>` JSX block beneath the PaneHeader (Menu renders its popover anchored to the trigger via Fluent v9 portal — no sibling render needed). Updated inline comments to cite task 097 + reference WorkspacePaneMenu / ContextPaneMenu siblings. |
| `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/components/shell/ThreePaneShell.tsx` | (a) Added `import { ChatRegular } from "@fluentui/react-icons"`. (b) Added `leftCollapsedIcon={<ChatRegular />}` prop on `<ThreePaneLayout>` (consumes task 096's new shared-lib API) so the Assistant collapsed strip renders the chat icon centered instead of the rotated "Assistant" text fallback. Mirrors the icon the Assistant PaneHeader itself shows when expanded. Workspace + Context will pass their own `centerCollapsedIcon` / `rightCollapsedIcon` in their sibling Wave-2 tasks (098 / 099). |

### Visual / UX changes (operator-visible)

| Surface | Before (task 096) | After (task 097) |
|---|---|---|
| Assistant PaneHeader rightSlot trigger | Icon-only `<Button>` with `<HistoryRegular />` icon, no label, opens slide-in overlay | Subtle `<Button>` with text "History" + `<ChevronDownRegular />` icon (after label) — visually identical to "Workspace ▾" + "Tools ▾" |
| Surface for the session list | Right-edge `<OverlayDrawer>` (360px slide-in) | Inline `<MenuPopover>` anchored to the trigger (positioning="below-end"), 360px max-height with internal scroll |
| List item rendering | Custom `<button>` rows inside a `<div role="list">` (Drawer body) | Fluent v9 `<MenuItem>` rows inside `<MenuList>` (standard Menu semantics, keyboard nav out of the box) |
| Loading / empty / error states | Drawer body shows centered Spinner / empty message / Retry button | MenuPopover shows the same states inline (`statusRow` style); Retry calls `setReloadKey` + the fetch effect refires (popover stays open via `event.stopPropagation()`) |
| Collapsed Assistant strip | Rotated "Assistant" text (task 094 fallback rendering — task 096 added the icon API but ThreePaneShell hadn't passed it yet) | Centered `<ChatRegular />` icon (consumes task 096 `leftCollapsedIcon` prop); aria-label "Assistant" retained via existing `leftPaneCollapseLabel` |
| PaneHeader title font | 16px (`fontSizeBase400`) — landed in Wave 1 task 096 | 16px (unchanged — Wave 1 already applied; this task confirms no regression) |

### What this does NOT change

- **BFF endpoint contract**: `GET /api/ai/chat/sessions?limit=50` is called identically — same URL, same auth, same response shape. The BFF is wholly untouched (Wave 2 of the project is frontend-only).
- **Telemetry constant**: `TELEMETRY_HISTORY_OVERLAY_LOAD_FAILURE` is still the only event emitted on failure. The constant name retains the word "overlay" for now to avoid churning the App Insights consumer; a rename to `TELEMETRY_HISTORY_LOAD_FAILURE` is a candidate follow-up but is NOT part of this task (operator-visible behavior is unchanged).
- **`LegalWorkspace` standalone**: no LegalWorkspace files touched. LegalWorkspace doesn't render `ConversationPane` / `ThreePaneShell` and so is wholly unaffected. FR-25 / NFR-10 preserved.
- **Wave 2 sibling tasks**: Workspace pane (task 098) + Context pane (task 099) are running in parallel and own their own pane-specific revisions. This task's commit is Wave 2 commit 1 of 3 — deploy is coordinated by the main session after all three commits land.

### ADR compliance

- **ADR-012** (shared component library): `HistoryMenu` is solution-local in SpaarkeAi (mirrors WorkspacePaneMenu + ContextPaneMenu placement — pane-specific menus stay solution-local; the foundation primitives `<Menu>` / `<MenuTrigger>` / `<MenuPopover>` come from Fluent v9). The `leftCollapsedIcon` prop wired in ThreePaneShell consumes task 096's shared-lib API exactly as intended.
- **ADR-021** (Fluent v9 tokens only): no hex / rgba literals introduced. Trigger uses `tokens.colorNeutralForeground*` via Fluent's subtle Button appearance; popover uses `tokens.fontSize*` / `tokens.spacing*` / `tokens.colorNeutralForeground*`; status rows use `tokens.colorPaletteRedForeground1` (matches existing error styling). Dark-mode safe.
- **ADR-022** (React 19): `HistoryMenu` is a functional component with hooks (`useState`, `useEffect`, `useCallback`); ConversationPane changes are all functional-component prop edits.
- **ADR-028** (no auth surface change): `HistoryMenu` accepts `authenticatedFetch` as a prop (same as the prior `HistoryOverlay`) — no token snapshots, no `accessToken` props anywhere. Auth contract preserved per §H-4.

### Operator-verifiable (post Wave-2 deploy)

1. Open SpaarkeAi → Assistant pane PaneHeader: the rightSlot now shows a subtle button labeled "History" with a small chevron arrow after the text — identical visual treatment to Workspace pane's "Workspace ▾" and Context pane's "Tools ▾".
2. Click "History ▾": a dropdown opens (anchored below the trigger, not a side-overlay). Up to 50 recent chat sessions render as MenuItems with a title (semibold) and a relative timestamp ("Just now" / "5m ago" / "3d ago" / localized date).

4. Collapse the Assistant pane (click the pane header): the collapsed strip now shows a centered `<ChatRegular />` icon instead of rotated "Assistant" text. Click the strip to re-expand. ARIA label "Assistant" still announced by screen readers (preserved via `leftPaneCollapseLabel`).
5. Edge cases: open the dropdown with no sessions → MenuPopover shows "No recent conversations." inline. Open with a network failure → shows "Couldn't load history. Try again." + Retry button (clicking Retry re-fires the fetch; popover stays open).
6. Backwards-compat: open standalone LegalWorkspace (`?webresourceName=sprk_corporateworkspace`) → completely unchanged (no LegalWorkspace files touched; LegalWorkspace doesn't render `ConversationPane`).

Renaming to `TELEMETRY_HISTORY_LOAD_FAILURE` (and updating App Insights queries that consume it) is a candidate cosmetic follow-up. **Not** fixed here because (a) the rename would touch the telemetry test file and require coordinating with any App Insights queries that already filter on the existing name, (b) operator-visible behavior is unchanged, (c) sibling Wave-2 tasks are landing in parallel and we want minimal cross-task churn.

## Task 098 — Workspace pane: tabs + dropdown polish

> **Date**: 2026-05-22
> **Task**: 098 — Workspace pane revisions: remove inline pin icon from tab rows, bump tab title font, downsize close × icon, rename dropdown trigger label, surface pin toggle as a left-column affordance on every layout row in the Select Workspace section, remove the "Edit current workspace" menu entry (moved to task-093 Manage workspaces side pane).
> **Phase**: F (Verification — remediation, Round 6 operator smoke — Wave 2 of 3)
> **Driver**: Operator feedback 2026-05-22 (Workspace pane block) — the per-tab pin icon clutters every tab; the dropdown label is singular when it should be plural; pinning is not surfaced from the workspace selection surface; Edit current dilutes the dropdown's "selection-only" purpose. Wave 2 commit 2 of 3 (siblings: task 097 = Assistant, task 099 = Context).
> **Verdict**: **PASS — Workspace tabs cleaner, dropdown is the canonical pin surface, Edit moves out (task 093); LegalWorkspace untouched**

### Operator feedback addressed (Workspace pane block, Round 6)

> "Workspace pane:
> - In the pane title, increase the title font size by equivalent 2px [DONE in Wave 1 task 096 — automatic via PaneHeader `size={400}`]
> - In the tabs, remove the 'pin' icon from the tab title
> - In the tabs, increase the size of the tab title
> - In the tabs, reduce the size of the close 'x' icon
> - In the Workspace drop down, change the label of the drop down from 'Workspace' to 'Workspaces'
> - In the Workspace dropdown, add the pin indicator icon and turn on/off to the dropdown; pin indicator to the left of the workspace
> - In the drop down, remove the 'Edit current'
> - Move the 'Edit' workspace to the Manage workspace [hosted by task 093]
> - Move the delete workspace to the Manage workspace [hosted by task 093]"

### What changed

#### `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/components/workspace/WorkspaceTabManagerComponent.tsx`

- **Pin button removed from every tab row.** Operator: "pin belongs in the workspace selection surface, not on every open tab." The `PinRegular`/`PinFilled` imports, the `pinnedIds` derived `Set<string>` state + sync effect, and the `handlePinToggle` callback were all deleted. The tab row now contains only the label + close affordance.
- **Tab title font size bumped one Fluent v9 step**: `tokens.fontSizeBase200` → `tokens.fontSizeBase300` (with matching `lineHeightBase200` → `lineHeightBase300`). The bumped title visually matches the slightly larger pane title polished in Wave 1 (task 096). The tab loading badge stays at `fontSizeBase200` — the spinner row is intentionally less prominent than the resolved title.
- **Close × icon downsized** by swapping `DismissRegular` (20px) → `Dismiss12Regular` (12px). Both are real exports from `@fluentui/react-icons` v9. The Button hit area is unchanged at 16×16 (the surrounding tab itself is the primary 40px target per Fluent v9 tab pattern). Choosing `Dismiss12Regular` over `Dismiss16Regular` produces the cleanest visual subordination to the bumped title.
- The Wave-1 `pinButton` / `pinButtonActive` style entries were deleted.
- The pin localStorage contract (`spaarke:workspace:pinned-list` in `services/pinnedWorkspaces.ts`) and the cold-load auto-open behavior in `WorkspacePane.tsx` are **unchanged** — the dropdown (below) writes to the same list.

#### `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/components/workspace/WorkspacePaneMenu.tsx`

- **Trigger label**: `"Workspace"` → `"Workspaces"` (operator request — plural is more accurate; the dropdown lists ALL available workspaces, not just the current one).
- **Pin indicator per layout row (Select Workspace section)**. Each `<MenuItem>` now renders a `<div className={styles.layoutRow}>` containing:
  ```
  [pin Button] [layout name <span>] [CheckmarkRegular if active]
  ```
  - Pin icon variant: `PinRegular` (outline) when unpinned, `PinFilled` (solid) when pinned.
  - Color tokens: unpinned uses `tokens.colorNeutralForeground3` (subtle); pinned uses `tokens.colorBrandForeground1` (unambiguous brand accent at a glance).
  - The pin Button uses `appearance="subtle"` + `size="small"` with 20×20 `minWidth/height`. `aria-pressed` reflects state. Tooltip: `"Pin {name} to start"` / `"Unpin {name} from start"`.
  - **stopPropagation** pattern: the Button's `onClick` calls `e.stopPropagation()` before invoking the toggle handler, so the parent `<MenuItem onClick={() => handleLayoutSelect(layout.id)}>` does NOT also fire. An `onKeyDown` handler stops Enter/Space from bubbling to the MenuItem when the pin Button is focused — Button's native click-on-keyup handling still toggles pin.
  - **Synchronous re-render**: pin state is mirrored into a React `Set<string>` (`pinnedIds`) initialised from `getPinnedWorkspaces()`. A `useEffect` keyed on `menuOpen` re-syncs from localStorage whenever the menu opens (defensive — covers pins changed by another surface).
  - Writes go through `pinWorkspace(layoutId, layoutName)` / `unpinWorkspace(layoutId)` from `services/pinnedWorkspaces.ts` — the task-092 storage contract, unchanged. The cold-load `WorkspacePane` mount effect consumes the same list, so pinning from the dropdown auto-opens that workspace as a tab on the next page load.
- **"Edit current workspace" menu entry removed** along with its `handleEditWorkspace` callback and the `EditRegular` icon import. Operator: "the dropdown should be for SELECTION, not editing — editing lives in the manage surface." A JSDoc breadcrumb above the action section now reads:
  ```
  Edit + Delete moved to Manage workspaces side pane (task 093).
  Operator feedback 2026-05-22: dropdown should be for SELECTION,
  not editing — editing lives in the manage surface.
  ```
  The `launchWizard` helper itself remains in the file (still used by `handleCreateWorkspace`) and is available for task 093 to import + re-use for edit/saveAs flows from the new side pane.
- **`+ New Workspace` and `Manage workspaces` entries are untouched** (Manage workspaces stub still logs the task-093 breadcrumb to console).

### Not in scope

- `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/components/shell/ThreePaneShell.tsx` — `centerCollapsedIcon` prop wiring is handled by the main session after all Wave-2 commits land (sequential to avoid 3-way merge on a single file with Assistant/Context agents).
- `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/components/workspace/WorkspacePane.tsx` — the cold-load auto-open effect is intentionally not touched. The dropdown writes to the same localStorage list that effect already reads.
- `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/services/pinnedWorkspaces.ts` — task-092 API consumed unchanged.
- `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/components/workspace/WorkspaceTabManager.ts` — verified by grep: zero pin-related metadata in this file. Pin state was owned by `pinnedWorkspaces.ts` + the component-local `pinnedIds` Set; no tab-manager changes needed.
- `src/client/shared/Spaarke.UI.Components/*` — Wave 1 sealed.
- `src/solutions/LegalWorkspace/*` — FR-25 preservation.

### Bundle

- **Post-task-098 SpaarkeAi bundle**: 892.78 KB gzip.
- **Wave-1 baseline (task 096)**: 896.67 KB gzip.
- **Delta**: **-3.89 KB gzip** (-0.43%). The reduction comes from deleting the per-tab pin button code (state + handler + JSX), the `PinRegular`/`PinFilled` imports in WorkspaceTabManagerComponent, the `EditRegular` import + `handleEditWorkspace` callback + Edit current MenuItem in WorkspacePaneMenu, and the unused `pinButton`/`pinButtonActive` style entries. The new dropdown pin column reuses imports already present (Button, Tooltip, makeStyles, mergeClasses) and adds back PinRegular/PinFilled — net is still negative.

### ADR compliance

- **ADR-012** (Shared component library): both files modified are SpaarkeAi-local — they consume context (tab state, layouts hook, pin service) that does not belong in the shared library. Correctly local. Shared `@spaarke/ui-components` (PaneHeader, ThreePaneLayout) untouched.
- **ADR-021** (Fluent v9 tokens only): no new hex / rgba literals. Pin column uses `tokens.colorNeutralForeground3` / `tokens.colorNeutralForeground1` / `tokens.colorBrandForeground1` / `tokens.colorNeutralBackground3Hover`. Tab title moves between Fluent v9 semantic size tokens (`fontSizeBase200` → `fontSizeBase300` + matching line-height). Dark-mode safe by construction.
- **ADR-022** (React 19): functional components only; no new hooks beyond `useState` / `useEffect` / `useCallback` (already used). No class components, no React 16 fallbacks.
- **ADR-025** (Fluent v9 icon library): `Dismiss12Regular`, `PinRegular`, `PinFilled` are all `@fluentui/react-icons` v9 exports (verified by `node -e require('@fluentui/react-icons')` against the installed package). No new SVG web resources.
- **ADR-028** (auth v2): no auth surface touched. `useAiSession` and `authenticatedFetch` consumption in `WorkspacePaneMenu` is unchanged.

### Smoke test plan (post-deploy)

1. Load SpaarkeAi (`?webresourceName=sprk_spaarkeai`); Workspace pane mounts. Verify pinned workspaces auto-open as tabs (existing task-092 behavior, unchanged).
2. Verify each open tab shows label + close × only (no pin icon). Tab label is one step larger than before; close × is visibly smaller (Dismiss12Regular).
3. Open the Workspaces dropdown (header right slot — trigger button now reads "Workspaces ▾"). Verify each layout row shows: pin icon (LEFT), name, optional active checkmark (RIGHT).
4. Click the pin icon on an unpinned workspace → it flips to `PinFilled` brand-color immediately; `localStorage.getItem('spaarke:workspace:pinned-list')` includes the entry; the row's MenuItem.onClick (handleLayoutSelect) did NOT fire (no new tab opened, menu still open).
5. Click the layout name (anywhere except the pin icon) → menu closes, new workspace opens as a tab. Pin state unchanged.
6. Click the pin icon on a pinned workspace → it flips back to `PinRegular`; localStorage entry removed.
7. Verify the dropdown no longer contains "Edit current workspace"; "+ New Workspace" and "Manage workspaces" entries still present.
8. Reload the page → workspaces that are pinned auto-open as tabs (round-trips through localStorage).
9. Backwards-compat: open standalone LegalWorkspace (`?webresourceName=sprk_corporateworkspace`) → completely unchanged.

**Wave 2 — operator smoke feedback, 2026-05-22**

### Operator feedback addressed (Context pane block, 2026-05-22)

> "Context pane:
> - In the pane title, increase the title size font by 2px equivalent [DONE in Wave 1 — automatic]

> - For the quick start tool, Add a title identifying as 'Quick Start'
> - For the Semantic Search criteria tool, include the 'type' fields as are available in the full semantic search code page"

Search button launches the modal as today. NO Saved Searches in the compact in-pane view.

### Files modified

- `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/components/context/ContextPaneController.tsx` — dropped stage label rendering from `<PaneHeader>` rightSlot (Tools dropdown alone, right-justified — mirrors Workspace pane). Wrapped the welcome-stage `<GetStartedCardsWidget>` in a new "Quick Start" section header (`<Text size={400} weight="semibold">`, color `colorNeutralForeground1`, padding `spacingVerticalM` top / `spacingVerticalS` bottom / `spacingHorizontalM` sides). `stageLabelMap` + `contextStage` are retained for ARIA / debug — surfaced as `data-context-stage` on the root for test-harness assertions, keeping `noUnusedLocals` satisfied without rendering any visible "Sources" / "Get Started" / etc. text.
- `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/components/context/ContextPaneMenu.tsx` — added a clickable pin icon on the LEFT of each tool's name (`PinRegular` outline / `PinFilled` solid brand foreground). Single-pin semantics enforced at the storage layer. Pin click uses `stopPropagation()` + `preventDefault()` so it does NOT trigger the MenuItem's `onSelectTool`. Tooltip + `aria-pressed` + `aria-label` provided. Pin state hydrated on mount + re-read whenever the menu opens (covers other-tab pin changes). Pin styling mirrors task 098's `pinButton` / `pinButtonActive` posture on the Workspace pane verbatim so the operator sees a coherent cross-pane pin UX. The `<CheckmarkRegular>` active marker remains on the row's icon prop to indicate the currently SELECTED tool (which may differ from the pinned default at runtime).
- `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/components/context/SemanticSearchCriteriaTool.tsx` — replaced single-select Domain `<Dropdown>` with a 2×2 grid of **4 type-toggle buttons** (Documents = `DocumentRegular`, Matters = `BriefcaseRegular`, Projects = `FolderRegular`, Invoices = `ReceiptRegular`). Active type uses `appearance="primary"`; the rest use `appearance="subtle"`. Added **per-domain filter dropdowns**: Document Type + File Type (Documents domain only), Matter Type (Documents + Matters domains). Static placeholder option lists (`Contract`/`NDA`/`Brief`/`Agreement`/`Invoice`; `PDF`/`DOCX`/`XLSX`/`PPTX`/`TXT`; `Litigation`/`Transactional`/`Regulatory`/`Advisory`) with a TODO for filter-options endpoint wiring. Added **Date Range dropdown** with preset options: Off / Last 7 days / Last 30 days / Last 90 days / Custom range (the "Custom range" option is a static value today; expanding to inline date inputs is documented as a follow-up). Replaced the previous from/to `<Input type="date">` row entirely. Removed the `headerSubtitle` "Refine your query..." line — the layout already matches the operator's screenshot without it. Search button is now full-width primary at the bottom. Build URL `data` payload extended with `documentType` / `fileType` / `matterType` / `dateRange` params (only emitted when relevant for the active domain AND non-default). Backwards-compat persistence in `localStorage["spaarke:context:semantic-search-criteria"]` — missing fields read as undefined and default to "All" / "Off" on next mount.
- `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/hooks/useContextTool.ts` — `readPersistedTool()` now consults the new `getPinnedContextTool()` utility as the fallback when no `selected-tool` value exists in localStorage. If both `selected-tool` AND `pinned-tool` exist, `selected-tool` wins (user's last-used > pinned default). This makes the pin's "default on load" semantics take effect on first session + cold reset without disturbing the existing tool-selection persistence flow. Header JSDoc updated to document the new first-mount semantics.
- `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/services/contextToolPin.ts` — **NEW** utility. Exports `getPinnedContextTool()` / `pinContextTool(id)` / `unpinContextTool()`. Single-pin storage at `localStorage["spaarke:context:pinned-tool"]` (JSON string). Validated against `VALID_CONTEXT_TOOL_IDS` on every read; corrupt / unknown values fall back to `null`. Same try/catch-wrapped posture as `useContextTool.ts` (task 095) and `usePaneCollapse.ts` (task 094) — silent failure on private-browsing / quota-exceeded.

### What is NOT changed (deliberate)

- **`ThreePaneShell.tsx`** — icon-wiring across all 3 panes (the `*CollapsedIcon` props added by task 096) is owned by the main session after Wave 2 lands. Not touched here.
- **`@spaarke/ai-widgets/GetStartedCardsWidget`** — out of scope. The new "Quick Start" header is rendered AROUND the widget by `ContextPaneController`, not by editing the widget itself.
- **`@spaarke/ui-components/PaneHeader`** — Wave 1 sealed (task 096). The rightSlot's right-justification is the existing CSS — removing the stage label `<Text>` is sufficient to make the Tools dropdown alone sit right-justified.
- **Backend filter-options endpoint wiring** — the per-domain filter dropdowns use static placeholder lists today. The TODO in `SemanticSearchCriteriaTool.tsx` documents this. The full SemanticSearch Code Page will receive whichever values the user picked via URL query params; the modal's own `useFilterOptions` hook fetches the real lists on the page side.
- **"Custom range" date inputs** — the Date Range dropdown's "Custom range" option is static today; selecting it does not currently surface from/to date inputs in the pane. Documented as a follow-up in the file header.
- **`src/solutions/LegalWorkspace/*`** — untouched (FR-25 / NFR-10 preserved).
- **`src/client/code-pages/SemanticSearch/*`** — read for visual reference (`SearchFilterPane.tsx`, `SearchDomainTabs.tsx`, `FilterDropdown.tsx`, `DateRangeFilter.tsx`, `types/index.ts`) but NOT imported — the `SearchDomain` union is replicated locally in `SemanticSearchCriteriaTool.tsx` to keep the SpaarkeAi bundle tree-shake clean.

### Operator-verifiable

Click the pin on Semantic Search → the pin flips to filled / brand foreground; refresh the browser (or clear `localStorage["spaarke:context:selected-tool"]`) → on next load, Semantic Search is the default tool. Click the pin again → pin clears; on next cold load, Quick Start (the hardcoded default) is selected.

Switch to Matters → Document Type + File Type disappear, only Matter Type remains. Switch to Projects or Invoices → only Date Range remains. ### ADR compliance

- **ADR-012** (Shared component library): all five files modified are SpaarkeAi-local. The `SearchDomain` union, `DateRangePreset` union, static option lists, storage keys, modal launch helper are all solution-specific concerns; no shared-lib placement needed. `getPinnedContextTool` / `pinContextTool` / `unpinContextTool` live in `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/services/contextToolPin.ts` (mirroring `pinnedWorkspaces.ts` in the same directory).
- **ADR-021** (Fluent v9 tokens only): no hex / rgba literals. All colors use `colorBrandForeground1`, `colorNeutralForeground1/2/3`, `colorNeutralBackground1`, `colorNeutralBackground3Hover`, `colorNeutralStroke2`. All spacing uses `spacingHorizontal*`, `spacingVertical*`. Font sizes use `fontSizeBase200`. Font weights use `fontWeightSemibold`. Border radius uses `borderRadiusMedium`. The only hardcoded pixel values are the `20px` / `72px` / `0` for the pin button + textarea min-height + button padding, all of which are layout-dimension literals (not color / spacing / typography tokens) — same posture as task 098's pin button on the Workspace pane.
- **ADR-022** (React 19): all five files are functional components / hooks — no class components, no React 16 fallbacks. State management via `React.useState` + `React.useCallback`. Lazy initializer pattern (`useState(() => readPersistedCriteria())`) for one-shot hydration.
- **ADR-025** (Fluent v9 icon library): all icons from `@fluentui/react-icons` v9 — `PinRegular`, `PinFilled`, `ChevronDownRegular`, `AppsListRegular`, `SearchRegular`, `CheckmarkRegular`, `Search20Regular`, `DocumentRegular`, `BriefcaseRegular`, `FolderRegular`, `ReceiptRegular`. No new SVG web resources.
- **ADR-028** (no auth surface change): criteria stay client-side until the modal launch hands off to `sprk_semanticsearch`, which has its own MSAL bootstrap. Pin / unpin / selected-tool are all client-side localStorage only. No `authenticatedFetch` calls added. No new token snapshots.
