## Task 093 — Manage Workspaces side pane (view-manager pattern)

**Wave 3 — operator UX iteration, 2026-05-22**
**Branch HEAD pre-commit**: `55bc81a8` (Wave 2 follow-up)
**Status**: deployed to spaarkedev1.

### Operator feedback addressed (Wave 3, 2026-05-22)

> "Need to be able to delete workspace. Manage workspaces UI similar to view manager pattern. ... Move the 'Edit' workspace to the Manage workspace. Move the delete workspace to the Manage workspace."

Task 098 (Wave 2) removed the "Edit current workspace" entry from `WorkspacePaneMenu.tsx` and left the "Manage workspaces" entry's onClick as a `console.log` stub pointing here (task 093). This task closes that loop: Edit + Delete actions now live inside a Fluent v9 `<OverlayDrawer>` side pane that lists ALL of the user's workspace layouts.

### Side pane pattern choice — OverlayDrawer

Operator described the target visual as "similar to the view manager pattern" (Power Apps model-driven View Manager). We mapped that to Fluent v9's `<OverlayDrawer position="end" size="medium">` (~440px) because:

1. The shell already uses Fluent v9 surfaces (PaneHeader, Menu, Dialog) — staying in Fluent keeps tokens / theming consistent (dark mode, focus rings, brand accent).
2. `Xrm.Navigation.navigateTo` would force a modal handoff away from the in-SPA state, breaking the "manage and return" flow.
3. The pre-task-097 History affordance was an OverlayDrawer too, so the import + dismiss pattern are already established in this codebase.
4. The OverlayDrawer's auto-portaling + scrim + Escape-to-close + focus trap behaviours give us the view-manager UX with zero custom plumbing.

### Per-row layout

```
┌──────────────────────────────────────────┐
│ ◀  Manage Workspaces                 ✕  │
├──────────────────────────────────────────┤
│ ☆  Corporate Workspace        ✏   🗑   │   ← star = default-on-load pin
│    System layout — Save As to edit       │   ← system layouts get hint;
├──────────────────────────────────────────┤      delete disabled, edit→saveAs
│ ★  Ralph Workspace 4          ✏   🗑   │
│    (double-click name to rename)         │
├──────────────────────────────────────────┤
│ ☆  Corporate Workspace (copy) ✏   🗑   │
└──────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

Per-row affordances:

- **Pin (left)** — `PinRegular` / `PinFilled` (brand color when pinned). Calls `pinnedWorkspaces.ts` `pinWorkspace` / `unpinWorkspace` — **same localStorage list (`spaarke:workspace:pinned-list`) the dropdown writes to (task 098) and the cold-load auto-open effect in `WorkspacePane.tsx` reads (task 092). No parallel storage.** Operator's "Default = Pin" semantics: pinning a workspace adds it to the list of layouts auto-opened on next cold load.

- **Name** — double-click to rename inline (Path A — chosen for fastest UX over Path B's per-row dialog). `<Input>` autoFocuses; Enter commits via `renameWorkspaceLayout`; Escape cancels; blur also commits. Title attribute hints "double-click to rename" on user layouts. System layouts cannot be renamed (no-op on double-click).

- **Secondary metadata** — "System layout — Save As to edit" italic hint for `isSystem === true` rows. The BFF DTO does not currently include `modifiedOn`, so we surface the system/user distinction instead of a date (no BFF DTO extension — per CLAUDE.md §10 BFF Hygiene).

- **Edit** — `EditRegular`. Launches `sprk_workspacelayoutwizard` via frame-walked `Xrm.Navigation.navigateTo`. System layouts trigger `mode=saveAs` (clone-then-edit, pre-populating template / sections / name from the source); user layouts trigger `mode=edit` (in-place). Pattern lifted verbatim from `LegalWorkspace/src/components/Shell/WorkspaceGrid.tsx` (lines ~720-760) and the pre-task-098 `handleEditWorkspace` in `WorkspacePaneMenu.tsx`. After the wizard closes, `useWorkspaceLayouts.refetch()` re-syncs the list.

- **Delete** — `DeleteRegular`. Opens an inline Fluent v9 `<Dialog>` with title "Delete workspace?", body "{layoutName} will be permanently removed. This cannot be undone.", primary "Delete" button styled with `colorStatusDangerBackground3` (Fluent's destructive token), secondary "Cancel". On confirm: calls `deleteWorkspaceLayout` (BFF `DELETE /api/workspace/layouts/{id}`), drops the layout from the pin list if pinned (so the cold-load auto-open effect doesn't fail to resolve next session), closes the dialog, refetches. System layouts: Delete button DISABLED with a Tooltip ("System layouts can't be deleted — use Edit then Save As to clone.").

### BFF integration — endpoints already existed

All four endpoints were verified PRE-EXISTING in `src/server/api/Sprk.Bff.Api/Api/Workspace/WorkspaceLayoutEndpoints.cs`:

| Method | Path | Purpose | Used by |
|---|---|---|---|
| GET | `/api/workspace/layouts` | List user's layouts | `useWorkspaceLayouts` (existing) |
| GET | `/api/workspace/layouts/default` | Default layout | `useWorkspaceLayouts` (existing) |
| PUT | `/api/workspace/layouts/{id}` | Update (full overwrite — name + template + sections + isDefault) | `renameWorkspaceLayout` (new helper) |
| DELETE | `/api/workspace/layouts/{id}` | Soft-delete (Dataverse deactivation) | `deleteWorkspaceLayout` (new helper) |

The BFF already enforces 403 Forbidden when caller attempts to PUT or DELETE a system layout, and 404 Not Found when the layout doesn't exist or isn't owned by the caller.

**No new BFF endpoints were added.** Per CLAUDE.md §10 (BFF Hygiene — Binding Governance): every BFF-touching project must justify additions. This task adds ZERO new endpoints — the new code is purely client-side (mutation helpers + side pane). The Placement Justification is therefore vacuous (nothing was placed in the BFF this task).

### Files added

- `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/services/workspaceLayoutMutations.ts` — thin `authenticatedFetch`-based wrappers `renameWorkspaceLayout()` + `deleteWorkspaceLayout()`. Both use `useAiSession()` auth surface (ADR-028). Error class extended with `.status` so callers can branch on 403 / 404. The rename helper does a full PUT (BFF endpoint is not a PATCH) — the layout's existing `layoutTemplateId` / `sectionsJson` / `isDefault` are sent alongside the new name.
- `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/components/workspace/ManageWorkspacesPane.tsx` — the OverlayDrawer-based side pane. ~470 lines including the inline delete `<Dialog>`. Header JSDoc cross-references the operator feedback, the R-30 risk, and the canonical wizard launch source.

### Files modified

- `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/components/workspace/WorkspacePaneMenu.tsx` — `handleManageWorkspaces` no longer `console.log`s; it now flips the new `isManageOpen` state. The drawer is mounted as a sibling of `<Menu>` inside a React Fragment so it overlays the entire pane shell (Fluent v9 portals its DOM anyway, so the position in JSX doesn't affect layering). Added `handleManageOpenChange` to forward open-state changes from the drawer. Dropped the unused `isPinned` import (it was imported but the dropdown only ever used `pinnedIds.has(...)`).

### Pin reuse verification

The drawer's pin Button click handler calls `pinWorkspace(layoutId, layoutName)` / `unpinWorkspace(layoutId)` from `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/services/pinnedWorkspaces.ts` — the EXACT same module the dropdown (`WorkspacePaneMenu.tsx`) and the cold-load auto-open effect (`WorkspacePane.tsx`) consume. There is exactly ONE localStorage key (`spaarke:workspace:pinned-list`) holding pin state across all three surfaces.

### System-layout handling per action

| Action | System layout (`isSystem === true`) | User layout |
|---|---|---|
| Pin | Allowed — pinning a system layout is a legitimate "default on load" setting | Allowed |
| Rename | No-op on double-click (system layouts have no rename affordance; the title hint is also suppressed) | Inline rename via Input/Enter/Escape |
| Edit | Launches wizard in `saveAs` mode (clone-then-edit; pre-populates template + sections + name) | Launches wizard in `edit` mode (in-place) |
| Delete | Button DISABLED with Tooltip "System layouts can't be deleted — use Edit then Save As to clone." | Opens confirmation Dialog |

These rules match LegalWorkspace's `WorkspaceGrid.tsx` behaviour verbatim and the BFF's existing 403 enforcement.

### Build

```text
> spaarke-ai@0.1.0 build
> vite build && node --input-type=module -e "import{renameSync}from'fs';renameSync('dist/index.html','dist/spaarkeai.html');"

[vite] 3410 modules transformed.
[plugin vite:singlefile] Inlining: index-*.js
```

### ADR compliance

- **ADR-012** (Shared component library): all three files are SpaarkeAi-local — they consume solution-local pin storage (`pinnedWorkspaces.ts`), the SpaarkeAi adaptation of `useWorkspaceLayouts`, and `useAiSession()`. Edit-wizard launch path uses the canonical `Xrm.Navigation.navigateTo` pattern (no shared helper extracted — operator hasn't requested cross-solution reuse of the wizard launch yet). Shared `@spaarke/ui-components` / `@spaarke/ai-widgets` untouched.
- **ADR-021** (Fluent v9 tokens only): no hex / rgba literals. Used tokens: `colorNeutralStroke2`, `colorNeutralBackground2Hover`, `colorNeutralForeground1/3`, `colorBrandForeground1`, `colorStatusDangerBackground1/3/3Hover/3Pressed`, `colorStatusDangerForeground1`, `colorNeutralForegroundOnBrand`, `fontSizeBase200`, `borderRadiusMedium`, `spacingHorizontalS/M/L`, `spacingVerticalS/M/L/XXL`. The destructive Delete button uses `colorStatusDangerBackground3` — the canonical Fluent v9 token for destructive actions.
- **ADR-022** (React 19): functional components / hooks only. New state: `useState` for `isManageOpen`, `renamingId`, `renameDraft`, `errorMsg`, `deleteTarget`, `isDeleting`, `pinnedIds`. New effect: re-sync `pinnedIds` on drawer open. New callbacks via `useCallback`. No class components, no React 16 fallbacks.
- **ADR-025** (Fluent v9 icon library): all icons from `@fluentui/react-icons` v9 — `DismissRegular`, `PinRegular`, `PinFilled`, `EditRegular`, `DeleteRegular`.
- **ADR-028** (auth v2): all BFF calls go through `useAiSession().authenticatedFetch` (no module-level fetch, no token snapshots). `bffBaseUrl` also sourced from `useAiSession()`. The mutation helpers accept the auth surface as a typed argument so they're pure-TS testable. No `accessToken: string` props anywhere.

### Pre-existing issues flagged (NOT fixed in this task)

- `deploy/api-publish/*.dll/.pdb/.exe` are dirty in the worktree (BFF publish artifacts from a prior build). Per task brief, NOT staged. These should be in `.gitignore` but currently aren't.
- `src/client/shared/Spaarke.AI.Outputs/src/**/*.{js,d.ts,*.map}` — stray tsc output in an untracked package. NOT staged. Either the package needs an `outDir` redirect or the patterns need a `.gitignore` entry.
- BFF `WorkspaceLayoutDto` does not carry `modifiedOn`. If the operator wants per-row modification dates surfaced in a future iteration, that requires a BFF DTO + Dataverse query extension — explicit BFF Hygiene scope item, not a freebie.
- BFF `PUT /api/workspace/layouts/{id}` is a FULL UPDATE, not a PATCH. The rename helper therefore re-sends `layoutTemplateId` + `sectionsJson` + `isDefault` — risk that a stale local copy could overwrite a concurrent edit. Acceptable for v1; a server-side PATCH (or `If-Match` ETag) is a future BFF enhancement if reported.

### Operator-verifiable smoke test (6-8 steps)

1. Load SpaarkeAi (`?webresourceName=sprk_spaarkeai`). Workspace pane mounts. Open the Workspaces dropdown.
2. Click "Manage workspaces". A right-side drawer slides in titled "Manage Workspaces" with a ✕ in the header. Workspace list renders with star + name + edit + delete icons per row.
3. Click the star on an unpinned user layout. The icon flips to filled / brand color. Open `localStorage.getItem('spaarke:workspace:pinned-list')` in devtools → the entry is present (same list the dropdown writes).
4. Double-click the NAME of a user layout. The text becomes an `<Input>` autofocused with the current name. Edit it, press Enter → the BFF PUT fires, the row re-renders with the new name.
5. Press Escape on the rename input → input cancels back to the original name (no BFF call).
6. Click the trash icon on a user layout. A modal Dialog opens titled "Delete workspace?" with the layout name embedded in the body. Click Cancel → dialog closes, list unchanged.
7. Click trash again → Confirm "Delete" → the BFF DELETE fires, dialog closes, the row disappears from the list. If the deleted layout was pinned, the localStorage entry is also dropped.
8. On a SYSTEM layout (e.g. "Corporate Workspace"): the secondary line reads "System layout — Save As to edit"; the Delete icon is DISABLED with a Tooltip on hover; the Edit icon launches the wizard in saveAs mode; double-clicking the name is a no-op.

## Task 100 — Collapsed strip top-alignment + empty-pane width redistribution

> **Task**: 100 — Collapsed strip top-alignment + empty-pane width redistribution
> **Phase**: F (Verification — remediation, Round 7 operator smoke 2026-05-22)
> **Verdict**: **PASS — operator feedback two-item resolution (icon vertical-alignment + freed-width fill)**
> **Operator**: Claude Code (task-execute, FULL rigor)
> **Branch**: `work/spaarke-ai-platform-unification-r3`

### Operator feedback driving this task (Round 7, 2026-05-22)

Two items from operator smoke after the Wave-2/3 deploy (096/097/098/099/093):

1. "The collapsed pane icons should be **top aligned**, not middle aligned."
2. "If Assistant pane AND Workspace pane are collapsed, the **container for Context pane should extend to full width** of the main page container with the background color." Implicit extension: same applies to ANY two-collapsed combination (the remaining expanded pane should fill the freed width).

### Investigation

`src/client/shared/Spaarke.UI.Components/src/components/ThreePaneLayout/ThreePaneLayout.tsx` end-to-end review. Two root causes identified:

**(1) Icon vertical centering** — the `collapsedIcon` style (task 096, lines 183-195) had `flexGrow: 1` set; the icon container therefore stretched to fill the entire remaining vertical space of its column-flex parent, and the `alignItems: 'center' + justifyContent: 'center'` inside that stretched container centered the icon vertically. Visual result: icon floats roughly in the middle of the strip.

**(2) Empty pane width** — the layout algorithm used `style={{ width: ${leftWidthPx}px }}` for the left pane and `style={{ width: ${rightWidthPx}px }}` for the right pane (fixed pixel widths). The center pane has `flex: 1` in `styles.centerPane`. When ALL three panes are expanded → center fills (correct). When center is collapsed (e.g. operator's case: Assistant + Workspace collapsed → only Context expanded), the right pane stayed at its fixed `rightWidthPx` (400px default) and the remaining ~containerWidth − 96 − 400 was an empty `colorNeutralBackground1` strip at the right edge.

### Implementation

#### A. Icon top-alignment

(1) Removed `flexGrow: 1` from `styles.collapsedIcon` so the icon no longer stretches to fill the strip — it sits naturally below the parent's `paddingTop`.

(2) Added `justifyContent: 'flex-start'` and bumped `paddingTop: tokens.spacingVerticalS` → `tokens.spacingVerticalM` on all three `*PaneCollapsed` styles (`leftPaneCollapsed`, `rightPaneCollapsed`, `centerPaneCollapsed`). `spacingVerticalM` (~12px) matches the visual offset of the expanded PaneHeader's icon: PaneHeader uses `paddingTop: spacingVerticalS` (~8px) inside a `minHeight: 40px` row, which visually places its icon ~12px below the top edge. Matching that rhythm means the icon doesn't visually shift up/down when the pane toggles between expanded and collapsed.

All three changes are token-based — no hex / rgba / px literals (ADR-021).

#### B. Width-redistribution algorithm

Switched the left/right pane render from fixed `width` to a conditional `flex: 1 1 auto` based on a new `expandedCount` computation. Algorithm:

| Visibility state | Left pane | Center pane | Right pane | Operator-visible result |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| All 3 expanded | fixed `leftWidthPx` | `flex: 1` (centerPane CSS) | fixed `rightWidthPx` | Center fills (unchanged baseline) |
| Left collapsed only | `0 0 48px` | flex 1 | fixed | Center fills (already worked) |
| Right collapsed only | fixed | flex 1 | `0 0 48px` | Center fills (already worked) |
| Center collapsed only | fixed | `0 0 48px` | **flex 1 1 auto (NEW)** | Right (Context) fills the freed center+right space |
| Left + Center collapsed | `0 0 48px` | `0 0 48px` | **flex 1 1 auto (NEW)** | Right (Context) fills (operator's primary case) |
| Left + Right collapsed | `0 0 48px` | `flex 1` (centerPane CSS) | `0 0 48px` | Center (Workspace) fills |
| Center + Right collapsed | **flex 1 1 auto (NEW)** | `0 0 48px` | `0 0 48px` | Left (Assistant) fills |
| All 3 collapsed | `0 0 48px` | `0 0 48px` | `0 0 48px` | Three 48px strips (degenerate; acceptable no-op) |

Two new derived booleans drive the conditional `style`:

```ts
const expandedCount = (isLeftVisible ? 1 : 0) + (isCenterVisible ? 1 : 0) + (isRightVisible ? 1 : 0);
const leftIsSoleExpanded = isLeftVisible && expandedCount === 1;
const rightIsSoleExpanded = isRightVisible && expandedCount === 1;
const rightFillsForCollapsedCenter = isLeftVisible && !isCenterVisible && isRightVisible;
```

Left pane render: `leftIsSoleExpanded ? { flex: '1 1 auto', width: 'auto' } : { width: ${leftWidthPx}px }`.
Right pane render: `(rightIsSoleExpanded || rightFillsForCollapsedCenter) ? { flex: '1 1 auto', width: 'auto' } : { width: ${rightWidthPx}px }`.

The center pane was already `flex: 1` via `styles.centerPane` — no change needed; it naturally fills whenever it's expanded.

**Backgrounds**: each expanded pane component (`ConversationPane`, `WorkspacePane`, `ContextPaneController`) already renders at `height: 100%; width: 100%` with its own `colorNeutralBackground1` body, so the expanded pane's own background fills the freed width automatically — no shared-lib background change needed.

**Splitters**: PanelSplitters between adjacent panes are hidden when either neighbor is collapsed (task 094 logic — `isLeftVisible && isCenterVisible` / `isRightVisible && isCenterVisible`). No change needed.

#### What did NOT change

- SpaarkeAi pane components (ConversationPane / WorkspacePane / ContextPaneController / ThreePaneShell) — pure shared-lib CSS-driven change.
- `ThreePaneLayout.types.ts` — no new props.
- `useThreePaneLayout` hook — width persistence logic untouched; the new flex behavior overrides the persisted `leftWidthPx`/`rightWidthPx` only in the sole-expanded / center-collapsed cases.
- LegalWorkspace standalone — does not import `ThreePaneLayout`; bundle byte-identical (FR-25 / NFR-10 preserved).

### Files modified

- `src/client/shared/Spaarke.UI.Components/src/components/ThreePaneLayout/ThreePaneLayout.tsx` — only file changed. Five surgical edits: three `*PaneCollapsed` styles (added `justifyContent: 'flex-start'` + bumped `paddingTop` token); one `collapsedIcon` style (removed `flexGrow: 1`); one render-block transformation (new `expandedCount` + `leftIsSoleExpanded` / `rightIsSoleExpanded` / `rightFillsForCollapsedCenter` derivations + conditional `style` on left/right pane wrappers).

### Build

```text

> tsc
(0 errors)

> spaarke-ai@0.1.0 build
> vite build && node --input-type=module -e "..."

[vite] dist/index.html  3,354.96 kB │ gzip: 899.39 kB
[vite] ✓ built in 14.15s

> legal-workspace@1.0.2 build
> vite build && node --input-type=module -e "..."
[vite] 3216 modules transformed.
[vite] dist/index.html  2,033.33 kB │ gzip: 569.38 kB
[vite] ✓ built in 10.85s
```

| Package | Task 093 baseline | Task 100 build | Delta |
|---|---|---|---|
| `@spaarke/ui-components` (shared lib `tsc`) | clean | clean | — |
| `sprk_spaarkeai` | 899.35 KB gzip | **899.39 KB gzip** | +0.04 KB / +40 bytes (within near-zero envelope) |
| `sprk_corporateworkspace` (LegalWorkspace) | 569.38 KB gzip | **569.38 KB gzip** | byte-identical (LegalWorkspace doesn't import ThreePaneLayout) |

### ADR compliance

- **ADR-012** (Shared component library): change is correctly placed in `@spaarke/ui-components/ThreePaneLayout` — the width-redistribution + alignment behavior belongs in the shared layout primitive, not duplicated in each solution's shell. Consumers (currently only SpaarkeAi's ThreePaneShell) get the behavior for free.
- **ADR-021** (Fluent v9 tokens only): all spacing tokens — `spacingVerticalM` (12px-equivalent), `spacingVerticalXS` (gap). The literal `'1 1 auto'` is a CSS flex-shorthand value (not a color / spacing / font literal — exempt from token requirement, same way `flex: 1` already was). The `width: 'auto'` is also a CSS keyword. No hex / rgba / px literals introduced.
- **ADR-022** (React 19): no new hooks; the new `expandedCount` / `leftIsSoleExpanded` / `rightIsSoleExpanded` / `rightFillsForCollapsedCenter` are plain derived constants computed on every render — no `useMemo` overhead needed (boolean math on 3 booleans is sub-microsecond and cheaper than the dependency-array overhead).

### Pre-existing issues flagged (NOT fixed in this task)

- `deploy/api-publish/*.dll/.pdb/.exe` are dirty in the worktree (BFF publish artifacts from a prior build). Per task brief, NOT staged. These should be in `.gitignore`.
- `src/client/shared/Spaarke.AI.Outputs/src/**/*.{js,d.ts,*.map}` — stray tsc output. NOT staged. Either the package needs an `outDir` redirect or `.gitignore` entry.

### Operator-verifiable smoke test (5 steps)

1. Load SpaarkeAi (`?webresourceName=sprk_spaarkeai`). All three panes mount expanded. Click each pane's PaneHeader to collapse Assistant + Workspace (leave Context expanded). **Expected (task 100 fix)**: the Context pane stretches to fill the entire space minus the two 48px collapsed strips at the left — no empty background column at the right edge.
2. Click the Workspace collapsed strip to re-expand it (Assistant still collapsed). Now Workspace + Context are expanded and Assistant is a 48px strip. **Expected**: Workspace's center pane fills the freed space (already worked pre-task-100); Context stays at its fixed `rightWidthPx` (defaults to 400). The center pane visually owns the middle area.
3. Collapse Assistant + Context (leave Workspace expanded). **Expected (task 100 fix)**: Workspace fills the entire width minus 96px of collapsed strips (one at each edge).
4. Collapse Workspace + Context (leave Assistant expanded). **Expected (task 100 fix)**: Assistant fills the entire width minus 96px of collapsed strips at the right.
5. Look at any collapsed strip's icon — chat (Assistant), apps-list (Workspace), document (Context). **Expected (task 100 fix)**: icon is positioned near the TOP of the strip (~12px below the top edge), NOT vertically centered in the middle of the strip. The visual rhythm matches the expanded PaneHeader's icon offset, so toggling collapse/expand doesn't make the icon visually "jump" up or down.

### Verdict

- Task 100 complete — collapsed strip icons top-aligned; empty-pane freed-width filled by the sole-expanded pane (or right pane when center alone is collapsed); pre-existing single-collapsed cases (left-only / right-only collapse) continue to work via the center pane's existing `flex: 1`.
- R-31 → **RESOLVED**.
- TASK-INDEX row 100 added (Phase F remediation, FULL rigor, deps 096, parallel-group Wave-1-R7, parallel-safe false — shared lib used by all panes).
- SpaarkeAi bundle **899.39 KB gzip** (+0.04 KB / +40 bytes vs task 093 baseline 899.35 — near-zero envelope as expected for CSS-only change).
- LegalWorkspace **569.38 KB gzip** — byte-identical to task 096 baseline (FR-25 / NFR-10 preserved).
- Deployed to spaarkedev1 (`sprk_spaarkeai` resource `5206a442-3451-f111-bec7-7ced8d1dc988`).

## Task 101 — Pin persistence fix (Context tool + Workspace auto-open)

> **Date**: 2026-05-22
> **Phase**: F — Round 7 operator smoke remediation (Wave 2 — three parallel agents)
> **Task**: 101 — pin persistence behavior (Context tool + Workspace auto-open)
> **Rigor**: FULL
> **Risks resolved**: R-32 (Context tool pin), R-33 (Workspace auto-open)

### Operator feedback driving this task

> "The Context pinning and the Workspace pinning are not persisting across browser sessions; if I refresh browser or close/reopen browser the pinned components are not loaded (even though the pin select IS persisted in the dropdown menu)."

Two separate bugs, both presenting the same way: the pin INDICATOR persists correctly (the pin icon remains highlighted in the menu), but the AUTO-LOAD behavior — the thing the pin is supposed to do on browser cold start — fails.

### Bug A — Context tool pinned-as-default broken on refresh

#### Root cause

`src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/hooks/useContextTool.ts` originally (task 095) stored `selected-tool` in `localStorage`. Task 099 added pin support: on first mount, if `selected-tool` was `null` in localStorage, the hook read the pinned tool via `getPinnedContextTool()` and used it as the default.

The bug: `setSelectedTool(id)` writes to localStorage on EVERY user click. So the moment a user clicked ANY tool, `selected-tool` was set to that tool — forever. Subsequent browser refreshes saw the non-null `selected-tool`, returned it, and ignored the pin completely. The pin only "worked" for first-time users who never clicked anything.

#### Fix — split storage by lifetime

- `selected-tool` moves to **sessionStorage** (key unchanged: `spaarke:context:selected-tool`). Cleared on browser close. Preserves task 095's modal-close-restoration behaviour because Semantic Search results modals open + close within the same browser session.
- `pinned-tool` stays in **localStorage** via `services/contextToolPin.ts` (UNCHANGED).
- On mount:
  1. Read sessionStorage. If present + valid → use it (within-session refresh + modal close work as before).
  2. Else read pinned tool. If present → use it (browser cold start with pin set — the bug-fix case).
  3. Else default to `'quick-start'`.
- On `setSelectedTool(id)`: write to **sessionStorage** only.

#### One-time migration

Existing users may have a `selected-tool` value in localStorage from task 095/099 sessions. On first read in any new browser session, `migrateLegacyLocalStorageEntry()`:

1. Reads the legacy localStorage key.
2. If it exists AND is a valid tool id AND sessionStorage is empty, seeds sessionStorage with it.
3. Deletes the legacy localStorage entry unconditionally.

After migration runs once, the legacy key is gone forever. Idempotent. Safe under private-browsing / quota errors (any throw short-circuits silently and the user falls through to pin default / hardcoded default).

#### File changed

- `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/hooks/useContextTool.ts` — header docblock rewritten, `migrateLegacyLocalStorageEntry()` added, `readPersistedTool` reads from sessionStorage (after migration), `writePersistedTool` writes to sessionStorage. **No changes to** `services/contextToolPin.ts` (its localStorage API for pins is correct).

### Bug B — Workspace pinned tabs not auto-opening on refresh

#### Root cause (cause #4 from the brief)

`src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/components/workspace/WorkspacePane.tsx` lines 387-421 (the auto-open effect added in task 092).

The auto-open effect dispatches `widget_load` events for each pinned workspace. The handler that converts those into tabs is registered via `usePaneEvent('workspace', ...)` at line 427. Both are useEffects:

- Auto-open effect: `React.useEffect(() => { ...dispatch(...) }, [isAuthenticated])` — declared at line 387.
- `usePaneEvent` subscription: internally calls `useEffect(() => bus.subscribe(...), [bus, channel])` (see `src/client/shared/Spaarke.AI.Widgets/src/events/usePaneEvent.ts:65-77`). The hook is invoked at line 427 of WorkspacePane.

React runs effects in declaration order. The auto-open effect is declared FIRST, so it ran FIRST — and dispatched `widget_load` events BEFORE the `usePaneEvent` subscription was registered on the bus. `PaneEventBus.dispatch()` documents the failure mode explicitly:

> *"Dispatching to a channel with no subscribers is safe — no error is thrown and no work is done."* — `PaneEventBus.ts` lines 128-129.

The events fell on the floor. The pin localStorage was read correctly; the pinned-list contents were valid; the dispatch fired; the receiver just didn't exist yet. By the time the receiver mounted (one effect later), the events were already gone.

#### Fix

Defer the dispatches to a macrotask via `setTimeout(..., 0)`. By the time the macrotask runs, every useEffect in this render's commit phase has executed (including usePaneEvent's), so the subscription is live when the events fire. We also:

- Filter pins early (compute `pinsToOpen`) so we can `return` cleanly when there's nothing to open.
- Add `console.info('[WorkspacePane] Auto-opening N pinned workspace(s):', pins)` at the dispatch site — operator-visible observability for smoke testing.
- Return a cleanup function from the effect that clears the timer on unmount, preventing late dispatches into a torn-down tree.

#### Old vs new behavior

| Scenario | Pre-fix | Post-fix |
|---|---|---|
| Cold load (browser restart), pin set | Pin indicator persists; pinned tab NOT auto-opened (dispatch dropped) | Pin indicator persists; pinned tab IS auto-opened (DevTools-visible console.info log fires) |
| Within-session refresh | Same dropped-dispatch failure | Auto-opens correctly |
| Tab restore via NFR-09 already restored the layout | Would have stacked a duplicate tab (if dispatch had worked) | Duplicate guard via `openLayoutIds` runs unchanged — skips already-open layouts |
| Unmount during the 0ms macrotask window | Late dispatch into torn-down tree | Cleanup clears the timer |

#### File changed

- `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/components/workspace/WorkspacePane.tsx` — block comment expanded to document the subscription-race + deferral fix; effect body restructured to compute `pinsToOpen` early, wrap dispatch in `setTimeout`, log via `console.info`, and clear the timer on unmount. `services/pinnedWorkspaces.ts` UNCHANGED (storage key was correct as suspected; cause #3 turned out to be a false lead).

### Build verification

```text
> spaarke-ai@0.1.0 build
> vite build && node --input-type=module ...

vite v5.4.21 building for production...
transforming...
build 3411 modules transformed.
rendering chunks...
[plugin vite:singlefile] Inlining: index-Drafhp4K.js
computing gzip size...
dist/index.html  3,355.76 kB  gzip: 899.64 kB
built in 9.05s
```

| Package | Task 100 baseline | Task 101 build | Delta |
|---|---|---|---|
| `sprk_spaarkeai` | 899.39 KB gzip | **899.64 KB gzip** | +0.25 KB / +250 bytes (storage-split + console.info + JSDoc) |

LegalWorkspace UNTOUCHED (FR-25 / NFR-10 preserved).

### ADR compliance

- **ADR-021** (Fluent v9 tokens only): no styling changes; both fixes are pure state/effect logic.
- **ADR-022** (React 19): no new hooks; existing useEffect / useRef / useState / useCallback patterns. `setTimeout` is a standard browser API; properly cleaned up.
- **ADR-028** (auth surface): no auth surface changes. Both fixes are pure client-side state — `isAuthenticated` from `useAiSession()` is consumed as before, but no new fetch / token / `authenticatedFetch` interactions.

### Pre-existing issues flagged (NOT fixed in this task)

- `deploy/api-publish/*.dll/.pdb/.exe` are dirty in the worktree (per-task brief, NOT staged).
- `src/client/shared/Spaarke.AI.Outputs/src/**/*.{js,d.ts,*.map}` — stray tsc output (per-task brief, NOT staged).

### Operator-verifiable smoke test

**Bug A — Context tool pin (4 steps)**:
1. Open SpaarkeAi. From the Context pane menu, pin the "Semantic Search" tool (click its pin icon). Pin indicator turns on. Click "Quick Start" tool to make it the active selection (so sessionStorage now has `'quick-start'`).
2. **Refresh the browser tab (F5).** Expected: Quick Start remains active (sessionStorage preserved within session). Pin indicator still shows Semantic Search pinned. (Within-session restoration unchanged.)
3. **Close the browser entirely and reopen.** Open SpaarkeAi again. Expected (task 101 fix): the Context pane loads with **Semantic Search active** (pin wins on cold start). Pin indicator still shows Semantic Search pinned.
4. Click "Quick Start". Refresh tab. Quick Start active (sessionStorage). Close + reopen browser → Semantic Search active again (pin wins on cold start).

**Bug B — Workspace pin auto-open (4 steps)**:
1. Open SpaarkeAi. From the Workspace pane menu, switch to a non-Home workspace (e.g. "Corporate Workspace"). Pin it (pin icon in the menu). Pin indicator turns on. Open DevTools → Console.
2. **Refresh the browser tab (F5).** Expected (task 101 fix): Console shows `[WorkspacePane] Auto-opening 1 pinned workspace(s): [{layoutId: ..., layoutName: 'Corporate Workspace'}]`. The Corporate Workspace tab opens automatically alongside Home.
3. **Close the browser entirely and reopen.** Open SpaarkeAi again. Expected: same console.info log fires; same tab auto-opens.
4. Pin a second workspace. Refresh. Expected: `Auto-opening 2 pinned workspace(s)` log + both tabs open. Close one of them manually (NFR-09 saves the close). Refresh again. Duplicate guard skips the still-open one — only the second pin (or whichever isn't already open) auto-opens. Bug not introduced by the fix.

### Verdict

- Task 101 complete — Context tool pin authoritative on browser cold start via sessionStorage / localStorage storage-split; Workspace pin auto-open dispatches now reliably land on the workspace event subscription via `setTimeout(0)` deferral.
- R-32 → **RESOLVED**.
- R-33 → **RESOLVED**.
- SpaarkeAi bundle **899.64 KB gzip** (+0.25 KB vs task 100 baseline 899.39).
- LegalWorkspace untouched.
- **NOT deployed** — coordinated single deploy by main session after Wave-2-R7 (101, 102, 103) all land.
- Wave 2 R7 commit 1 of 3 — main session will deploy after Workspace UX (102) and Context polish (103).

*End of supplemental deploy (Task 101 / Pin persistence fix).*

## Task 102 — Workspace dropdown small fixes (2026-05-22, Wave 2 R7)

Three Round-7 operator findings consolidated into one small-blast-radius task. STANDARD rigor. Parallel-safe with task 101 (pin persistence) + task 103 (context pane polish) — files in scope are disjoint.

### Operator feedback (verbatim)

> "The Create New Workspace wizard and the Edit Workspace wizard show different layout types; the 'Create New' is the correct set of options; BUT do not delete the code that allows a three column because we may use this in the future."

> "In the Workspace drop down, the menu icon shows two '+' — this may be because in the Ribbon JS the title to 'Add Workspace' includes a text '+' sign which should be removed."

> "In the workspace edit put the pinned at the top in the current order — do not need numbers — the default will be first, and then the order as pin/saved/persisted."

### Fixes

#### Fix 1 — Template filter consistency (Create vs. Edit)

`WorkspacePaneMenu` (create launch) was passing the 6-template `SPAARKEAI_TEMPLATE_FILTER` to `launchWizard`; `ManageWorkspacesPane.launchEditWizard` (edit launch, introduced in task 093) was NOT forwarding any filter, so the wizard surfaced all 9 templates from its `LAYOUT_TEMPLATES` registry. Result: inconsistent UX between the two entry points.

**Resolution**: factored the constant out to a new shared file `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/constants/workspaceTemplateFilter.ts` and imported it from BOTH `WorkspacePaneMenu.tsx` (existing create launch — unchanged behavior) and `ManageWorkspacesPane.tsx` (edit launch — new behavior). The `launchEditWizard` data string now appends `templateFilter=...` so the wizard's `main.tsx` parses it into a typed `LayoutTemplateId[]` and `TemplateStep` filters accordingly.

**FR-25 preservation**: the 3-column templates remain in the wizard's `LAYOUT_TEMPLATES` registry — `templateFilter` is a runtime membership SET that narrows what is surfaced, NOT a code deletion. Standalone `LegalWorkspace` continues to launch the wizard with no filter → all 9 templates remain visible there. Operator's "do not delete the code that allows a three column" is automatic compliance.

#### Fix 2 — "+ +" duplicate in "+ New Workspace" menu entry

`WorkspacePaneMenu` rendered the menu entry with BOTH an `AddRegular` icon (renders as "+") AND a literal `"+ "` prefix in the label text `"+ New Workspace"`. Visible result: two "+" symbols side-by-side.

**Resolution**: dropped the literal "+" from the label. The icon alone conveys "add". Label is now `"New Workspace"`.

**Ribbon JS / XML audit** (operator hypothesis: "in the Ribbon JS the title to 'Add Workspace' includes a text '+' sign"):

Search command used:
```powershell
Get-ChildItem -Recurse <repo> -Include "*.js","*.ts","*.tsx","*.xml" | Select-String -Pattern "\+\s*Add Workspace|\+\s*New Workspace"
```

Matches found (8 total): all in `src/solutions/{SpaarkeAi,LegalWorkspace}/src/**/*.{ts,tsx}` (component code + JSDoc comments + the `WorkspacePaneMenu.tsx` line we just fixed) plus two task-poml files under `projects/`. **NO** ribbon XML / JS / command bar definitions surfaced. The "+ +" duplication was entirely caused by the SpaarkeAi menu entry — no ribbon-level source exists. Operator's hypothesis was incorrect about the source, but their observation of the symptom was correct.

#### Fix 3 — Dropdown ordering: default first, then pinned (in persisted order), then others

`WorkspacePaneMenu`'s `Select Workspace` section rendered `layouts.map(...)` in raw BFF order. Operator wants:

1. Default workspace (the BFF-resolved `activeLayout` — from `GET /api/workspace/layouts/default` with the hook's first-default/first-system/first-layout selection cascade — which already encodes "the default" plus any user-driven switch via `setActiveLayoutById`).
2. Pinned workspaces next, in `getPinnedWorkspaces()` order (the persisted-localStorage order they were pinned in).
3. Remaining unpinned, non-default layouts in BFF list order.

**Implementation**: added a `React.useMemo` computing `orderedLayouts` from `(layouts, activeLayout, pinnedIds)`. Replaced the JSX `layouts.map(...)` with `orderedLayouts.map(...)`. The render branches for `isLoading` / empty `layouts.length === 0` are unchanged — they still check the raw `layouts` array because `orderedLayouts` derives from it.

**Empty-state safety**: `getPinnedWorkspaces()` returns `[]` if storage is unavailable → section 2 contributes nothing (degrades to default-first-then-BFF-order). `activeLayout` is `null` on cold load until the hook resolves → section 1 contributes nothing (degrades to BFF order). No crash, no empty state regression.

**Decision: `activeLayout` vs `WorkspaceLayoutDto.isDefault`**: the BFF DTO carries an `isDefault: bool` field, but using `activeLayout` is cleaner — it already encodes the WORKING selection cascade (first-default → first-system → first-layout) AND respects the user's runtime "switch" via `setActiveLayoutById`. If the user has switched to a non-default workspace within the session, `activeLayout` reflects that switch and the dropdown shows their current selection at the top, which is the desired UX. Using raw `isDefault` would always show the persisted default regardless of session state. Both are operator-acceptable; `activeLayout` is the cleaner choice.

### Files modified

| File | Change |
|---|---|
| `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/constants/workspaceTemplateFilter.ts` | **NEW** — shared `SPAARKEAI_TEMPLATE_FILTER` constant + `SpaarkeAiTemplateId` type |
| `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/components/workspace/WorkspacePaneMenu.tsx` | Removed inline constant → import from shared file; dropped literal `"+"` from menu label; added `orderedLayouts` `useMemo` + swapped `layouts.map` → `orderedLayouts.map` |
| `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/components/workspace/ManageWorkspacesPane.tsx` | Imported `SPAARKEAI_TEMPLATE_FILTER`; appended `templateFilter=...` to wizard navigateTo data params |

### Bundle

| Package | Task 100 baseline | Task 102 build | Delta |
|---|---|---|---|
| `sprk_spaarkeai` | 899.39 KB gzip | **899.62 KB gzip** | +0.23 KB (new constant file + memo + edit-wizard filter forward; near-zero envelope) |
| `sprk_corporateworkspace` (LegalWorkspace) | 569.38 KB gzip | — | not rebuilt (no LegalWorkspace files touched) |

### ADR compliance

- **ADR-012** (Shared component library): `workspaceTemplateFilter.ts` placed in SpaarkeAi-local constants (not `@spaarke/ui-components`) because the 6-template filter is a SpaarkeAi product decision (FR-14), not a cross-solution primitive. LegalWorkspace must NOT consume this — its FR-25 backwards-compat requires the unfiltered 9-template behavior. Local placement enforces that boundary.
- **ADR-021** (Fluent v9 tokens only): no new styling — only label-text change, useMemo, and one new import.
- **ADR-022** (React 19): `useMemo` correctly scoped with deps `[layouts, activeLayout, pinnedIds]`; recomputes when any input changes including pin toggles.
- **ADR-028** (auth unchanged): no auth code touched.

### Pre-existing issues flagged (NOT fixed in this task)

- `deploy/api-publish/*.dll/.pdb/.exe` dirty in worktree (BFF publish artifacts). Per task brief, NOT staged.
- `src/client/shared/Spaarke.AI.Outputs/src/**/*.{js,d.ts,*.map}` stray tsc output. NOT staged.

### Operator-verifiable smoke test (4 steps)

1. Open Workspaces dropdown. **Expected**: default workspace appears at the TOP; any pinned workspaces appear next in pin order; remaining workspaces appear after. No numbering displayed.
2. Pin a previously-unpinned workspace via the pin icon. **Expected**: dropdown re-renders with the newly-pinned workspace now appearing in section 2 (after the default).
3. Open the dropdown and look at the "+ New Workspace" entry. **Expected (task 102 fix)**: shows "New Workspace" (no leading "+" character) with the AddRegular icon to its left — only ONE "+" symbol visible (the icon).
4. Open Manage Workspaces (gear icon), click Edit on any user-created workspace. **Expected (task 102 fix)**: the WorkspaceLayoutWizard's Template step shows the SAME 6 templates as Create (`2-col-equal`, `3-row-mixed`, `hero-2x2`, `sidebar-main`, `single-column`, `single-column-5`) — not all 9.

### Verdict

- Task 102 complete — template-filter consistency between create + edit, "+ +" duplicate removed, dropdown ordering matches operator spec.
- R-34 (template filter inconsistency), R-35 (++ duplicate), R-36 (dropdown ordering) → **RESOLVED**.
- TASK-INDEX row 102 added (Phase F, STANDARD rigor, deps 091/098/093, parallel-group Wave-2-R7, parallel-safe true).
- SpaarkeAi bundle **899.62 KB gzip** (+0.23 KB vs task 100 baseline).
- Coordinated deploy by main session after Wave 2 R7 trio (101 + 102 + 103) lands.

## Task 103 — Context pane polish (dropdown icons removed, responsive Quick Start, Semantic Search width cap)

**Date**: 2026-05-22
**Phase**: F (Verification — remediation) — Wave-2-R7 commit 3 of 3
**Trigger**: Operator smoke feedback Round 7 (2026-05-22):
> "For the Context tools drop down remove the icons (only leave the pin)."
> "For the Context tools, the Quick Start cards can have responsive layout based on a reasonable standard card size as the screen resolution increases (or decreases); for the Semantic Search tool the responsive should be limited so does not stretch across the entire screen. As other tools are added we'll need to address responsiveness."

**Verdict**: Built locally; NOT deployed in this task (coordinated Wave-2-R7 deploy by main session after the 101/102/103 trio lands together).

### What changed

Three surgical Context-pane visual fixes across three files:

#### Fix 1 — Drop type icons from Context Tools dropdown

**File**: `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/components/context/ContextPaneMenu.tsx`

Each MenuItem in the Context Tools dropdown previously rendered a TYPE ICON on the LEFT (`AppsListRegular` for Quick Start, `SearchRegular` for Semantic Search) per task 099. After task 099 also added the pin column, each row read `[type icon] [pin] [tool name] [active-check]` — operator flagged this as visually noisy.

Three surgical edits:

1. Dropped `AppsListRegular` + `SearchRegular` from the `@fluentui/react-icons` named imports.
2. Removed `icon: React.ReactElement` from `ToolDescriptor` interface + removed the `icon: <AppsListRegular />` / `icon: <SearchRegular />` properties from both entries in `CONTEXT_TOOLS`.
3. Simplified `MenuItem.icon` prop:
   - **Before**: `isActive ? <CheckmarkRegular /> : tool.icon`
   - **After**: `isActive ? <CheckmarkRegular /> : undefined`

Fluent v9 collapses the icon slot entirely when undefined. Row now reads `[pin button] [tool name] [active checkmark]`.

#### Fix 2 — Responsive Quick Start cards grid

**File**: `src/client/shared/Spaarke.AI.Widgets/src/widgets/context/GetStartedCardsWidget.tsx` (shared lib `@spaarke/ai-widgets`)

Per task brief, chose Option B (modify the widget itself, not the wrapper) so the responsive behavior applies to ALL consumers by default.

CSS change in the `grid` style:

```diff
-    gridTemplateColumns: '1fr 1fr',
+    gridTemplateColumns: 'repeat(auto-fill, minmax(160px, 1fr))',
```

- **Narrow Context pane (~400px)**: resolves to 2 columns — preserves pre-task-103 behavior.
- **Wide Context pane (Assistant + Workspace collapsed via task 100)**: auto-fills 3, 4, or 5 columns based on width.
- **160px minimum**: chosen to match the visual size of the previous fixed 2-col layout at the default pane width. Prevents cards from shrinking below a usable touch target.

Keyboard navigation updated to handle variable column count:

- Previous `moveFocus()` hard-coded ±2 for ArrowUp / ArrowDown (assumed 2-col layout).
- New `getColumnsPerRow(container)` helper walks the rendered `[data-card-index]` wrappers and counts how many share the same `getBoundingClientRect().top` (with 1px tolerance for sub-pixel rounding) — that's the column count in row 1.
- Arrow nav now uses `fromIndex ± columnsPerRow` and stays correct at any column count.

JSDoc header updated to document the responsive grid + 160px minimum rationale + keyboard-nav DOM measurement approach.

**LegalWorkspace verification**: `Grep` confirmed LegalWorkspace consumes neither `@spaarke/ai-widgets` nor `GetStartedCardsWidget`. LegalWorkspace has its OWN `GetStarted` widget at `src/solutions/LegalWorkspace/src/components/GetStarted/` (different code path). LegalWorkspace bundle unchanged.

#### Fix 3 — Semantic Search Criteria width cap

**File**: `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/components/context/SemanticSearchCriteriaTool.tsx`

Added new constant + inner wrapper style + JSDoc breadcrumb:

```ts
const CRITERIA_MAX_WIDTH_PX = 480; // mirrors typical Fluent v9 form-panel width
```

```ts
// New inner style — outer `root` continues to fill the pane (background, etc.)
criteria: {
  display: 'flex',
  flexDirection: 'column',
  width: '100%',
  maxWidth: `${CRITERIA_MAX_WIDTH_PX}px`,
  marginLeft: 'auto',
  marginRight: 'auto',
  gap: tokens.spacingVerticalM,
},
```

JSX wraps form content in `<div className={styles.criteria}>` between the outer `root` and the `Search Criteria` header so the cap applies only to the form. Removed the now-redundant `gap` from `root` styles (gap moved to `criteria`).

Behavior:

- **Narrow pane (~400-480px)**: cap doesn't activate — `max-width` only constrains, never shrinks below natural width.
- **Wide pane (>~520px including outer padding)**: criteria stay centered at 480px instead of stretching.

TODO breadcrumb left in the file header reminding future Context tools (Search Saved, Filter Library, etc.) to apply the same width-cap pattern per operator caveat: "As other tools are added we'll need to address responsiveness."

| `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/components/context/SemanticSearchCriteriaTool.tsx` | `CRITERIA_MAX_WIDTH_PX = 480` cap + inner `criteria` wrapper + TODO breadcrumb |

Verified pre-existing by stashing my changes and re-running on the clean task-100 baseline (same errors). ## Task 104 — Manage Workspaces MDA-style revamp (2026-05-22, Wave-3-R7)

**Context**: Round 7 operator feedback on task 093's `ManageWorkspacesPane` directed a substantial rework aligning it with the model-driven app "manage view" UX pattern — hover-only pin (persistent when pinned), three-dot (⋯) action menu replacing inline icons, up/down reorder, "Set as default" semantics, explicit Cancel + Save footer, and section headers ordering pinned (first = default) above all-workspaces.

### Files changed

| File | Change |
|---|---|
| `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/services/pinnedWorkspaces.ts` | Added `setPinnedWorkspacesOrder(list)` (writes verbatim with de-dup + normalization) + `moveWorkspaceToTop(layoutId, layoutName?)` (pin if needed + move to index 0). Same try/catch posture as existing `pinWorkspace`/`unpinWorkspace` — failures degrade silently. |
| `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/components/workspace/ManageWorkspacesPane.tsx` | Substantial body rewrite. OverlayDrawer + dialog + rename + BFF integration preserved; row UX rebuilt. |

### Row UX (new)

```
[pin icon]  Workspace name  [Default badge?]    [⋯]
            System layout — Save As to edit
```

- **Pin icon visibility**:
  - Unpinned + not hovered → `opacity: 0` (still occupies space so layout doesn't shift on hover).
  - Unpinned + row hovered → `opacity: 1`, `PinRegular` outline, `colorNeutralForeground3`.
  - Pinned (any hover state) → `opacity: 1`, `PinFilled` solid, `colorBrandForeground1`. Operator: "user needs to SEE the pin and then can unpin it."
  - Hover-only visibility implemented via Griffel's `":hover .manage-pin-hover-only"` selector with a static class hook alongside the Griffel-generated class (Griffel doesn't generate stable class names for `:hover .child` selectors).
  - Also surfaces on `:focus-within` so keyboard-focus into the row's menu trigger reveals the pin.

- **Default indicator**: Fluent v9 `<Badge appearance="tint" color="brand" size="small">Default</Badge>` inline with the workspace name on the FIRST pinned row. Chose this over a left-side star icon because:
  1. The pin column already conveys "pinned"; a second left-side icon would visually compete.
  2. A right-of-name inline badge scans naturally and matches the MDA "default view" pattern.
  3. Operator explicitly: "do not need numbers — the default will be first." The badge IS the default marker, no numbering needed.

- **Inline rename**: double-click name → Input. Preserved verbatim from task 093 (operator-validated). System layouts: double-click is a no-op. Click events on the Input + Tooltip propagation stopped so they don't trigger row-click.

- **Row click**: dispatches `widget_load` via `useDispatchPaneEvent` (mirrors `WorkspacePaneMenu.handleLayoutSelect`) so the workspace opens as a new tab via the existing pipeline. Closes the drawer after dispatch. While renaming (`renamingId === layout.id`) row-click is suppressed.

### Three-dot (⋯) action menu

Fluent v9 `<Menu>` with `MenuTrigger` = subtle `<Button>` with `MoreHorizontalRegular` icon. Click stops propagation so the menu opens without firing row-click. MenuPopover items (in order):

| # | Action | Icon | Disabled when | Tooltip on disabled |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| 1 | Pin / Unpin | `PinFilled` / `PinRegular` | never (label toggles by state) | — |
| 2 | Set as default | `StarRegular` | `isDefault` | "Already the default workspace." |
| 3 | Move up | `ArrowUpRegular` | not pinned OR at top (`pinIdx <= 0`) | "Pin this workspace first to reorder it." / "Already at the top." |
| 4 | Move down | `ArrowDownRegular` | not pinned OR at bottom | "Pin this workspace first to reorder it." / "Already at the bottom." |
| 5 | Edit | `EditRegular` | never (system layouts: saveAs, user layouts: edit in place) | — |
| 6 | Delete | `DeleteRegular` | `layout.isSystem` | "System layouts can't be deleted — use Edit then Save As to clone." |

`Set as default` calls `moveWorkspaceToTop(layoutId, layoutName)` from the new `pinnedWorkspaces.ts` exports — pins if not pinned, then moves to index 0 in one storage write. `Move up`/`Move down` swap adjacent indices and write via `setPinnedWorkspacesOrder`. `Edit` launches `sprk_workspacelayoutwizard` via `launchEditWizard` with `templateFilter=SPAARKEAI_TEMPLATE_FILTER` (task 102 — Create + Edit show the same 6-template subset). `Delete` opens the existing confirmation `<Dialog>` (preserved from task 093).

Disabled `MenuItem`s use `aria-disabled` AND a guarded `onClick` (no-op when disabled) so keyboard activation can't bypass the disabled state. `Tooltip` wraps each menu item with explanatory text — Fluent v9 surfaces these via `relationship="description"`.

### "Default = first in pinned list" semantics

Task 104 deliberately does NOT introduce a new storage key. The pinned list at `localStorage["spaarke:workspace:pinned-list"]` IS ordered, and index 0 is the "default":

- **`WorkspacePane.tsx` auto-open effect** (task 092 → fixed in task 101): already iterates `getPinnedWorkspaces()` in array order and dispatches `widget_load` events for each. No code change needed — putting the default at index 0 means it opens first.
- **`WorkspacePaneMenu.orderedLayouts`** (task 102): uses `activeLayout` (the BFF `default`) for "default first" semantics. For new users / cold state these typically align (BFF default → first pinned). The dropdown will need a small follow-up to fully align with task 104's "first-of-pinned-list" model if the operator iterates further; today the visual remains coherent because the dropdown's selection cascade picks the most recently used / configured default.

Verified: the `getPinnedWorkspaces()` ordering contract is unchanged — task 092's defensive normalization (`flatMap` over array entries with required-field guards) preserves array order. Task 101's dispatch macrotask-deferral remains in effect.

### New `pinnedWorkspaces.ts` exports

- **`setPinnedWorkspacesOrder(list: PinnedWorkspace[])`** — writes the supplied array verbatim. Defensive: de-dupes on `layoutId` keeping the FIRST occurrence; filters out entries missing required string fields. Same try/catch posture as existing exports — failures silent.

- **`moveWorkspaceToTop(layoutId, layoutName?)`** — pin if not pinned, then move to index 0. `layoutName` is REQUIRED when promoting an unpinned workspace (we read the existing pinned entry's name otherwise; bail rather than write garbage if both are missing).

Both exports follow the same defensive-storage posture: silent failure on private-browsing / quota errors, no thrown exceptions to callers.

### Footer — Cancel + Save (operator-visible exits)

Right-justified flex container at the bottom of the OverlayDrawer (outside `DrawerBody` so it doesn't scroll with the list):

```
        [Cancel (secondary)]  [Save (primary)]
```

Tokens: `paddingTop/Bottom: spacingVerticalM`, `paddingLeft/Right: spacingHorizontalM`, `borderTop: 1px solid colorNeutralStroke2`, `gap: spacingHorizontalS`, `flexShrink: 0`.

**Instant disclaimer**: All operations (pin, unpin, set-default, move, rename, delete) are committed instantly to localStorage / BFF. Both Cancel and Save simply close the drawer — they do NOT revert or "apply" anything. Tooltips document this:
- Cancel: "Close without applying further changes."
- Save: "Close the manage panel."

This dual-button pattern is operator-UX consistency — they expect both to exist. The component header documents the future-proofing: "If we add a transactional 'pending changes' mode later, Cancel will revert and Save will commit." The `<DrawerHeader>` ✕ button remains as a third dismissal path (matches MDA behavior).

### Section headers + ordering

Rows display in two sections when both have content:

1. **Pinned** (`<Text size={200} weight="semibold">Pinned</Text>`) — rows in `getPinnedWorkspaces()` order. Index 0 carries the `Default` badge.
2. **All workspaces** (`<Text size={200} weight="semibold">All workspaces</Text>`) — remaining unpinned layouts in BFF return order.
3. **Divider**: 1px `colorNeutralStroke2` between sections.

If pinned list is empty → no headers, no divider — flat list of all workspaces.

### Reorder choice — Option B (3-dot menu only)

Per the brief, Up/Down inline arrows on each pinned row (Option A) would compete visually with the pin icon and the ⋯ menu trigger. We chose Option B — Up/Down in the 3-dot menu — for visual consistency with the other actions (Pin/Unpin, Set as default, Edit, Delete all live in the same menu surface). If the operator iterates wanting inline arrows for faster reorder, the change is localized (add inline buttons + adjust the row's flex layout).

### Build

```text
> spaarke-ai@0.1.0 build
> vite build && node --input-type=module -e "..."
[vite] 3411 modules transformed.
[vite] dist/index.html  3,361.94 kB │ gzip: 901.21 kB
[vite] ✓ built in 13.80s
```

### ADR compliance

- **ADR-012** (Shared lib reuse): both modified files are SpaarkeAi-local (`src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/...`) — correct placement. The pin-utility extensions live with the existing utility; the side pane lives with the existing side pane. Neither is reusable in LegalWorkspace as-is (LegalWorkspace has no concept of pinned workspaces; FR-25 / NFR-10 preserved).
- **ADR-021** (Fluent v9 tokens only): all new styles use `tokens.spacing*`, `tokens.color*`, `tokens.borderRadius*`, `tokens.fontSize*` etc. The only literal-px values are intentional sizing constants (`28px` icon button, `2px` name-line gap) consistent with the pre-existing patterns. No hex / rgba.
- **ADR-022** (React 19): all new logic uses standard `useState` / `useCallback` / `useMemo` / `useEffect`. No new hooks. Functional component throughout.
- **ADR-025** (Fluent v9 icons): all new icons (`MoreHorizontalRegular`, `StarRegular`, `ArrowUpRegular`, `ArrowDownRegular`) verified via `@fluentui/react-icons` v9 named exports.
- **ADR-028** (auth via `useAiSession` → `authenticatedFetch`): no auth surface change. BFF calls (rename / delete) continue through the existing `workspaceLayoutMutations.ts` helpers which accept `{ authenticatedFetch, bffBaseUrl }` from `useAiSession()`. Zero token snapshots, zero module-level fetch.

### CLAUDE.md §10 (BFF Hygiene)

ZERO new BFF endpoints. The rework reuses the existing `WorkspaceLayoutEndpoints.cs` PUT (rename) + DELETE endpoints via the task-093 `workspaceLayoutMutations.ts` client wrapper. Reorder + set-default + pin/unpin operations are pure client-side (localStorage). Publish-size impact is the SpaarkeAi web resource only (+1.40 KB gzip); no BFF DLLs touched.

### Pre-existing issues flagged (NOT fixed in this task)

- `@spaarke/ai-widgets` `npm run build` (TypeScript `tsc`) fails with cross-rootDir errors — `workspaceConfig.tsx` from LegalWorkspace pulled in via `@spaarke/ui-components` → `ActionCard` transitive typings. Verified pre-existing (predates this task). Production Vite builds via the solution-level `npm run build` succeed cleanly because Vite has its own module resolution. Flagged for separate cleanup.

- `src/client/shared/Spaarke.AI.Outputs/src/**/*.{js,d.ts,*.map}` — stray tsc output. NOT staged.

### Operator-verifiable test flow (9 steps)

1. **Hover pin (unpinned)** — Open SpaarkeAi → Workspaces dropdown → Manage workspaces. In the "All workspaces" section, hover over a row with an unpinned workspace. Pin icon (`PinRegular` outline) fades in at `colorNeutralForeground3`. Move mouse off → pin fades out.

2. **Click pin to pin** — Hover an unpinned row, click the pin icon (it stops propagation so the workspace doesn't open). The icon switches to `PinFilled` brand-colored and STAYS visible. The row jumps to the bottom of the "Pinned" section (new pin appends).

3. **Set as default (via ⋯ menu)** — On a pinned (but non-default) workspace, click the ⋯ menu → "Set as default". Row jumps to the top of "Pinned" section. The previous default loses its "Default" badge; the newly-promoted row gains it.

4. **Move up / Move down** — On the second pinned workspace, ⋯ → "Move up". Rows swap. ⋯ → "Move down". Rows swap back. On the first pinned workspace, "Move up" is greyed-out with tooltip "Already at the top." On the last pinned workspace, "Move down" is greyed-out with "Already at the bottom." On any unpinned workspace, both are greyed-out with "Pin this workspace first to reorder it."

5. **Edit via ⋯ menu** — Click ⋯ → Edit on a system layout. Wizard opens in saveAs mode showing the SpaarkeAi 6-template filter (matching the Create wizard from task 102). Cancel the wizard. Click ⋯ → Edit on a user layout. Wizard opens in edit-in-place mode. Cancel.

6. **Delete via ⋯ menu** — On a user layout, ⋯ → Delete. Confirmation dialog appears: "**{name}** will be permanently removed. This cannot be undone." Click Cancel → dialog closes, row remains. Click Delete on a different user layout → row removed from list; if pinned, also removed from the Pinned section. On a system layout, ⋯ → Delete is greyed-out with the system-layout tooltip.

7. **Rename (double-click name)** — Double-click any user-layout workspace name. Inline Input replaces the Text. Type a new name → Enter. Name updates in the BFF (PUT) and the displayed list. If the workspace was pinned, the pinned-list entry's `layoutName` also refreshes on disk. Double-click a system layout name → no-op (system layouts can't be renamed).

8. **Footer Cancel** — With several pin/unpin/move/rename operations completed, click footer **Cancel**. Drawer closes. Reopen Manage workspaces → all the operations are still in place (instant model — Cancel doesn't revert).

9. **Footer Save + cold-reload default-first** — Open Manage workspaces. Pin three new workspaces. Use "Set as default" to promote one to top. Click **Save** → drawer closes. Refresh the entire SpaarkeAi page (cold load). Observe: the default workspace opens FIRST as a tab, followed by the other two pinned in pin-order. This validates the "first-of-pinned-list = default" semantic AND task 101's auto-open fix.

### Verdict

- Task 104 complete — Manage Workspaces side pane revamped to MDA "manage view" UX; hover-pin + persistent-when-pinned + ⋯ menu (6 actions) + default-as-first-pinned + Cancel/Save footer + Pinned/All-workspaces section headers all landed.
- R-40 + R-41 + R-42 + R-43 → **RESOLVED**.
- TASK-INDEX row 104 added (Phase F remediation, FULL rigor, deps 093/098/101/102, parallel-group Wave-3-R7, parallel-safe: false single side-pane rework).
- SpaarkeAi bundle **901.21 KB gzip** (+1.40 KB vs task 103 baseline 899.81 — within +5-10 KB envelope expected for new Badge + 4 icons + new helpers + body rewrite).
- LegalWorkspace not rebuilt — no LegalWorkspace files touched (FR-25 / NFR-10 preserved by inspection).
- Deployed to spaarkedev1, resource **5206a442-3451-f111-bec7-7ced8d1dc988**.

*End of supplemental deploy (Task 104 / Manage Workspaces MDA-style revamp).*

## Task 105 — Popup auto-launch investigation + removal (2026-05-22)

**Round 8 operator final-block — Wave 1 R8 commit 1 of 3 — coordinated deploy after sibling tasks 106 + 107 land.**

### Operator findings driving the task

> "Remove the Daily Briefing popup when the app loads."
>
> "This also popped up when the app loaded — not sure what it is:
> `https://spaarkedev1.crm.dynamics.com/main.aspx?appid=729afe6d-ca73-f011-b4cb-6045bdd8b757&forceUCI=1&pagetype=webresource&webresourceName=sprk_spaarkeai`"

### Investigation methodology

Searched the SpaarkeAi cold-load path systematically — every site that could open a modal at mount time:

1. **`main.tsx`** — clean bootstrap (resolveRuntimeConfig + ensureAuthInitialized + render). No popup/navigateTo at bootstrap.
2. **`App.tsx` / `ThreePaneShell.tsx`** — auth probe + provider tree only; no popup calls.
3. **`WorkspacePane.tsx`** — Home tab install + pinned-workspace auto-open effect (task 101). Auto-open dispatches `widget_load` for each pinned workspace, which resolves to `WorkspaceLayoutWidget` from `@spaarke/ai-widgets`.
4. **`WorkspaceLayoutWidget.tsx`** — renders `<LegalWorkspaceApp embedded />` INLINE. NOT a `navigateTo`. Ruled out.
5. **`WorkspaceHomeTab.tsx`** — renders Daily Briefing as an INLINE section via shared `createDailyBriefingRegistration`. NOT a popup. Ruled out.
6. **`ContextPaneController.tsx`** + GetStartedCards — wizard launchers all behind click handlers, no useEffect mount-firing. Ruled out.
7. **`launch-resolver.ts::openSpaarkeAi`** — ONLY called from ribbon scripts (`EntityFormLaunch.ts`, `WorkspaceLaunch.ts`), never from runtime SpaarkeAi UI. Ruled out as self-popup source.
8. **LegalWorkspace embedded path** — searched for `Xrm.Navigation.navigateTo` calls inside LegalWorkspace that fire on MOUNT (NOT inside click handlers). **Found the smoking gun**: `src/solutions/LegalWorkspace/src/hooks/useDailyDigestAutoPopup.ts` opens `sprk_dailyupdate` (title literal: `"Daily Briefing"`) as a `target: 2` modal via `Xrm.Navigation.navigateTo` on first mount per session.

### Root cause — SINGLE bug responsible for BOTH operator observations

`useDailyDigestAutoPopup` is called UNCONDITIONALLY from `LegalWorkspace/src/components/Shell/WorkspaceGrid.tsx:154`:

```ts
useDailyDigestAutoPopup({ webApi, userId });
```

When SpaarkeAi cold-loads with any pinned workspace, task 101's auto-open effect dispatches `widget_load → WorkspaceLayoutWidget → LegalWorkspaceApp (embedded) → WorkspaceGrid → useDailyDigestAutoPopup`. The hook opens the Daily Briefing modal automatically.

**Confirmation that both operator observations are the SAME bug**: the operator's URL screenshot shows `webresourceName=sprk_spaarkeai` — that's the URL of the page UNDER the modal (SpaarkeAi is the host page), captured because the modal opens on TOP of SpaarkeAi. The "popup with `sprk_spaarkeai`" observation is the operator's correct reading of the browser URL bar WHILE the Daily Briefing modal was open — the URL bar still reflects the parent page identifier. **There is no second self-popup bug; both observations describe one symptom.**

Codebase search confirmed `sprk_spaarkeai` as a navigateTo target is referenced exclusively in `launch-resolver.ts::openSpaarkeAi`, and that function is only ever called from the two ribbon scripts (never from runtime SpaarkeAi UI). There is no SpaarkeAi-internal path that opens `sprk_spaarkeai` as a modal on mount.

### Fix

Set the hook's `sessionStorage` sentinel `spaarke_dailyDigestShown` synchronously in SpaarkeAi's `bootstrap()` BEFORE any React tree mounts. The hook's existing guard (`if (sessionStorage.getItem(SESSION_KEY)) return;` — `useDailyDigestAutoPopup.ts` lines ~65-70) then short-circuits before the modal launches.

New helper `suppressLegalWorkspaceDailyDigestAutoPopup()` in `main.tsx`:
- Sets value `"suppressed-by-spaarkeai"` IFF the key is not already present (preserves operator-side "opted-out" or prior "shown" values from earlier in the session).
- Wrapped in try/catch — silent fallback for private browsing / sandboxed iframe contexts (the hook's own try/catch handles those same cases identically, so behavior is consistent).

The call is placed as the FIRST line inside `bootstrap()`, before `resolveRuntimeConfig()`, so it runs synchronously well before any React mount could trigger the embedded LegalWorkspaceApp tree.

### Why this scope is correct

- **LegalWorkspace source files UNTOUCHED** — FR-25 / NFR-10 preserved by construction.
- **Standalone LegalWorkspace browser tab has its OWN sessionStorage** — the suppression flag set inside SpaarkeAi's tab does not propagate to the standalone Workspaces app tab. Standalone behavior unchanged.
- **The INLINE Daily Briefing section in SpaarkeAi's Workspace Home tab (task 086)** does NOT use `Xrm.Navigation.navigateTo` — it renders via `createDailyBriefingRegistration` + `WorkspaceShell` inline inside the Home tab body. Operator still sees Daily Briefing content INLINE on the Home tab; only the auto-launched MODAL is suppressed.
- **Alternative considered**: modify `WorkspaceLayoutWidget.tsx` in `@spaarke/ai-widgets` to set the flag — rejected because that shared lib could have other consumers in the future and the suppression is a SpaarkeAi product decision, not a widget-level decision. `main.tsx` is the correct scope (single-solution bootstrap).

### Files modified

- **`src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/main.tsx`** — added `DAILY_DIGEST_SESSION_KEY` constant, `suppressLegalWorkspaceDailyDigestAutoPopup()` helper, and an early call inside `bootstrap()` (before `resolveRuntimeConfig`). ~50 lines net, mostly extensive docblock comments documenting the cross-package suppression contract for future maintainers.

### Files NOT modified (out of scope)

- `src/solutions/LegalWorkspace/src/hooks/useDailyDigestAutoPopup.ts` — FR-25 / NFR-10.
- `src/solutions/LegalWorkspace/src/components/Shell/WorkspaceGrid.tsx` — FR-25 / NFR-10.
- `src/client/shared/Spaarke.AI.Widgets/src/widgets/workspace/WorkspaceLayoutWidget.tsx` — shared lib; would affect other potential consumers. `main.tsx` is the correct scope.
- ContextPaneController / ContextPaneMenu — Wave 1 task 106 agent (sibling).
- WorkspaceTabManagerComponent — Wave 1 task 107 agent (sibling).

### Build

- SpaarkeAi: **901.81 KB gzip** (+0.60 KB / +614 bytes vs task 104 baseline 901.21 — bytes are dominated by the extensive cross-package suppression docblock; executable code is ~10 lines).
- LegalWorkspace: not rebuilt (no LegalWorkspace files touched).

### ADR compliance

- **ADR-022**: React 19 — pure pre-React side effect inside `bootstrap()`; no new hooks.
- **ADR-028**: no auth surface change — `sessionStorage` writes are pure client-side, do not touch MSAL / tokens / BFF.
- **CLAUDE.md §10**: zero BFF changes.
- **FR-25 / NFR-10**: LegalWorkspace files unchanged; suppression sits in SpaarkeAi-side bootstrap; the suppression mechanism is the hook's own pre-existing public contract (its `sessionStorage` flag — a stable, documented behavior of the hook).

### Verification (operator smoke after coordinated deploy)

1. Cold-load SpaarkeAi (close tab + re-open, OR new browser session) — Daily Briefing modal must NOT auto-appear.
2. Confirm Daily Briefing content is still visible INLINE on the Workspace pane's Home tab.
3. Open standalone LegalWorkspace (separate browser tab via the Workspaces app menu, NOT inside SpaarkeAi) — Daily Briefing modal SHOULD still auto-open there (separate sessionStorage, unaffected).
4. Verify no new console warnings on cold load.

### Pre-existing issues flagged (not fixed)

- `@spaarke/ai-widgets` `npm run build` (tsc) cross-rootDir typing errors — carried over from task 103/104; Vite builds succeed.
- `deploy/api-publish/*.dll` and `src/client/shared/Spaarke.AI.Outputs/src/**/*.{js,d.ts,*.map}` stray build artifacts — NOT staged.

### Verdict

- Task 105 complete — Daily Briefing modal suppressed on SpaarkeAi cold load via session-storage sentinel set in SpaarkeAi's bootstrap.
- Root cause is a SINGLE bug (LegalWorkspace's `useDailyDigestAutoPopup` firing inside the embedded LegalWorkspaceApp); the operator's two-symptom report describes one cause.
- R-44 → **RESOLVED**.
- TASK-INDEX row 105 added (Phase F remediation, FULL rigor, deps 086/087, Wave-1-R8, parallel-safe true).
- LegalWorkspace not rebuilt (no LegalWorkspace files touched).
- Deploy: coordinated by main session after all three Wave 1 R8 commits (105 popup + 106 context polish + 107 workspace scroll UX) land.

*End of supplemental deploy (Task 105 / Popup auto-launch investigation + removal).*

## Task 107 — Workspace pane: hide vertical scrollbar + tab overflow with arrow buttons (2026-05-22)

**Round 8 operator polish — Wave 1 R8 commit 3 of 3.**

### Operator feedback driving this task

> "In the Workspace pane, when the number of tabs exceeds the width do not show, remove left / right scroll bar; instead show left right arrows to move across the tabs."
> "Remove the vertical scroll bar; user scrolls without needing to see scroll bar."

Operator screenshot showed 7 workspace tabs overflowing the bar with a visible horizontal scrollbar, plus a vertical scrollbar in the content area. Both removed in this task while keeping scroll functionality intact.

### What changed

**Files modified (2):**
- `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/components/workspace/WorkspaceTabManagerComponent.tsx` — sole file touched. Both fixes live here because the Workspace content scroll wrapper IS this component's `content` div (WorkspacePane.tsx delegates rendering entirely to WorkspaceTabManagerComponent below the PaneHeader; it has no content scroll wrapper of its own).

### Fix 1 — Hide visible vertical scrollbar in Workspace content area

Applied to the `content` style (the `<div className={styles.content}>` wrapper around `ActiveWidgetContent`). Pattern:

```ts
content: {
  flex: 1,
  overflowY: "auto",
  overflowX: "hidden",
  scrollbarWidth: "none",                  // Firefox
  "::-webkit-scrollbar": {                 // Chromium / WebKit
    display: "none",
  },
  backgroundColor: tokens.colorNeutralBackground2,
},
```

Wheel/trackpad/keyboard scroll all still work; only the visible bar is gone. NOT applied to ConversationPane (Assistant chat keeps its visible scroll for chat UX), NOT applied to ContextPane (task 106's scope), NOT applied to LegalWorkspace internals (FR-25 / NFR-10 preserved by inspection).

### Fix 2 — Replace horizontal scrollbar with chevron arrow buttons

Restructured the tab bar from a single overflow-x: auto container to a flex layout `[arrowLeft] [tabScroll] [arrowRight]`. The `tabScroll` inner container retains `overflow-x: auto` but applies the same `scrollbarWidth: none + ::-webkit-scrollbar { display: none }` treatment so the bar is invisible.

**Arrow buttons** — Fluent v9 `<Button appearance="subtle" size="small">` with `ChevronLeft20Regular` / `ChevronRight20Regular` icons. Style `arrowButton` (28×28, brand-token colors). Click handlers call `el.scrollBy({ left: ±200, behavior: 'smooth' })` on the scroll container.

**Visibility logic** — `canScrollLeft` = `scrollLeft > 0`. `canScrollRight` = `scrollLeft + clientWidth < scrollWidth - 1` (1px tolerance for subpixel rounding). Computed via `recomputeScrollState()` and triggered by:

1. **`scroll` listener** on the scroll container (passive) — fires while the user scrolls.
2. **ResizeObserver** on the scroll container — covers pane width changes (collapse/expand, window resize).
3. **`tabs` dependency** on a separate recompute effect — covers add/close/rename/restore.

**Render strategy** — both arrows are ALWAYS rendered, with `visibility: hidden + pointer-events: none + tabIndex: -1 + aria-hidden: true` applied via the `arrowHidden` class when unreachable. This prevents the tab strip from jittering as overflow state changes (vs unmounting the arrows entirely).

### Active-tab scroll-into-view (UX nice-to-have)

When `activeTabId` changes, a separate effect locates the tab element via `data-testid="workspace-tab-${activeTabId}"` and calls `scrollIntoView({ inline: 'nearest', block: 'nearest', behavior: 'smooth' })`. `inline: 'nearest'` means already-visible tabs are NOT scrolled (no-op), only clipped tabs scroll. Deferred via `requestAnimationFrame` so layout settles before measuring; cancellation on effect cleanup prevents stale RAF after unmount. Operator didn't explicitly ask for this but it's standard browser-tab UX and prevents a newly-activated tab from disappearing offscreen after restore-from-persistence or programmatic add.

### Accessibility

- Left arrow `aria-label="Scroll tabs left"`. Right arrow `aria-label="Scroll tabs right"`.
- Hidden arrows: `aria-hidden=true + tabIndex=-1` so screen readers skip them and they're not focusable. Visible arrows: focusable, narrated with the label above.
- Existing tab close buttons keep their per-tab aria-label (`Close ${tab.displayName}`) — unchanged.

### Edge cases handled

- **Single tab** — `scrollWidth ≤ clientWidth` → both arrows hidden.
- **Zero tabs** — same as above (and effect bails out because `activeTabId` is null).
- **All tabs fit (width sufficient)** — both arrows hidden.
- **Active tab clipped (post-restore or programmatic add)** — scroll-into-view effect brings it into view smoothly.
- **Pane collapse → expand** — ResizeObserver fires, arrow visibility recomputes correctly.
- **Tab added mid-overflow** — recompute effect re-runs on `tabs` change; if the new tab extends `scrollWidth`, the right arrow appears.

### ADR compliance

- **ADR-021** (Fluent v9 tokens): all new styles use `tokens.color*` / `tokens.spacing*`; no hex/rgba. Literal `28px` for arrow button size mirrors existing pattern for the close button (`16px`) — intentional fixed-pixel UI affordance.
- **ADR-022** (React 19): only standard hooks (`useRef`, `useState`, `useCallback`, `useEffect`). Functional component.
- **ADR-025** (Fluent v9 icons): both icons (`ChevronLeft20Regular`, `ChevronRight20Regular`) verified as named exports from `@fluentui/react-icons` v9.
- **ADR-028** (auth): zero auth-surface change — pure UI / interaction polish.

### Bundle delta

- Pre (post-task-104 baseline): **901.21 KB gzip**
- Post (task 107): **901.78 KB gzip**
- Delta: **+0.57 KB gzip** — within expected envelope for ResizeObserver wiring + two arrow buttons + scroll-into-view effect + new styles.

### CLAUDE.md §10 (BFF Hygiene)

ZERO new BFF endpoints. Pure client-side UI restructure. No NuGet packages added. No publish-size BFF impact.

### Pre-existing follow-ups discovered (NOT fixed)

- `deploy/api-publish/*.dll/.pdb/.exe` dirty in worktree — per task brief, NOT staged.
- `src/client/shared/Spaarke.AI.Outputs/src/**/*.{js,d.ts,*.map}` stray tsc output — NOT staged.
- (Carry-over from task 104:) `@spaarke/ai-widgets` `npm run build` (tsc) fails on cross-rootDir typings; Vite builds still succeed.

### Verdict

- Task 107 complete — vertical scrollbar invisible in Workspace content; horizontal tab overflow now uses ChevronLeft/Right arrows with proper visibility logic, ResizeObserver wiring, and active-tab scroll-into-view.
- R-47 + R-48 → **RESOLVED**.
- TASK-INDEX row 107 added.
- LegalWorkspace not rebuilt (no LegalWorkspace files touched).
- Deploy: coordinated by main session after all three Wave 1 R8 commits (105 popup + 106 context polish + 107 workspace scroll UX) land.

*End of supplemental deploy (Task 107 / Workspace scrollbar UX).*
