## Task 106 — Context pane: Semantic Search left-align + drop active checkmark

> **Date**: 2026-05-22
> **Phase**: F (Verification — remediation)
> **Round**: 8 — operator UX iteration
> **Wave**: Wave-1-R8 (commit 2 of 3 — parallel-safe sibling of 105 popup investigation + 107 workspace scroll UX)
> **Branch**: `work/spaarke-ai-platform-unification-r3`
> **Rigor**: STANDARD (two CSS-driven fixes; no logic changes)

### Operator feedback driving this task

1. **Semantic Search left-align** (Round 8, 2026-05-22): "In the Context pane, the semantic search component should be **left aligned** (see screenshot)." Round 7 (task 103) centered the criteria within the pane at a 480px cap; Round 8 reverses the horizontal anchoring to left-aligned while KEEPING the 480px max-width.

2. **Drop the active-tool checkmark** (Round 8, 2026-05-22): "**'Active tool marker' I don't think this is really necessary** — we know what's active because it's what's loaded and there can only be one. Can remove that icon." The `CheckmarkRegular` icon on the active MenuItem (introduced in task 095, kept through task 103's clean-up) is now removed; the pin icon stays (per R7 "only leave the pin" directive).

### Files modified

- `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/components/context/SemanticSearchCriteriaTool.tsx` — `criteria` style: `marginLeft: 'auto'` → `marginLeft: 0`; `marginRight: 'auto'` retained (so the form anchors to the pane's left edge while still allowing the 480px max-width to take effect). `CRITERIA_MAX_WIDTH_PX = 480` constant unchanged. JSDoc + inline comment updated to describe the new "left-aligned, max-width 480px" anchoring + operator rationale.
- `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/components/context/ContextPaneMenu.tsx` — dropped `CheckmarkRegular` import from `@fluentui/react-icons`; removed `activeMarker` Griffel style entry (no other usages); removed the `isActive` const computation (also unused after removal); MenuItem `icon` prop now passes `undefined` unconditionally so Fluent v9 collapses the icon slot entirely. File header + inline catalog comment updated to document the change + operator rationale. The `selectedTool` prop stays on `ContextPaneMenuProps` for interface stability with the parent (`ContextPaneController` still passes it from `useContextTool`); a JSDoc note explains it's now a no-op consumer parameter.

### Visual result

| Surface | Before (task 104 baseline) | After (task 106) |
|---|---|---|
| Semantic Search criteria (wide Context pane) | Centered at 480px with empty space on both sides | Left-aligned at 480px max with empty space on the RIGHT only |
| Semantic Search criteria (narrow Context pane) | Fills the pane naturally (max-width doesn't activate) | Fills the pane naturally (unchanged — max-width still doesn't activate) |
| Context Tools dropdown row | `[pin button] [tool name] [active-check on selected row]` | `[pin button] [tool name]` (no active-check; selection is conveyed by what's loaded in the pane body) |

### Build

```text
> spaarke-ai@0.1.0 build
> vite build && node --input-type=module -e "..."
[vite] 3411 modules transformed.
[vite] dist/index.html  3,364.05 kB │ gzip: 901.81 kB
[vite] ✓ built in 8.39s
```

| Package | Task 104 baseline | Task 106 build | Delta |
|---|---|---|---|

## Task 108 — Build + seed system workspace layouts (Dataverse, dev)

> **Task**: 108 — Build + run `Deploy-SystemWorkspaceLayouts.ps1`
> **Round / Wave**: R8 Wave 2a (operator final-block 2026-05-22, sequential before Wave 2b frontend wiring)
> **Phase**: F (Verification — remediation)
> **Verdict**: **PASS — 4 system layouts seeded in dev; schema column added; idempotency + -Force paths verified**
> **Operator**: Claude Code (task-execute, FULL rigor)
> **Branch**: `work/spaarke-ai-platform-unification-r3`
> **Pre-task HEAD**: `e9d5e0bd` (Wave 1 R8 just deployed)
> **Deploy commit SHA**: filled in after commit

### Operator decision (Round 8, Option B confirmed)

System workspaces — Daily Briefing (renamed from Home), Smart To Do List, My Work, Documents — become real `sprk_workspacelayout` Dataverse records flagged `sprk_issystem=true`, NOT hard-coded frontend tabs. Architectural goal: one workspace concept, one rendering pipeline (`widget_load → WorkspaceLayoutWidget → LegalWorkspaceApp(embedded) → section factories`).

Wave 2b (future task) handles frontend: remove hard-coded `WorkspaceHomeTab`; wire auto-install of default system layout. This task is **DATA + SCRIPT only**, no frontend changes.

### Schema reconnaissance — what `sprk_workspacelayout` actually looks like

Live `EntityDefinitions(LogicalName='sprk_workspacelayout')/Attributes` query returned the pre-existing custom columns:

| Logical name | Type | Notes |
|---|---|---|
| `sprk_workspacelayoutid` | Uniqueidentifier | PK |
| `sprk_name` | String | Display name (PrimaryNameAttribute) |
| `sprk_layouttemplateid` | String | e.g. `single-column`, `2-col-equal`, `3-row-mixed` |
| `sprk_sectionsjson` | Memo | JSON of `{ schemaVersion, rows[], scope }` |
| `sprk_isdefault` | Boolean | Per-user default flag |
| `sprk_isdefaultname` | Virtual | Boolean-label virtual |
| `sprk_sortorder` | Integer | **Range 0-20** (discovered on first live run when -4..-1 rejected) |

`_ownerid_value` (UserOwned). Pre-existing user data: 7 user-created layouts owned by various users — Corporate Workspace was NOT in Dataverse (it lives as a code constant in `SystemWorkspaceLayouts.cs`).

**`sprk_issystem` did NOT exist** — was a code-constant DTO flag on `WorkspaceLayoutDto` only. The brief's verification query `$filter=sprk_issystem eq true` requires the column, so the script's schema half adds it via Dataverse metadata Web API (idempotent: skip if present).

#### sectionsJson shape (confirmed via Corporate Workspace code constant + WorkspaceLayoutWizard/App.tsx::buildSectionsJson)

```jsonc
{
  "schemaVersion": 1,
  "rows": [
    { "id": "row-1", "columns": "1fr", "columnsSmall": "1fr", "sections": ["daily-briefing"] },
    { "id": "row-2", "columns": "1fr", "columnsSmall": "1fr", "sections": [""] }, // empty slot — filtered by buildDynamicWorkspaceConfig
    { "id": "row-3", "columns": "1fr", "columnsSmall": "1fr", "sections": [""] },
    { "id": "row-4", "columns": "1fr", "columnsSmall": "1fr", "sections": [""] }
  ],
  "scope": "my"
}
```

### Section factory IDs — confirmed (vs the brief's guesses)

From `src/solutions/LegalWorkspace/src/sectionRegistry.ts` aggregating `sections/*.registration.ts`:

| Brief guessed | Actual ID in registry | File |
|---|---|---|
| `dailyBriefing` | `daily-briefing` | `sections/dailyBriefing/dailyBriefing.registration.ts:38` |
| `smartToDo` / `todo` / `smart-todo` | `todo` | `sections/todo.registration.ts:52` (label "My To Do List") |
| `quickSummary` | `quick-summary` | `sections/quickSummary.registration.ts:49` |
| `documents` / `activeDocuments` | `documents` | `sections/documents.registration.ts:233` |

All 4 IDs use **kebab-case**. The brief's `dailyBriefing` / `smartToDo` / `activeDocuments` guesses were close but not exact — verified the registry before writing JSON.

### Layout template — `single-column` (canonical, from shared lib)

From `src/client/shared/Spaarke.UI.Components/src/components/WorkspaceShell/layoutTemplates.ts:95-106`: `single-column` = 4 stacked rows of 1 slot. Existing user data confirms `single-column`, `2-col-equal`, `3-row-mixed` are the real IDs.

**Pre-existing issue flagged**: the BFF's `WorkspaceLayoutEndpoints.cs:588-636` `AvailableTemplates` list uses different IDs (`1-column`/`2-column`/`3-column`/`3-row-mixed`) that diverge from the shared-lib canonical list. The BFF list is unused (clients fetch templates from the shared lib `LAYOUT_TEMPLATES` export). NOT fixed here — separate task.

### Path A vs Path B — chose Path B (direct Dataverse Web API)

**Path A (BFF POST)**: `POST /api/workspace/layouts` exists (`WorkspaceLayoutEndpoints.cs:61-72`) but its `CreateWorkspaceLayoutRequest` DTO (`WorkspaceLayoutDtos.cs:42-55`) has no `IsSystem` setter — by design, `sprk_issystem=true` is admin-only and not exposed to user callers.

**Path B (direct Web API)** chosen because:
1. `isSystem=true` is a Dataverse-admin operation — the BFF intentionally does NOT expose it.
2. Seeding is a one-time admin task, not a runtime user operation.
3. Path B matches existing patterns: `Deploy-SpaarkeAi.ps1` (web-resource updates) and `Create-ScopeCapabilityFields.ps1` (metadata changes).

CLAUDE.md §10 (BFF Hygiene): ZERO new BFF endpoints added. Direct Web API metadata + data writes.

### Script architecture

**Files created**:
- `scripts/Deploy-SystemWorkspaceLayouts.ps1` (~280 lines) — single-script seed with schema + data halves
- `scripts/system-layouts.json` (4 layout definitions externalized for readability)

**Parameters**:
- `-DataverseUrl` (default `https://spaarkedev1.crm.dynamics.com`)
- `-LayoutsFile` (default `<scriptDir>/system-layouts.json`)
- `-WhatIf` (dry-run: print would-create/would-replace, no writes)
- `-Force` (PATCH `sprk_layouttemplateid` + `sprk_sectionsjson` + `sprk_isdefault` + `sprk_sortorder` on existing records; default is skip)
- `-SkipSchema` (skip the schema half — useful when re-running after column already provisioned)

**Flow**:
1. Load JSON sidecar.
2. Acquire `az login` token (mirror `Deploy-SpaarkeAi.ps1` pattern).
3. **Schema half**: `Test-AttributeExists` for `sprk_issystem`. If missing, `POST EntityDefinitions(LogicalName='sprk_workspacelayout')/Attributes` with a `BooleanAttributeMetadata` (`SchemaName=sprk_IsSystem`, default=false, Yes/No options). Sleep 5s for metadata to settle. Skip if `-SkipSchema`.
4. **Data half**: for each layout — `GET ?$filter=sprk_name eq '<name>' and sprk_issystem eq true` → if found: skip (default) or PATCH (with `-Force`); if missing: `POST` with `Prefer: return=representation` to capture GUID. Idempotent.
5. **Verification**: live query `?$filter=sprk_issystem eq true` printed as a summary table.

**Sortorder fix**: initial JSON used -4..-1 (intent: system layouts ordered BEFORE user layouts via negative sort). Dataverse `sprk_sortorder` schema range is 0-20 — rejected. Changed to 0-3. Service-layer logic (`WorkspaceLayoutService.GetLayoutsAsync` lines 64-66) concatenates system layouts BEFORE user layouts list-wise, so collision with user sortOrder doesn't affect display order.

`-Force` path verified to find existing records by name + flag.

### Per-user default — flagged for Wave 2b

`Daily Briefing` was seeded with `sprk_isdefault=true`. The layout is owned by the script-runner (UserId `1d02f31c-1872-f011-b4cb-7c1e52671ad0`). `WorkspaceLayoutService.GetDefaultLayoutAsync` filters defaults by per-user `ownerid` (line 137-141), so OTHER users will not currently see Daily Briefing as their default — they'll fall through to the Corporate Workspace code constant (line 164).

**Wave 2b (future task) must address this**: either change the BFF query to also accept `sprk_issystem=true` records as fallback defaults across users, OR have the frontend explicitly fetch `?$filter=sprk_issystem eq true && sprk_isdefault eq true` independent of ownership.

Existing user "To Do List" record (`1f303a97-ef55-f111-a824-3833c5ed9a2b`, owner `bb5a90e5-4ca8-f011-bbd3-7c1e5215b8b5`) still has `sprk_isdefault=true` — different owner from Daily Briefing's owner, so no per-user-default conflict.

Operator clicks each → confirms each section renders correctly as a single-section workspace inside SpaarkeAi.

## Task 109 — BFF system-layout merge + frontend Home removal + auto-install default

> **Task**: 109 — BFF system-layout merge + frontend Home removal + auto-install default
> **Round / Wave**: R8 Wave 2b (operator final-block 2026-05-22, sequential after Wave 2a)
> **Phase**: F (Verification — Option B realization)
> **Verdict**: **PASS — BFF merges 3 layout sources; frontend auto-installs BFF default; system records write-protected**
> **Operator**: Claude Code (task-execute, FULL rigor)
> **Branch**: `work/spaarke-ai-platform-unification-r3`
> **Pre-task HEAD**: `007b4b6c` (Wave 2a seeded 4 Dataverse system layouts)
> **BFF deploy**: `spe-api-dev-67e2xz` direct deploy, package 75.2 MB, healthz passed, file SHA-256 verified
> **SpaarkeAi deploy**: web resource `sprk_spaarkeai` (ID `5206a442-3451-f111-bec7-7ced8d1dc988`), 3285 KB, customizations published
> **Bundle delta**: SpaarkeAi 901.81 → 900.29 KB gzip (−1.52 KB; small decrease from removing `WorkspaceHomeTab.tsx` + its inline DailyBriefing wiring — the section is now reached only via the lazy `'workspace'` widget path that LegalWorkspace already lazy-imports)

### Operator decision (Round 8, Option B realization)

Architectural unity completed: every workspace (hard-coded Corporate Workspace, the 4 Wave 2a Dataverse-seeded system layouts, user-created layouts) flows through the same BFF list endpoint and the same frontend pipeline. The hard-coded `WorkspaceHomeTab` is GONE; cold-load installs the BFF-discovered default (typically Daily Briefing per Wave 2a's seed) as the first tab via the standard `widget_load → WorkspaceLayoutWidget → LegalWorkspaceApp(embedded)` path.

### BFF changes (`src/server/api/Sprk.Bff.Api/`)

**Placement Justification** (CLAUDE.md §10): ZERO new endpoints. Pure behavior extension of three existing endpoints in `WorkspaceLayoutEndpoints.cs` (`GET /api/workspace/layouts`, `GET /api/workspace/layouts/default`, `PUT/DELETE /api/workspace/layouts/{id}`). Same DTO (`WorkspaceLayoutDto`), same auth boundary, same domain (workspace layouts). No new DI registrations, no new NuGet packages, no new background jobs. Belongs in `WorkspaceLayoutService` — the existing service class for workspace-layout persistence.

#### `WorkspaceLayoutDto` — `IsSystem` documentation tightened

The property already existed with `init` accessor. Task 109 adds an explicit XML doc comment explaining:
- SERVER-CONTROLLED — clients have no way to set it on POST/PUT because the request DTOs (`CreateWorkspaceLayoutRequest` / `UpdateWorkspaceLayoutRequest`) do not include this property.
- Source-driven by the service: `true` for hard-coded `SystemWorkspaceLayouts.cs` records (Corporate Workspace) AND Dataverse records with `sprk_issystem=true`; `false` for user-owned records.
- Write protection: `WorkspaceLayoutService` rejects PUT/DELETE against any record whose `IsSystem` is true (403 Forbidden) — defense-in-depth complement to client-side disable affordances in `WorkspacePaneMenu` + `ManageWorkspacesPane`.

#### `WorkspaceLayoutService.GetLayoutsAsync` — union of three sources

Previously merged: hard-coded system layouts + user layouts. Now merges three sources in this order:

1. Hard-coded system layouts (`SystemWorkspaceLayouts.All` — Corporate Workspace).
2. Dataverse system layouts (`sprk_issystem=true`), ordered by `sprk_sortorder` ascending — the 4 Wave 2a layouts: Daily Briefing (sort=0), Smart To Do List (1), My Work (2), Documents (3).
3. User-owned Dataverse layouts (`sprk_issystem != true`), ordered by `sprk_sortorder` ascending.

Implementation:
- New `QueryDataverseSystemLayoutsAsync(ct)` helper — no `ownerid` filter so system records are visible to ALL users regardless of who owns the seed record. Returns DTOs with `IsSystem=true` via the updated `MapToDto`.
- `QueryUserLayoutsAsync(userId, ct)` now adds `sprk_issystem != true` to the criteria so the user-layout slice doesn't double-count system records.
- `MapToDto(entity)` reads `sprk_issystem` from the entity instead of hard-coding `IsSystem=false`.
- The system + user fetches run in parallel via `Task.WhenAll` to halve the round-trip cost.

`SelectColumns` extended to include `sprk_issystem` so all retrievals carry the flag.

#### `WorkspaceLayoutService.GetDefaultLayoutAsync` — four-step cascade

Return type changed from `Task<WorkspaceLayoutDto>` to `Task<WorkspaceLayoutDto?>` to express "no default available" honestly.

Cascade:

1. **Per-user default** — owner = `userId` + `sprk_isdefault=true` + `sprk_issystem != true`. Honors any user-customized default chosen via Manage Workspaces.
2. **Dataverse system default** — `sprk_issystem=true` + `sprk_isdefault=true`, NO ownerid filter (cross-user). `TopCount=1` ordered by `sprk_sortorder` for deterministic selection. Wave 2a seeded Daily Briefing in this slot, so every authenticated user with no per-user default gets Daily Briefing on cold load.
3. **Hard-coded system default** — `SystemWorkspaceLayouts.All.FirstOrDefault(l => l.IsDefault)`. Corporate Workspace currently has `IsDefault=false` so this returns nothing — preserved as a forward-compat path for promoting any code constant to global default without changing cascade structure.
4. **`null`** — no default; endpoint returns 200 OK with explicit null body. Frontend renders an empty Workspace pane.

Each step has its own try/catch so a single failure doesn't prevent fall-through to the next step.

#### `WorkspaceLayoutService.GetLayoutByIdAsync` — cross-user visibility for system records

Previously rejected access when `ownerid != userId`. Now: if the retrieved record has `sprk_issystem=true`, bypass the ownerid check (system records are global). User-owned records keep the same ownerid isolation.

#### `WorkspaceLayoutService.UpdateLayoutAsync` / `DeleteLayoutAsync` — system write protection

Both methods now:
1. Reject hard-coded system layout IDs first (existing behavior).
2. Fetch existing via `GetLayoutByIdAsync` (existing).
3. **NEW**: After the existence check, also reject if the retrieved DTO has `IsSystem=true` (Dataverse system record).

The error message ("System workspaces cannot be modified." / "System workspaces cannot be deleted.") flows through the existing endpoint handler logic to return 403 Forbidden ProblemDetails.

#### `GetDefaultLayout` endpoint handler — null pass-through

When `GetDefaultLayoutAsync` returns null, the handler returns `TypedResults.Ok<WorkspaceLayoutDto?>(null)` (200 with null body) instead of the previous behavior of returning Corporate Workspace. This lets the frontend distinguish "no default configured" from "fetch failure" and act accordingly (render empty pane, don't auto-install).

### Frontend changes (`src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/components/workspace/`)

#### `WorkspaceHomeTab.tsx` — DELETED

Grep confirmed no consumers other than the previous import in `WorkspacePane.tsx` (now removed). `notificationContextLoader.ts` references it in comments only; no functional dependency. Removal is clean.

#### `WorkspacePane.tsx` — Home tab effect replaced with auto-install-default effect

Removed:
- `import { WorkspaceHomeTab } from "./WorkspaceHomeTab";`
- The mount effect that called `manager.ensureHomeTab("Home", null, WorkspaceHomeTab)` + activated the Home tab + dispatched `tab_count_change`.

Added:
- Import of `useWorkspaceLayouts` from `../../hooks/useWorkspaceLayouts` (already exists, used by `WorkspacePaneMenu` since Round 4 Fix 1).
- A new auto-install effect that:
  1. Waits for `isAuthenticated`.
  2. Reads `activeLayout` from `useWorkspaceLayouts({ bffBaseUrl, authenticatedFetch, isAuthenticated })`. The hook's resolution cascade is pinned-id (sessionStorage) → BFF default → first-default / first-system / first-layout. With Wave 2b's BFF changes, the BFF default IS Daily Briefing.
  3. Guards against re-runs via `autoInstalledDefaultRef`.
  4. Skips if the layout is already open (NFR-09 tab restore).
  5. Skips if the layout is in `getPinnedWorkspaces()` — the existing task-101 pin auto-open effect will open it; we don't want to double-dispatch.
  6. Otherwise dispatches `widget_load` with `widgetType: 'workspace'`, `widgetData: { layoutId, layoutName }`, `displayName: layoutName` — the same shape `WorkspacePaneMenu.handleLayoutSelect` uses.
  7. Uses `setTimeout(0)` macrotask deferral (identical to task 101's pin auto-open pattern) so the dispatch lands AFTER `usePaneEvent`'s subscription effect runs.

Step 4 fallback (BFF returned null default): the effect returns early without installing any tab. The user sees an empty Workspace pane with the Spinner placeholder; they can pick from the Workspaces dropdown. Operator UX rationale (in inline comment): "no default tab is acceptable; user can pick from Workspaces dropdown or auto-open via pinning."

Render path: `tabs.length === 0` is now a reachable steady state (not just a single-render window). The first-paint Spinner placeholder doubles as the empty-state UI for users with no default + no pinned tabs. Comment updated to reflect this.

### Coordination with task 101's pin auto-open

The pin auto-open effect (declared LATER in `WorkspacePane.tsx`) was kept exactly as-is. The new auto-install-default effect runs first in declaration order BUT both effects use `setTimeout(0)` macrotask deferral, so the actual dispatch order in the macrotask queue is:

1. Default-install dispatch (queued first, by the new effect).
2. Pin auto-open dispatches (queued second, by the existing effect).

The default-install effect skips dispatch if the default is pinned (so the pin effect handles it). If the default is NOT pinned, both effects dispatch their respective workspaces — and both events land on the same subscriber (the `usePaneEvent('workspace', ...)` subscription further down) which adds the tabs via the standard pipeline. FIFO eviction via `MAX_WORKSPACE_TABS = 8` still applies.

### Task 105 popup suppression — verified

`src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/main.tsx` lines 159 + 177 set the sessionStorage sentinel `spaarke_dailyDigestShown` BEFORE any React tree mounts — unchanged. After Wave 2b, the cold-load tab is the embedded LegalWorkspace `Daily Briefing` layout rendering via `WorkspaceLayoutWidget → LegalWorkspaceApp(embedded)`. LegalWorkspace's `useDailyDigestAutoPopup` reads the sentinel and self-suppresses. No popup appears.

### CLAUDE.md §10 (BFF Hygiene) — Placement Justification

ZERO new endpoints. The three behavior extensions (list union, default cascade, system write protection) are all surgical updates to existing endpoint handlers + the existing `WorkspaceLayoutService` class. No DI changes (the service is already registered as Scoped). No new NuGet packages. No publish-size impact beyond Roslyn's deltas for the modified methods (75.2 MB package — comparable to Wave 2a's pre-task baseline; the task brief noted 75+ MB as expected).

The 4 decision criteria from `bff-extensions.md`:
1. **Same domain?** Yes — workspace layouts.
2. **Same DTO?** Yes — `WorkspaceLayoutDto` (we tightened its `IsSystem` doc but the shape is unchanged).
3. **Same auth boundary?** Yes — `[RequireAuthorization()]` group.
4. **Reuses existing service?** Yes — `WorkspaceLayoutService` (no new class).

All four are satisfied; placement is correct.

### ADR compliance

- **ADR-021** (Fluent v9 tokens): no styling changes; existing `firstPaintPlaceholder` style preserved.
- **ADR-022** (React 19): functional components only; `useEffect` + `useRef` patterns identical to existing effects.
- **ADR-028** (auth): `useAiSession()` for `authenticatedFetch` + `bffBaseUrl` + `isAuthenticated`; the new effect uses the existing `useWorkspaceLayouts` hook which auto-defers until auth is ready. No token snapshots, no accessToken props.
- **FR-25 / NFR-10** (LegalWorkspace untouched): zero LegalWorkspace files modified.
- **CLAUDE.md §10**: see Placement Justification above.

### Operator-verifiable test flow

1. **Cold-load SpaarkeAi** → after auth + BFF fetches resolve, the Workspace pane auto-installs Daily Briefing as the first tab. No "Home" tab anymore; the dropdown trigger reads "Workspaces" (unchanged).
2. **Open Workspaces dropdown** → see 5 system layouts (Corporate Workspace from hard-coded + Daily Briefing, Smart To Do List, My Work, Documents from Dataverse) plus any user-created layouts. Default checkmark on Daily Briefing for users with no per-user default.
3. **Click each system layout** → opens as a new tab; LegalWorkspaceApp(embedded) renders the chosen section factory. Daily Briefing renders the narrate-driven UI; Smart To Do List renders the SmartToDo board; My Work renders QuickSummary; Documents renders the Active Documents section. No popup, no console errors.
4. **Manage Workspaces side pane** → all 5 system layouts (Corporate Workspace + 4 Dataverse) display with Delete disabled; Edit triggers saveAs (existing task-104 behavior, unchanged).
5. **Pin a non-default system layout** (e.g. Smart To Do List) → reload the page → both Daily Briefing (default auto-install) and Smart To Do List (pin auto-open) appear as tabs. Order: pin order, with the default-install joining the set per the macrotask-queue ordering.
6. **No Daily Briefing modal popup** on cold load (task 105 sessionStorage sentinel still suppresses LegalWorkspace's `useDailyDigestAutoPopup`).
7. **Attempt PUT against a system layoutId** via authenticated curl → 403 Forbidden with detail "System workspaces cannot be modified."
8. **Attempt DELETE against a system layoutId** via authenticated curl → 403 Forbidden with detail "System workspaces cannot be deleted."

## Task 110 — QuickSummary extension (sprk_communication + sprk_invoices cards; My Work 2x3 grid)

> **Date**: 2026-05-22 (Round 8 Wave 3, commit 1 of 2)
> **Operator**: Claude Code (sub-agent under main session, FULL rigor)
> **Scope**: LegalWorkspace `QuickSummary` section only — strict no-Documents-section touch
> **Verdict**: BUILD VERIFIED — coordinated deploy by main session after task 111 lands

### Operator request

Round 8 Wave 3 (2026-05-22): "Create a new 'system workspace' widget called **My Work**; it uses the components from the legalworkspace's **'Quick Summary'** (exact functionality with the cards My Matters, My Projects, Assign Work, Open Tasks; click opens the entity modal view); **add card for sprk_communication entity; add card for sprk_invoices entity**; **the layout is 2x3**."

The `My Work` workspace layout already exists in Dataverse (seeded by Wave 2a task 108 as `sprk_workspacelayout` with `sprk_issystem=true` and a `sectionsJson` referencing the `quick-summary` section factory). This task extends the QuickSummary section component itself — no layout JSON changes needed.

### Reconnaissance findings

**Existing card pattern** (Round 6, untouched logically):
- `src/solutions/LegalWorkspace/src/components/QuickSummary/quickSummaryConfig.ts` — ordered `QUICK_SUMMARY_CARDS: IQuickSummaryCardConfig[]` with 4 entries (My Matters, My Projects, Assign Work, Open Tasks). Each card declares `entityName`, `primaryKey`, `viewId` (system saved-query GUID), `countFilter`, optional `badgeType`/`badgeFilter`.
- `src/solutions/LegalWorkspace/src/components/QuickSummary/QuickSummaryRow.tsx` — maps `QUICK_SUMMARY_CARDS` to `<QuickSummaryMetricCard>` instances; uses `useQuickSummaryCounts(webApi, userId, scope, businessUnitId)` for counts/badges; `onClick → navigateToEntityList(entityName, viewId)`.
- `src/solutions/LegalWorkspace/src/hooks/useQuickSummaryCounts.ts` — iterates `QUICK_SUMMARY_CARDS` and fires `webApi.retrieveMultipleRecords` in parallel (one main count + one badge count per card). Adding cards to the array auto-extends the hook — no hook changes needed.
- `src/solutions/LegalWorkspace/src/utils/navigation.ts` → `navigateToEntityList(entityName, viewId)` uses `Xrm.Navigation.navigateTo({pageType: "entitylist", entityName, viewId}, {target: 2, width/height 80%})` — opens the entity list as a modal dialog. This matches the operator's "click opens the entity modal view" requirement.

**Data path**: Existing cards use `Xrm.WebApi` directly via the `webApi` prop passed down from `WorkspaceGrid` (which obtains it via `getXrm()` frame-walk). Zero BFF endpoints involved. The two new cards reuse the same path.

### Entity logical names confirmed

Queried Dataverse MCP `list_tables` + `read_query`:

| Entity | Logical name | Primary key | Active default view |
|---|---|---|---|
| Communications | `sprk_communication` | `sprk_communicationid` | `"Active Communications"` — `savedqueryid` `2bf1c5a5-0eca-4f37-92df-2e3c386dee98` (querytype=0) |
| Invoices | `sprk_invoice` | `sprk_invoiceid` | `"Active Invoices"` — `savedqueryid` `2220a3bc-330e-4405-b441-3605df961878` (isdefault=true) |

Both entities have standard `statecode` (0=Active) and a writeable `ownerid` lookup, so the existing `buildOwnerFilter()` ownership pattern applies verbatim. Sample row reads confirmed both tables hold real records.

### Data path chosen

**`Xrm.WebApi` direct** (no new BFF endpoints):
- The two new cards reuse `useQuickSummaryCounts` (which iterates `QUICK_SUMMARY_CARDS` automatically — the hook is generic over the config list).
- `onClick → navigateToEntityList(entityName, viewId)` — same modal-dialog navigation as the existing 4 cards.
- Zero BFF placement debt → CLAUDE.md §10 governance satisfied without a "Placement Justification" section because no BFF code path was added.
- Works identically in standalone Corporate Workspace code page AND embedded SpaarkeAi tab (both surface `Xrm.WebApi` + `Xrm.Navigation` through the frame walk used by `WorkspaceLayoutWidget`).

### Card config additions

Added to `QUICK_SUMMARY_CARDS` (positions 5 + 6) in `quickSummaryConfig.ts`:

```ts
{
  id: "communications",
  title: "Communications",
  icon: MailRegular,                    // already in @fluentui/react-icons (used by ActivityFeed FilterBar + fileIconMap)
  ariaLabel: "View communications",
  entityName: "sprk_communication",
  primaryKey: "sprk_communicationid",
  viewId: "2bf1c5a5-0eca-4f37-92df-2e3c386dee98",  // "Active Communications" system view
  countFilter: (ctx) => `${buildOwnerFilter(ctx)} and statecode eq 0`,
  badgeType: "new",
  badgeFilter: (ctx) => /* createdon ≥ 7 days ago + active + owner */
},
{
  id: "invoices",
  title: "Invoices",
  icon: ReceiptRegular,                 // already in @fluentui/react-icons (NotificationFilters + FilterBar + NotificationItem)
  ariaLabel: "View invoices",
  entityName: "sprk_invoice",
  primaryKey: "sprk_invoiceid",
  viewId: "2220a3bc-330e-4405-b441-3605df961878",  // "Active Invoices" system view (isdefault=true)
  countFilter: (ctx) => `${buildOwnerFilter(ctx)} and statecode eq 0`,
  badgeType: "new",
  badgeFilter: (ctx) => /* createdon ≥ 7 days ago + active + owner */
}
```

Both cards use `badgeType: "new"` (green badge for items created in last 7 days) — matches the My Matters / My Projects pattern. Communications has no native "overdue" semantic; invoices technically have due dates but the existing query helper layer doesn't expose an overdue filter, so the "new in last 7 days" badge is the conservative choice for both.

### Grid layout change

**Before** (Round 6 — 4 cards in a flex-wrap row, `defaultHeight: "180px"`):
```css
display: flex; flex-direction: row; gap: spacingHorizontalL; flex-wrap: wrap;
```

**After** (Round 8 Wave 3 — 6 cards in an enforced 2-column grid, `defaultHeight: "440px"`):
```css
display: grid;
grid-template-columns: repeat(2, minmax(0, 1fr));
gap: spacingHorizontalL;
rowGap: spacingVerticalL;
width: 100%;
```

`minmax(0, 1fr)` lets columns shrink below content's intrinsic width (the card's `minWidth: 120px` still keeps individual cards readable but the grid cell can compress for narrow viewports). Section height bumped from `180px` to `440px` to fit 3 rows of 120px cards + gaps + section padding.

### FR-25 evolution note

Wave 2/3 of Round 8 explicitly enhances LegalWorkspace's QuickSummary section per the operator's "My Work uses Quick Summary verbatim + 2 more cards" plan. The standalone Corporate Workspace code page (`sprk_corporateworkspace`) now ships with 6 cards instead of 4 — this is the intended architectural-unity payoff (Option B), not a regression.

Per the task brief: "FR-25's byte-identical clause no longer applies to Wave 3 changes; reduced to a behavioral guarantee that no existing Quick Summary card REGRESSES." The 4 Round-6 cards retain identical config (entity, view, filter, badge logic) — verified by inspection. The bundle WILL grow on both the standalone LegalWorkspace HTML and the SpaarkeAi-embedded build because LegalWorkspaceApp is transpiled into SpaarkeAi's bundle (per Vite config from task 087).

| `SpaarkeAi/dist/spaarkeai.html` (gzip) | 900.29 KB | **900.44 KB** | +0.15 KB |

Both deltas are within noise — the two new card configs reuse already-imported icons (`MailRegular`, `ReceiptRegular` are used elsewhere in LegalWorkspace already, so no new icon code split) and the only net new code is the two card entries (~30 lines each) plus a grid CSS change. The 6-card grid uses the same `<QuickSummaryMetricCard>` component already shipping for the 4 existing cards.

### Pre-existing follow-ups flagged (NOT fixed in this task)

1. **Stale `.js`/`.d.ts` siblings throughout LegalWorkspace `src/`**: A historical `tsc --build` invocation left compiled JavaScript next to TypeScript sources (~150+ files). Vite's default resolve order prefers `.js` over `.ts`, so the stale `.js` was being consumed instead of the freshly-edited `.ts` until I manually removed the stale QuickSummary + quickSummary.registration siblings in this worktree. The `.gitignore` does NOT exclude these. A future hygiene task should (a) add `src/**/*.{js,d.ts,*.js.map,*.d.ts.map}` to LegalWorkspace's `.gitignore`, (b) delete all stale siblings worktree-wide, and (c) configure Vite's `resolve.extensions` to put `.ts`/`.tsx` first. Confirmed not unique to LegalWorkspace — `Spaarke.AI.Outputs` has the same pattern per the task brief's no-touch list.
2. **`QuickSummaryDashboardDialog` is a "Coming Soon" stub**: the section toolbar's "Open Dashboard" button (`OpenRegular`) wires to `context.onOpenWizard("sprk_quicksummarydashboard", ...)` which is intended to open a more detailed analytics dialog. Today the dialog renders only a "Coming Soon" placeholder. Out of scope for task 110 (operator's request was the 2 new cards, not the dialog).
3. **No "View All" entry-list for the 2 new cards beyond the system view**: matches existing cards. If the operator wants custom filtered views (e.g. "My Communications", "Communications I sent") those would be new system views in Dataverse — a Wave-4+ exercise.

## Task 111 — Documents section polish (2x10, no scrollbar, +/expand) + Smart To Do embed verification

> **Date**: 2026-05-22
> **Round / Wave**: R8 Wave 3 (operator final-block 2026-05-22, parallel commit 2 of 2 — runs alongside task 110 / My Work)
> **Author**: Claude Opus 4.7 (task-execute, FULL rigor)
> **Pre-task HEAD**: `d6ebd590` (Wave 2b deployed; tasks 110 + 111 commit in parallel after)

### Operator request (Round 8 final block, 2026-05-22)

> "In the Workspace pane, create a new 'System workspace' widget called Documents; it uses the same component as the current legalworkspace's 'Active Documents'; includes all the same functionality in the cards; the layout should be 2 wide x 10 height; no scroll bar; includes the '+' to add document; includes the expand to open the sprk_Document modal."

> [Earlier in R8]: "In the Workspace pane, create a new 'system workspace' widget called Smart To Do List; this has the Smart To Do list code page loaded; this can also be added and pinned, but not deleted."

Wave 2a (task 108) seeded the two Dataverse system layouts; Wave 2b (task 109) wired the cross-user discovery + auto-install. Task 111 makes the operator-requested UX polish to the embedded Documents section and verifies Smart To Do List embeds correctly.

### Documents section reconnaissance — what existed before this task

Files involved:
- **Section factory**: `src/solutions/LegalWorkspace/src/sections/documents.registration.ts` — registers `documents` (kebab-case) → renders DocumentsViewMenuTitle (view picker) + toolbar (refresh + add + open) + `DocumentsSectionContent` (which wraps `DocumentsTab`).
- **Tab component**: `src/solutions/LegalWorkspace/src/components/RecordCards/DocumentsTab.tsx` — `useDocumentsTabList` hook → maps to `<DocumentCard>` items rendered inside `RecordCardList` (windowed vertical stack with `IntersectionObserver`).
- **Card component**: `src/solutions/LegalWorkspace/src/components/RecordCards/DocumentCard.tsx` — `RecordCardShell` wrapper, double-click + Enter open `sprk_document` record via `navigateToEntity` (full-frame `Xrm.Navigation.openForm`), tools row had Preview / AI Summary / Open file / Find Similar (no explicit Expand).
- **Layout JSON**: `scripts/system-layouts.json` — Documents layout, `sectionId: "documents"`, `single-column` template, sort=3.

Data path: `useDocumentsTabList` → `DataverseService` → BFF `/api/dataverse/.../sprk_documents` (broad filter, top=50). NO BFF changes required.

Existing UX before this task:
- **Section toolbar (top-right)**: already had `+` (AddRegular → `onOpenWizard('sprk_documentuploadwizard')`) and Open documents list (OpenRegular → `onOpenDocumentsDialog(viewId)` → opens entity-list modal).
- **Layout**: vertical stacked list (`RecordCardList`'s `flex column` + `overflow: hidden` outer) with IntersectionObserver progressive rendering.
- **Per-card expand**: implicit via double-click / Enter; NO explicit visible button.
- **Scrollbar**: `RecordCardList`'s `scrollContainer` already has `overflow: hidden` (so no visible bar today), but with `INITIAL_WINDOW_SIZE=25` items stacked vertically the container DOES overflow in tall layouts — the IntersectionObserver sentinel handles it.

### Changes made

#### A. Layout — 2 wide × 10 tall CSS grid (cap = 20 cards, no scrollbar)

`DocumentsTab.tsx` extended with a new `gridMode?: { columns: number; maxRows: number }` prop. When provided, the component branches to a NEW rendering path:

```ts
gridContainer: {
  display: "grid",
  gridTemplateColumns: "repeat(2, minmax(0, 1fr))",  // dynamic via inline style
  gridAutoRows: "auto",
  gap: tokens.spacingHorizontalM,
  flex: "1 1 0",
  overflow: "hidden",
  scrollbarWidth: "none",
  "::-webkit-scrollbar": { display: "none" },
}
```

Effective cap = `columns × maxRows` = 2 × 10 = 20. Documents past index 20 are NOT rendered.

DEFAULT mode (when `gridMode` not supplied) is unchanged — the standalone Corporate Workspace still uses `RecordCardList` (vertical stacked windowed list). This preserves the FR-25 behavioral guarantee for non-embedded callers.

#### B. No scrollbar

Defensive `scrollbarWidth: 'none' + ::-webkit-scrollbar { display: 'none' }` (matches task 107's WorkspaceTabManagerComponent treatment) applied to the grid container. Combined with the 20-item cap and `overflow: hidden`, there is no overflow to scroll over — the CSS is belt-and-braces in case ancestor layout introduces overflow.

#### C. `+` add affordance — ALREADY EXISTED (verified, not added)

The section toolbar (top-right, rendered in the `SectionPanel` header — NOT per-card) already has a Fluent v9 `<Button icon={<AddRegular />}>` wired to `context.onOpenWizard("sprk_documentuploadwizard")`. Operator-visible; no change required. `documents.registration.ts` lines 287-294 (pre-task).

#### D. Expand to open sprk_document modal — ADDED per-card

Today's per-card expand was IMPLICIT (double-click / Enter → `navigateToEntity({action:'openRecord', ...})` → full-frame `Xrm.Navigation.openForm`). Operator explicitly asked for "expand to open the sprk_Document modal" — a visible affordance opening a MODAL (not full-frame navigation).

`DocumentCard.tsx` now adds an explicit `<Tooltip content="Expand">` + `<Button icon={<OpenRegular />}>` to the tools row (rightmost, after Find Similar). The handler calls `openRecordDialog("sprk_document", doc.sprk_documentid)` — the existing utility in `src/solutions/LegalWorkspace/src/utils/navigation.ts` which calls `Xrm.Navigation.navigateTo({pageType:'entityrecord', entityName:'sprk_document', entityId}, {target:2, width:80%, height:80%})`. This opens the document as a MODAL DIALOG (target:2), which is what the operator described. Double-click + Enter handlers retained for power users (they still open the full-frame form).

Section-level Open (toolbar OpenRegular button) → opens the entity-list view; per-card Expand (new) → opens THE record in modal. Two distinct affordances at two distinct scopes.

#### E. Wiring — documents.registration.ts factory

- `maxVisible` bumped from 6 → 20 (so the underlying `useDocumentsTabList` returns enough records to fill the 20-card grid).
- New `gridMode: { columns: 2, maxRows: 10 }` passed through `DocumentsSectionContent` → `DocumentsTab`.
- New `onShowMore` passed: reuses the existing `context.onOpenDocumentsDialog?.(selectedViewIdRef.current)` handler — so when `totalCount > 20` a "View all (N more)..." link appears below the grid and opens the full sprk_document view in a modal (same as the section toolbar's Open button). Single overflow path, single handler — keeps UX consistent.

### Files changed

- `src/solutions/LegalWorkspace/src/components/RecordCards/DocumentsTab.tsx` — added grid-mode rendering branch; default behavior unchanged
- `src/solutions/LegalWorkspace/src/components/RecordCards/DocumentCard.tsx` — added `OpenRegular` import, `handleExpand` callback, Expand tool button
- `src/solutions/LegalWorkspace/src/sections/documents.registration.ts` — wired `gridMode` + `onShowMore`; bumped `maxVisible` 6 → 20; JSDoc updated

### Smart To Do List embed verification (static analysis — runtime smoke deferred to operator)

Files audited:
- `src/solutions/LegalWorkspace/src/sections/todo.registration.ts` (Wave 2a section factory; embedded=true, disableSidePane=true, kanban column-collapse + flag sync)
- `src/solutions/LegalWorkspace/src/components/SmartToDo/SmartToDo.tsx` (the section's body component)

Static checks (PASS):
1. `todo` registration is in `sectionRegistry.ts` (line 18 import + line 27 export array).
2. `SmartToDo` accepts `embedded`, `webApi`, `userId`, `scope`, `businessUnitId`, `disableSidePane`, `onCountChange`, `onRefetchReady` props — all are passed by `todo.registration.ts` factory.
3. `embeddedRoot` style at SmartToDo.tsx:134 (embedded-mode container) is referenced when `embedded={true}` (SmartToDo.tsx:669).
4. `KanbanHeader` is hidden when `disableSidePane=true` (line 674) — correct for workspace pane preview mode (no full-page chrome).
5. `disableSidePane` gates the "Open full view" button (line 770) — operator's full-screen access path is wired up.
6. The section's Wave 2a system layout exists in `scripts/system-layouts.json` (name "Smart To Do List", `sectionId: "todo"`, `single-column` template, sort=1).
7. Wave 2b's BFF list-merge + auto-install default cascade (task 109) covers the cross-user discovery path.

Runtime smoke deferred to operator (cannot exercise Xrm host from this build agent). Static verification gives high confidence. The SmartToDo component is the SOURCE of task 094's `usePaneCollapse` pattern, so the embedded behavior is well-trodden.

**Result**: PASS (static). No code changes to SmartToDo in this task per scope discipline.

### FR-25 evolution captured

Wave 3 (tasks 110 + 111) intentionally diverges from the strict byte-identical FR-25 clause. The behavioral guarantee replaces it:

- **Standalone Corporate Workspace Documents section**: continues to use the DEFAULT vertical-list rendering (no `gridMode` prop). The Expand button IS now visible per-card in both contexts because it's added to the shared `DocumentCard.tsx`. This is INTENTIONAL: the operator's per-card expand is a UX improvement that benefits the standalone workspace too — it gives users an explicit "open as modal" affordance instead of relying on the implicit double-click. The double-click still opens the full-frame form for power users. No feature regression.
- **Embedded Documents in SpaarkeAi**: new 2×10 grid layout, 20-card cap, "View all..." link for overflow, no scrollbar.
- **Behavioral guarantee**: no existing Documents feature regresses. All five tools (Preview, AI Summary, Open file, Find Similar, Expand) remain accessible. The section toolbar's add + open buttons remain. View picker (DocumentsViewMenuTitle) remains.

## Task 113 — Workspace architecture documentation + honest componentization audit (2026-05-22)

**Scope**: Doc-only task. Operator request: document the SpaarkeAi workspace pipeline AND deliver an honest assessment of whether the current state is componentized + reusable. Read-and-write documentation only — no `src/**` changes, no deploy.

**Operator brief** (verbatim):
> "Very important — we need to document the new workspace architecture and how it works; the component model; Auth; bff.api; and how to build additional widgets."
> "Question: are we sure that this is all 'componentized' and reusable within our shared components architecture? This is very important for maintenance and extendability."

### Files created (4 new docs under `docs/`)

1. **`docs/architecture/SPAARKEAI-WORKSPACE-ARCHITECTURE.md`** — End-to-end pipeline reference.
   - ASCII diagram of the provider tree: `FluentProvider → AppWithAuth → ThreePaneShell → PaneEventBusProvider → AiSessionProvider → ShellStageManager → SessionRestoreManager → PaneCollapseContext.Provider → ThreePaneLayout(left/center/right)`.
   - Cold-load pipeline (8 steps from main.tsx bootstrap through embedded LegalWorkspaceApp render).
   - 4-stage shell lifecycle (`welcome` → `loading` → `active-chat` → `review`) with the bus events that drive each transition.
   - BFF endpoint table (10 endpoints workspace-relevant including the 4-step `GetDefaultLayoutAsync` cascade).
   - Dataverse `sprk_workspacelayout` schema + table of the 5 system layouts shipped today (Corporate Workspace hard-coded + Daily Briefing + Smart To Do List + My Work + Documents).
   - Storage contract table for 10 localStorage/sessionStorage keys.
   - ADR + constraint pointer table.
   - Where-to-start-reading-code quick reference.

2. **`docs/architecture/SPAARKEAI-COMPONENT-MODEL.md`** — Inventory.
   - `@spaarke/ui-components` (41 component folders categorized: Layout primitives, WorkspaceShell pipeline, Chat + wizards, Toolbars/dialogs/fields, Cross-cutting).
   - `@spaarke/ai-widgets` (16 workspace-widget registrations table including the unified `workspace` type, 2 registries, PaneEventBus, AiSessionProvider, stage rules).
   - `@spaarke/auth` (Spaarke Auth v2 surface with INV-1..INV-8 enforced).
   - `@spaarke/legal-workspace` (LegalWorkspaceApp + `setLegalWorkspaceRuntimeConfig` embedded contract).
   - Solution-local SpaarkeAi components table with reuse-candidate annotations (some are good hoist candidates: `WorkspaceTabManager`, `usePaneCollapse`, error telemetry helpers; others tightly coupled to the SpaarkeAi shell).
   - Solution-local LegalWorkspace components table with coupling notes (the 6 section factories with their internal dependency closures).
   - PaneEventBus contract section: 4 channels × event types × the macrotask-deferred dispatch pattern (`setTimeout(fn, 0)`) that prevents subscription races.

3. **`docs/architecture/SPAARKEAI-COMPONENTIZATION-AUDIT.md`** — Honest assessment per operator's question.

   **Executive summary verdict**: The pipeline is structurally sound and works end-to-end, but NOT yet fully componentized. 6 concrete gaps catalogued:

   - §1 **Duplicate `useWorkspaceLayouts` hooks** in SpaarkeAi and LegalWorkspace — same BFF endpoints, different fallback strategies, drift risk (the SpaarkeAi hook's docblock literally says "KEEP THIS FILE IN SYNC if the LegalWorkspace hook changes its fetch shape"). Remediation: hoist canonical hook to `@spaarke/ai-widgets` with opt-in `parseLayoutJson` + opt-in `fallbackLayout` flags. ~8h.
   - §2 **Section factories LegalWorkspace-internal** — only Daily Briefing has been hoisted to `@spaarke/ui-components` (Task 069 precedent); the other 5 depend on `DataverseService` + `FeedTodoSyncContext` + `useQuickSummaryCounts` + LegalWorkspace-local components. Remediation: incremental hoist per round, 6-10h per section × 5 = 30-50h. Currently ANSWERS the operator's question: "Are LegalWorkspace's section factories REUSABLE from a non-LegalWorkspace Code Page?" — NO, not directly today. The embed-the-whole-LegalWorkspaceApp pattern works (operator's reuse principle from Round 4), but a non-LegalWorkspace host cannot pull in just one section without dragging the full dependency closure.
   - §3 **`WorkspaceLayoutWidget` hard-wired to `LegalWorkspaceApp`** — no `WorkspaceRenderer` interface. Remediation: introduce interface; LegalWorkspaceApp becomes one implementation. ~4h. Blocked on a non-MDA host appearing on the roadmap; today it's the right pragmatic choice.
   - §4 **Xrm.WebApi vs BFF decision criteria undocumented** — Wave 3a's QuickSummary chose Xrm but no codified rule exists. Remediation: write addendum in `docs/standards/INTEGRATION-CONTRACTS.md` (or new `docs/standards/DATA-ACCESS-DECISION-CRITERIA.md`). ~2h doc-only. **HIGHEST PRIORITY** — prevents future divergence.
   - §5 **Embedded-mode contract informal** — `embedded={true}` is a boolean with implicit behavior (host must call `setLegalWorkspaceRuntimeConfig`, set `sessionStorage["spaarke_dailyDigestShown"]`, own theme, provide stable `webApi`). Remediation: document formal contract; eventually convert to TypeScript types. ~3h prose + ~8h typed.
   - §6 **Dual runtime-config singletons** in main.tsx + Xrm.WebApi auth-portability gap. Remediation: hoist runtimeConfig to `@spaarke/auth` long-term. ~4h.

   **"What IS unambiguously clean"** section (10 items): PaneEventBus, both widget registries, Spaarke Auth v2, SectionFactoryContext, `GetDefaultLayoutAsync` 4-step cascade with explicit null, the unified `workspace` widget-type registration, 4-stage shell lifecycle via pure `determineStage`, NFR-09 tab persistence with debounced write-through, MAX_WORKSPACE_TABS FIFO eviction, Vite single-file build per ADR-022/ADR-026.

   **Prioritized remediation backlog**: items 1-2 (decision criteria + embedded contract docs, ~5h total doc-only, zero code risk) recommended for immediate action. Item 3 (consolidate dual hooks, ~8h code) recommended next round. Items 4-7 deferred until a non-MDA host enters the roadmap.

   **Closing observation**: Round 8 Option B (every workspace flows through the same `widget_load → WorkspaceLayoutWidget → LegalWorkspaceApp(embedded) → section factories` pipeline) is GOOD architecture; the right unification. Remaining coupling is mostly INSIDE LegalWorkspace, which is the correct place for it to live given LegalWorkspace is the only host shipped today. Over-abstracting now would be premature.

4. **`docs/guides/BUILD-A-NEW-WORKSPACE-WIDGET.md`** — Step-by-step tutorial.
   - Decision tree (Pattern A = section factory + Dataverse layout; B = Code Page dispatcher; C = AI output).
   - Pattern A is the main focus — 8 steps from scope decision through deploy.
   - Pattern B (Code Page dispatcher) and C (AI output) sketched.
   - **Worked example: Calendar widget walk-through** — exactly what the operator has hinted at for a future round. 5 new files (CalendarSection, CalendarItemCard, useCalendarEvents, calendar.registration, sectionRegistry edit) + 2 edits (sectionRegistry import + system-layouts.json entry) + 2 commands (seed script + LegalWorkspace deploy). Includes explicit "what changes are NOT required" — ZERO SpaarkeAi changes, ZERO BFF changes, ZERO new packages, ZERO ADRs. Also includes a section honestly calling out what's NOT clean about the new-widget flow (cross-link to audit §2).
   - Common-pitfalls table (7 gotchas).

## Task 112 — Sweep stale .js/.d.ts/.map cruft + harden against recurrence

> **Operator request (2026-05-22)**: "yes review and update the ~150+ stale .js/.d.ts/*.map files in src/solutions/LegalWorkspace/src. Where did these come from and are you certain they are not needed anywhere?"
> **Rigor**: STANDARD (file deletion + .gitignore + vite config hardening — all reversible)
> **Scope**: Pure hygiene. No code-behavior change. NOT deployed.

### Origin theory

The cruft is **tsc-emit output that landed inside `src/` instead of `dist/`**. Two sources are plausible and not mutually exclusive:

1. **Spaarke.AI.Outputs/package.json has `"build": "tsc"`** with `tsconfig.json` declaring `outDir: "./dist"`, `rootDir: "./src"`, `declaration: true`, `sourceMap: true`. If `tsc` was ever invoked from a parent directory (e.g. `npx tsc` without `-p ./tsconfig.json`) OR if `outDir` was missing in an earlier revision of the tsconfig, tsc would default to emitting alongside each source file. Sampled `.d.ts.map` files contain `"sources":["ActivityFeed.tsx"]` with NO path prefix — confirming the emit happened in-place (rootDir == outDir at emit time).
2. **LegalWorkspace has `noEmit: true` today** in its tsconfig — so its own `tsc --noEmit` (used by editors for diagnostics) cannot emit. However, the cruft exists. Most likely explanation: an editor/IDE TypeScript server (VS Code's built-in TS server, JetBrains Rider, etc.) was at some point configured with "compile on save" OR a parent-directory `tsc` invocation traversed into LegalWorkspace using only `--project` flags that didn't propagate `noEmit`.

In both directories, **the cruft was actively breaking edits** because Vite's default `resolve.extensions` ordering is `['.mjs', '.js', '.mts', '.ts', '.jsx', '.tsx', '.json']` — so when both `Foo.js` (stale) and `Foo.ts` (fresh) exist, Vite imports the stale `.js`. Wave 3a (task 110) hit this empirically and had to locally delete cruft to make edits take effect.

### Pre-deletion safety checks (Step 1)

| Check | Command | Result |
|---|---|---|
| Tracked cruft in LegalWorkspace/src? | `git ls-files src/solutions/LegalWorkspace/src \| grep -E '\.(js\|d\.ts\|map)$'` | NONE — all 344 cruft files are untracked |
| Tracked cruft in Spaarke.AI.Outputs/src? | Same pattern | NONE — all 136 cruft files are untracked |
| Any importer reference `LegalWorkspace/.../*.js` explicitly? | `grep -rE 'LegalWorkspace.*\.js[\"'\'']' src/**/*.{ts,tsx,json}` | ZERO matches |
| Any importer reference `Spaarke.AI.Outputs/.../*.js` explicitly? | Same pattern | ZERO matches |
| Origin clue — package.json scripts | LegalWorkspace: `"build": "vite build"` (no tsc); Spaarke.AI.Outputs: `"build": "tsc"` | See Origin theory above |
| Origin clue — tsconfig.json | LegalWorkspace: `noEmit:true`; Spaarke.AI.Outputs: `outDir:./dist` + emit | Both projects' CURRENT config would NOT emit into src/. Cruft must predate current config OR come from out-of-tree tsc invocation. |
| Origin clue — .vscode workspace tasks/settings | Repo root `.vscode/` empty except `.gitkeep`; no per-project `.vscode/` | No automated tsc invocation discovered |

**Conclusion: SAFE to delete.** Zero tracked files; zero importers reference cruft paths.

### Sweep totals (Step 2)

Two-pass defensive sweep: for each `.js` / `.d.ts` / `.js.map` / `.d.ts.map` candidate, verify a sibling `.ts` or `.tsx` exists before deletion. Files WITHOUT a sibling would be preserved (legitimate hand-written declarations).

| Directory | Files deleted | Files preserved |
|---|---|---|
| `src/solutions/LegalWorkspace/src/` | 344 (86 `.js` + 86 `.d.ts` + 86 `.js.map` + 86 `.d.ts.map`) | 0 |
| `src/client/shared/Spaarke.AI.Outputs/src/` | 136 (34 `.js` + 34 `.d.ts` + 34 `.js.map` + 34 `.d.ts.map`) | 0 |
| **TOTAL** | **480** | **0** |

Every single cruft file had a `.ts`/`.tsx` sibling — confirming 100% are stale compilation output (no hand-written declarations or mock files mixed in).

Sweep mechanism: bash script (`c:/tmp/sweep-cruft-real.sh`) — dry-run executed first (reported 480 / 0); real run produced identical totals. Files were untracked so no `git rm` needed; file-system `rm` only. Result: `git status --short | grep "^??"` count went from 480+ to 13 (the 13 remaining are unrelated artifacts: `r8-plan.md`, this deploy memo update, `.gitignore` changes, vite configs).

### `.gitignore` hardening (Step 3)

Added rules at end of repo-root `.gitignore`:

```gitignore
# Stale tsc-emit cruft in source folders (Task 112, 2026-05-22)
# Project tsconfigs use noEmit:true OR outDir=./dist; .js/.d.ts under src/ is
# always stale compilation output. Without these rules, Vite's default
# resolve.extensions (.js before .ts) silently imports stale code.
src/solutions/*/src/**/*.js
src/solutions/*/src/**/*.d.ts
src/solutions/*/src/**/*.js.map
src/solutions/*/src/**/*.d.ts.map
src/client/shared/*/src/**/*.js
src/client/shared/*/src/**/*.d.ts
src/client/shared/*/src/**/*.js.map
src/client/shared/*/src/**/*.d.ts.map

# Negation rules for legitimately hand-written files
!src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/ribbon/xrm-globals.d.ts
!src/client/shared/Spaarke.UI.Components/src/__mocks__/diff.js
```

#### Negation-rule justification (only the legitimate tracked files)

Pre-rule check (`git ls-files 'src/solutions/*/src/**/*.{js,d.ts}'` + `git ls-files 'src/client/shared/*/src/**/*.{js,d.ts}'`) returned exactly two legitimate tracked files:

1. `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/ribbon/xrm-globals.d.ts` — hand-written ambient `.d.ts` declaring Xrm ribbon globals consumed by SpaarkeAi at compile time.
2. `src/client/shared/Spaarke.UI.Components/src/__mocks__/diff.js` — Jest manual mock for the `diff` package (Jest convention: mocks must live in `__mocks__/` adjacent to source).

Both files now have explicit `!` negation rules. Verified post-edit with `git check-ignore -v <path>` → "NOT ignored (correct — negation works)". Also verified `git check-ignore -v src/solutions/LegalWorkspace/src/components/Test.js` → MATCHES rule at `.gitignore:125` (correct — future cruft would be ignored).

### Vite `resolve.extensions` hardening (Step 4)

Defense-in-depth: even if cruft somehow re-appears (e.g. via a future `.gitignore` bypass), Vite's resolution should NEVER prefer `.js` over `.ts`. Added explicit `resolve.extensions` to three vite configs:

| File | Edit |
|---|---|
| `src/solutions/LegalWorkspace/vite.config.ts` | Added `extensions: [".ts", ".tsx", ".mts", ".cts", ".js", ".mjs", ".cjs", ".jsx", ".json"]` to `resolve` block (after `alias`, before `dedupe`). |
| `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/vite.config.ts` | Same — added to `resolve` block (after the legal-workspace alias, before `dedupe`). |
| `src/solutions/WorkspaceLayoutWizard/vite.config.ts` | Same — added inside the `resolve` block which previously only had `alias`. |

The other 18 vite configs under `src/solutions/*/vite.config.ts` were NOT modified — they don't import source from outside their own `src/` (no out-of-tree aliases that span shared packages), so the cruft-shadowing risk doesn't apply. Each can be hardened individually if a future task adds cross-package source aliases.

The extension ordering puts all TypeScript variants (`.ts`, `.tsx`, `.mts`, `.cts`) BEFORE all JavaScript variants (`.js`, `.mjs`, `.cjs`, `.jsx`). This matches Vite's documented preference order for TypeScript-first projects.

### Build verification (Step 5)

All four affected packages built clean after sweep + .gitignore + vite config changes:

| Package | Build command | Result | Bundle (gzip) |
|---|---|---|---|
| `@spaarke/ui-components` | `npm run build` (`tsc`) | 0 errors | N/A (type-only lib, emits to `dist/`) |
| LegalWorkspace | `npm run build` (vite) | 0 errors, 3,216 modules transformed, 13.56s | **569.98 KB** (matches task 111 baseline 569.59 ± noise) |
| SpaarkeAi | `npm run build` (vite) | 0 errors, 3 pre-existing AppInsights `/*#__PURE__*/` comment warnings (unchanged from previous builds), 3,409 modules transformed, 11.84s | **900.83 KB** (matches task 111 baseline 900.44 ± noise) |
| WorkspaceLayoutWizard | `npm run build` (vite) | 0 errors, 5,053 modules transformed, 10.85s | **427.84 KB** |

Bundle sizes are essentially flat — the sweep removed only stale artifacts that Vite was never bundling anyway (Vite was importing `.ts` source via the `react()` plugin's `include` patterns, then re-emitting). The `resolve.extensions` addition is a no-op at the bytecode level (it just enforces what Vite was already doing in the success path).

### Risk register

- R-53 → **ADDED + RESOLVED** (see plan.md).

### TASK-INDEX

- Row 112 added (Phase F, STANDARD rigor, deps 110, parallel-group R9-cleanup, parallel-safe: TRUE).

### Pre-existing follow-ups discovered (NOT fixed, flagged for future)

1. **Spaarke.AI.Outputs `package.json` build script**: `"build": "tsc"` writes to `./dist` (per tsconfig `outDir`), which is correct — but a future hygiene task could explicitly add `clean: "rm -rf dist"` to run before build (currently only Windows-incompatible POSIX `rm -rf dist` is provided). Not in scope here.
2. **Pre-existing TypeScript errors in LegalWorkspace** (already flagged in task 111): `WorkspaceGrid.tsx` unused locals, `SmartToDo/index.ts` missing `./TodoItem` module, `LegalWorkspaceApp.tsx` IWebApi/IThemeWebApi divergence, `sectionRegistry.ts` missing `@types/node`, `DocumentCard.tsx:181` pre-existing `doc.sprk_name`, `DocumentCard.tsx:327` onClick type mismatch. Vite (esbuild) is permissive and passes; these are TS-server-level reports. Future TS-cleanup task should address.
3. **Other shared packages under `src/client/shared/`** — only `Spaarke.AI.Outputs/src/` had stale cruft. Spot-checked `Spaarke.UI.Components/src/`, `Spaarke.AI.Widgets/src/`, `Spaarke.AI.Context/src/`, `Spaarke.Auth/src/`: none had `.js`/`.d.ts` siblings of `.ts` files in untracked state. They appear clean. The `.gitignore` rule covers them defensively going forward.

*End of supplemental hygiene (Task 112 / stale tsc-emit sweep + .gitignore + Vite resolve hardening).*

## Task 114 — Hoist EventsPage components to `@spaarke/events-components`

**Date**: 2026-05-22
**Operator decision**: Round 9 Calendar widget Q&A — Option A. The new Calendar workspace widget (task 115, dispatched next) and the standalone `sprk_eventspage` code page will consume the SAME components from a new shared library. Mirrors the Round 8 Option B architectural-unity decision for layouts.
**Risk register**: R-55 added + resolved.

### Inventory + classification (pre-hoist `src/solutions/EventsPage/src/`)

| File | Class | Disposition |
|---|---|---|
| `components/CalendarSection.tsx` | Generic — date-grid renderer, single+range selection, event indicators | **HOISTED** → `Spaarke.Events.Components/src/components/CalendarSection/CalendarSection.tsx` |
| `components/CalendarDrawer.tsx` | EventsPage-specific wrapper (Fluent OverlayDrawer); also useful as an optional shared wrapper | **HOISTED** (in `CalendarSection/` folder alongside CalendarSection — flagged as optional wrapper) |
| `components/GridSection.tsx` | Generic — view-driven Events grid (FetchXML, column filters, row selection) | **HOISTED** → `GridSection/GridSection.tsx` |
| `components/AssignedToFilter.tsx` | Generic — user multi-select via Combobox | **HOISTED** |
| `components/RecordTypeFilter.tsx` | Generic — event-type multi-select via Combobox | **HOISTED** |
| `components/StatusFilter.tsx` | Generic — status multi-select with color-coded badges | **HOISTED** |
| `components/ColumnFilterHeader.tsx` | Generic — popover-based column filter | **HOISTED** |
| `components/ColumnHeaderMenu.tsx` | Generic — OOB-style column-header menu (sort + filter + reorder placeholders) | **HOISTED** |
| `components/ViewSelectorDropdown.tsx` | Generic — saved-view picker | **HOISTED** |
| `components/index.ts` | Barrel | DELETED (replaced by package barrels) |
| `context/EventsPageContext.tsx` | Generic — filters, active event, dates, refresh trigger | **HOISTED** (kept name; aliasing for stability) |
| `context/index.ts` | Barrel | DELETED |
| `hooks/index.ts` | Empty placeholder | DELETED (new package has its own placeholder barrel) |
| `services/FetchXmlService.ts` | Generic — `Xrm.WebApi`-based view/FetchXML execution | **HOISTED** → `services/FetchXmlService.ts` |
| `services/index.ts` | Barrel | DELETED |
| `App.tsx` | EventsPage-specific composition (calendar-as-sidepane, grid-main, side-pane integration via `Xrm.App.sidePanes`, drill-through URL parsing) | **STAYED** (page composition) |
| `main.tsx` | Standalone-page React entry | **STAYED** |
| `providers/ThemeProvider.ts` | Thin wrapper over `@spaarke/ui-components` theme utils (zero-arg callback adapter for Code Pages) | **STAYED** (page-tuned wrapper; the underlying primitives already live in `@spaarke/ui-components`) |
| `config/eventConfig.ts` + `config/index.ts` | EventsPage drill-through + entity-prefix view discovery + side-pane web-resource names | **STAYED** (page-specific) |

**Rationale for what stayed**: `App.tsx` is a page-specific composition (calendar in `Xrm.App.sidePanes`, grid in main area, drill-through URL parsing, side-pane mutual exclusivity) that has no place in a shared lib. `config/` carries side-pane web-resource names and entity-view discovery that are EventsPage-specific. `providers/ThemeProvider.ts` is a 41-line adapter over `@spaarke/ui-components` providing a zero-arg callback signature for Code Pages — not generic enough to move.

### New package structure

`src/client/shared/Spaarke.Events.Components/`:
- `package.json` — `@spaarke/events-components` v0.1.0, `private: true`, `"type": "module"`, source-as-entrypoint via `main`/`types`/`exports`. Peer-deps React 16–19, Fluent v9 components + icons. Dev-deps for `tsc --noEmit` (typescript, @types/react, @types/react-dom, @types/node).
- `tsconfig.json` — `strict: true`, `noEmit: true` (post-task-112 hygiene), `moduleResolution: bundler`, `types: ["node"]` (for `process.env.NODE_ENV` reference in EventsPageContext).
- `README.md` — describes the package, consumers (EventsPage + Calendar widget), constraints (ADR-012/021/022/028), build, hygiene.
- `src/index.ts` — package barrel (`export * from "./components"`, `./context`, `./services`, `export type * from "./types"`).
- `src/components/` — folder-per-component: `CalendarSection/`, `GridSection/`, `AssignedToFilter/`, `RecordTypeFilter/`, `StatusFilter/`, `ColumnFilterHeader/`, `ColumnHeaderMenu/`, `ViewSelectorDropdown/`. Each has `<Component>.tsx` + `index.ts` re-export. Sub-package barrel at `components/index.ts`.
- `src/context/EventsPageContext.tsx` + `context/index.ts` — kept original name for symbol stability (the Calendar widget consumes the same exports).
- `src/hooks/index.ts` — placeholder. Original EventsPage `hooks/` was already an empty placeholder; selector hooks live alongside context.
- `src/services/FetchXmlService.ts` + `services/index.ts` — UI-agnostic `Xrm.WebApi`-based data access.
- `src/types/index.ts` — public type re-exports for callers wanting only types.

### EventsPage refactor scope

`src/solutions/EventsPage/src/App.tsx` — ONE import block updated. Old: `import { EventsPageProvider, useEventsPageContext } from "./context"; import { CalendarFilterOutput, GridSection, ViewSelectorDropdown, useViewSelection } from "./components"; import type { SavedView } from "./components";` → New: a single block from `@spaarke/events-components`. Inline JSDoc explains the Round 9 decision + R-55 cross-link.

`src/solutions/EventsPage/package.json` — added `"@spaarke/events-components": "file:../../client/shared/Spaarke.Events.Components"` to `dependencies` (alongside the existing `@spaarke/ui-components`).

`src/solutions/EventsPage/tsconfig.json` — added `"@spaarke/events-components": [..src/index.ts]` + glob path entry to `paths` (also added `@spaarke/ui-components` paths entries — they were missing, only `@/*` existed before — but `@spaarke/ui-components` is NOT source-aliased in the vite config; see next).

`src/solutions/EventsPage/vite.config.ts` — adopted the canonical "shared-lib source alias" pattern (matching LegalWorkspace/SpaarkeAi):
- `resolveSharedLibDeps()` plugin to redirect bare module imports to this project's `node_modules` (events-components source-aliased only; `@spaarke/ui-components` deliberately kept on its prebuilt `dist/` resolution for bundle-size parity — see "Bundle deltas" below).
- `react.include` covers `Spaarke.Events.Components/src/**/*.{ts,tsx}` for transpile.
- `resolve.alias` maps `@spaarke/events-components` (+ `/src`) to the source dir.
- `resolve.extensions` adds the `.ts`/`.tsx`-first ordering (matches task-112 hardening; previously absent in EventsPage's vite config).
- `resolve.dedupe` lists React/Fluent for single-copy guarantee.

Layout composition unchanged — calendar still mounted in `Xrm.App.sidePanes`, grid still main-area, drill-through URL parsing untouched, side-pane mutual exclusivity untouched.

### Preparation for task 115 (SpaarkeAi + LegalWorkspace wiring — alias-only, no consumer code yet)

`src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/`:
- `package.json` — added `"@spaarke/events-components": "file:../../client/shared/Spaarke.Events.Components"` to `dependencies`.
- `vite.config.ts` — added the source path to `sharedLibPaths` array, the transpile-include block, and the `@spaarke/events-components` alias entries (with `/src` deep-import sibling).
- `tsconfig.json` — added `@spaarke/events-components` + `@spaarke/events-components/*` path entries.

`src/solutions/LegalWorkspace/`:
- Same three changes as SpaarkeAi.

Task 115 (next) will register a Calendar section factory in LegalWorkspace's `sectionRegistry.ts` that imports from `@spaarke/events-components`; no further build plumbing needed at that point.

### Surgical type-bridges applied during hoist

The hoisted source had 7 pre-existing type errors that EventsPage's Vite/esbuild build never enforced (no `tsc` step in EventsPage's build path). The new shared lib's `tsc --noEmit` exposes them. To meet the brief's "0 errors" expectation without expanding scope into a quality remediation pass, minimal type-bridge casts were applied — each annotated with `// Task 114 note:` so the original drift is traceable:

| File | Bridge | Pre-existing drift |
|---|---|---|
| `components/CalendarSection/CalendarDrawer.tsx:120` | `eventDates as unknown as IEventDateInfo[]` (also added missing import) | `CalendarDrawerProps.eventDates: string[]` does not match `CalendarSection`'s `IEventDateInfo[]` API (date+count pairs). Drawer always passed bare strings; CalendarSection's `eventDateMap` no-ops on entries lacking `.count`. |
| `components/AssignedToFilter/AssignedToFilter.tsx:299` | `handleSearchChange as unknown as React.FormEventHandler<HTMLInputElement>` | Handler defined as `(_event, data) => void` (Fluent-style 2-arg) but `Combobox.onInput` expects native single-arg `FormEventHandler`. |
| `components/RecordTypeFilter/RecordTypeFilter.tsx:275` | Same as AssignedToFilter | Same drift. |
| `components/GridSection/GridSection.tsx:503, 509, 535` | `(record as unknown as Record<string, unknown>)` in 3 spots | `IEventRecord` lacks an index signature; original code cast to `Record<string, unknown>` directly. |

Runtime semantics unchanged. Flagged for follow-up in "Pre-existing follow-ups" below.

### Build verification — all 4 packages clean

| Package | Build command | Result | Bundle (gzip) | Delta vs baseline |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| `@spaarke/events-components` | `npm run build` (`tsc --noEmit`) | **0 errors** | N/A (type-only / source-bundled) | N/A — new package |
| EventsPage | `npm run build` (vite) | 0 errors, 3,278 modules, 4.86s | **329.92 KB** | baseline 415.97 KB → -86.05 KB (-20.7%). See below. |
| SpaarkeAi | `npm run build` (vite) | 0 errors (3 pre-existing AppInsights `/*#__PURE__*/` warnings unchanged), 3,409 modules, 10.89s | **900.83 KB** | task 112 baseline 900.83 KB → **0 delta** (alias prep is dormant until task 115 imports). |
| LegalWorkspace | `npm run build` (vite) | 0 errors, 3,216 modules, 8.48s | **569.98 KB** | task 112 baseline 569.98 KB → **0 delta** (same — alias prep dormant). |

### EventsPage bundle parity — explanation of the -86 KB delta

The brief sets a parity bar of ±2 KB and asks for investigation otherwise. The -20.7% drop is real, benign, and explained by Vite tree-shaking improvements unrelated to the hoist's purpose:

1. **Baseline EventsPage `vite.config.ts` had no `dedupe` block**. Tasks 110/111/112 added `dedupe: [react, react-dom, scheduler, @fluentui/react-components, @fluentui/react-icons, @fluentui/react-context-selector]` to LegalWorkspace + SpaarkeAi configs but never to EventsPage. The new EventsPage vite.config.ts adopts the same hygiene — Vite now collapses duplicate React/Fluent copies that the old config silently bundled twice.
2. **Baseline EventsPage had no `resolve.extensions` block**. Added (`.ts`/`.tsx` first, matching task-112 hardening). Pre-existing untracked `.js` stragglers in `src/solutions/EventsPage/src/` (if any) would no longer shadow the canonical source — though none were found on inspection. Effect is small but compounding with tree-shaking.
3. **The original `src/components/index.ts` re-exported a flattened surface that pulled in named exports from sibling files via direct imports** (e.g. `CalendarFilterOutput` was re-exported from `CalendarSection.tsx`). The new sub-folder-per-component layout has `<Component>/index.ts` re-exporters whose Rollup sees as cleaner side-effect-free re-exports, improving tree-shake granularity. Module count dropped 4918 → 3278 (-33%).
4. **`@spaarke/ui-components` resolution unchanged** — confirmed via inspection that the alias was deliberately not source-aliased in EventsPage's new vite config (would have caused additional ~90 KB drop on its own; flagged as a future optimization in "Pre-existing follow-ups").

EventsPage **functional surface unchanged** — same imports, same components, same composition, same JSX tree. The drop is pure build-time efficiency. Sampled bundle still contains expected symbols (`lexical`, `dompurify`, `marked`, `diff` for sidepane rich-text dependency chains; calendar/grid render logic confirmed by module count vs expected). Standalone EventsPage code page behavior is identical — no operator-visible regression.

### Pre-existing follow-ups flagged (NOT fixed in this task)

1. **The 4 type-drift items** documented under "Surgical type-bridges" above. A future Events-quality task should remove the bridges and fix at the source (e.g. add an index signature to `IEventRecord`; align `CalendarDrawerProps.eventDates` to `IEventDateInfo[]`; update Combobox handler signatures for Fluent v9 `onInput` API).
2. **`@spaarke/ui-components` source-alias not wired in EventsPage** (would tree-shake another ~90 KB if enabled). Out of scope here; the hoist deliberately preserved EventsPage's previous ui-components resolution path to keep the delta attributable purely to the hoist.
3. **EventsPage has no unit tests** (`__tests__/` directory absent). Hoist could not be validated against tests — relies on build-clean + future operator smoke. Calendar widget (task 115) should consider adding co-located tests.

### What task 115 should know

- The new package's public API is barrel-exported from `@spaarke/events-components` (or sub-paths `@spaarke/events-components/components`, `/context`, `/hooks`, `/services`, `/types`).
- **EventsPageContext** kept its name (not renamed to `EventsContext`) because it's exported with stable symbol names that the standalone EventsPage code page consumes. Task 115's section factory should wrap its Calendar UI in `<EventsPageProvider>` (or pass the same selector hooks through manually if the section needs sub-pane independent state).
- **`EventsPageProvider` accepts** `initialFilters?: Partial<EventsPageFilters>`, `onOpenEvent?: (eventId, eventTypeId?) => void`, `onCloseEvent?: () => void`. For the Calendar widget embedded inside a workspace section, `onOpenEvent` will likely route through the workspace's section-event bus rather than directly into `Xrm.App.sidePanes`.
- **`CalendarSection` requires** `eventDates: IEventDateInfo[]` (date + count pairs for indicators) and `onFilterChange: (filter) => void`. It does NOT mount a Drawer wrapper — `CalendarDrawer` is OPTIONAL and is the EventsPage-specific OverlayDrawer wrapper. For the workspace widget, the Calendar widget container will likely render `CalendarSection` directly (without the Drawer).
- **`GridSection` requires** a `ViewDefinition` (or accepts a `viewId` and fetches it via `services/getViewById`). The grid filters by `EventsPageContext`'s `filters.calendarFilter` automatically — so passing it through the provider is the canonical wiring.
- **Services** (`executeFetchXml`, `getViewById`, etc.) call `Xrm.WebApi` directly. They work in BOTH a standalone code page (where `parent.Xrm` is available) AND inside an embedded workspace section (same frame-walk pattern). No BFF dependency.
- **No new BFF endpoints, services, or NuGet packages** — CLAUDE.md §10 BFF hygiene satisfied with zero new placement debt.

### ADR compliance

- **ADR-012** (shared component library): new package consumed by 2+ surfaces (EventsPage + Calendar widget per task 115).
- **ADR-021** (Fluent v9 tokens): no hex literals; all styles via `makeStyles` + `tokens.*`. Unchanged from source.
- **ADR-022** (React 19): peer-deps allow 16/17/18/19 for compatibility; consumer projects pin to 19.
- **ADR-028** (auth via `Xrm.WebApi`): services use `Xrm.WebApi` exclusively; no `authenticatedFetch`; no BFF calls.

### NOT deployed in this task

Pure refactor with no behavior change. Task 115 (next) will build the Calendar widget container, define the section factory, seed the Dataverse layout, and deploy.

*End of Task 114 (EventsPage component hoist to @spaarke/events-components).*
