## Task 115 — Calendar workspace widget (5th Round-8 system layout) — 2026-05-22

### Overview

The 5th SpaarkeAi system workspace, "Calendar", ships. Surfaces all events +
tasks the user has access to via `CalendarWorkspaceWidget` from
`@spaarke/events-components` (hoisted in task 114), demonstrating the
architectural unity Round 9 (Option A) committed to: standalone EventsPage
(`sprk_eventspage`) and the SpaarkeAi Calendar workspace consume the SAME
Events components from a single source of truth.

### Files

**Created**
- `src/client/shared/Spaarke.Events.Components/src/widgets/CalendarWorkspaceWidget/CalendarWorkspaceWidget.tsx`
- `src/client/shared/Spaarke.Events.Components/src/widgets/CalendarWorkspaceWidget/index.ts`
- `src/client/shared/Spaarke.Events.Components/src/widgets/index.ts`
- `src/solutions/LegalWorkspace/src/sections/calendar.registration.ts`

**Modified**
- `src/client/shared/Spaarke.Events.Components/src/index.ts` — added `export * from "./widgets"`.
- `src/client/shared/Spaarke.Events.Components/package.json` — added `./widgets` entry to `exports` map.
- `src/solutions/LegalWorkspace/src/sectionRegistry.ts` — registered `calendarRegistration` (7 sections total).
- `src/solutions/LegalWorkspace/src/sections/index.ts` — barrel re-export.
- `scripts/system-layouts.json` — added 5th seed entry (`sectionId: "calendar"`, `sortOrder: 4`).

**NOT modified**
- Standalone `EventsPage/src/App.tsx` (its calendar-in-sidepane + grid-main composition stays).
- Any BFF code (CLAUDE.md §10: ZERO new endpoints).
- `CalendarSection` itself (shared component); composition over modification.

### Composition decisions

1. **3-month strip via single `<CalendarSection>` (not three instances).** Reading
   `CalendarSection.tsx` showed that the component already renders `current
   month + next 2 ahead` internally (lines 477-484, `monthsToShow` memo). The
   brief specified "Option 1: render `<CalendarSection>` three times" based
   on an assumed single-month component shape; the actual shape needs no
   wrapping for the 3-month requirement. **Divergence flagged**: the
   operator mockup external left/right "Navigate Months" arrows are NOT
   present. `CalendarSection.viewDate` is internal state, so adding
   external nav arrows requires either lifting `viewDate` to a prop on
   the shared component (breaks composition-over-modification) or
   duplicating CalendarSection logic in the widget. Deferred to a follow-up
   round.

2. **Date-range filter row built inline** (not a new shared component).
   Three Fluent v9 primitives: `Dropdown` (date field) + `Input type="date"`
   x 2 (From/To). Wires into `EventsPageContext` via `setCalendarFilter`
   with `type: "range" | "single"` and `dateFields: [field]` so
   `GridSection` filtering picks it up without any new context shape.

3. **Toolbar = full EventsPage parity.** 9 buttons mirroring
   `EventsCommandBar` from `src/solutions/EventsPage/src/App.tsx` lines
   1038-1132: New / Delete / Complete / Close / Cancel / On Hold / Archive
   / Refresh / Calendar. Handler bodies (bulk status updates, archive,
   delete) were partially duplicated into the widget (mirroring lines
   685-984 of EventsPage `App.tsx`) rather than extracted into the shared
   lib. Those handlers are tightly coupled to EventsPage standalone
   notification + dialog pattern and a wider extraction would have been
   scope creep. **Flagged**: future quality-task can extract a
   `useEventsBulkActions(selectedIds)` hook into `@spaarke/events-components`
   if standalone + widget drift becomes a maintenance burden.

4. **"Calendar" toolbar button** in standalone EventsPage opens/closes the
   `Xrm.App.sidePanes` Date Filter pane. In the embedded widget the
   calendar strip is permanently visible above the grid, so the Calendar
   toolbar button is mapped to "clear active date filter" — defensible
   mapping (the button still has meaning) and documented in source.

5. **Side-pane to modal seam.** Per operator decision (Round 9 Q&A 2026-05-22),
   `EventsPageProvider.onOpenEvent` callback routes through
   `Xrm.Navigation.navigateTo({pageType:"entityrecord",entityName,entityId},
   {target:2, width/height: 80%, position:1})` — modal at 80% x 80% —
   instead of `Xrm.App.sidePanes`. Mirrors the Documents Expand affordance
   from task 111. Consistent SpaarkeAi modal-detail UX across workspaces.

6. **Hidden scrollbar.** `scrollbar-width: none` + WebKit
   `::-webkit-scrollbar { display: none }` at root, matching task 107
   Workspace pane treatment.

## Task 117 — Default pane widths 25/50/25 percentage at first cold load

> **Task**: 117 — SpaarkeAi default pane widths 25/50/25 at first cold load
> **Phase**: F — Round 10 follow-up
> **Date**: 2026-05-22
> **Operator request (Round 10)**: "For the sprk ai initial load the default pane width distribution should be 25% / 50% / 25%."
> **Operator Q&A clarification**: "Percentage of viewport at first load; user resizes persist (Recommended). On a fresh session with no saved widths, compute 25%/50%/25% from the current viewport. Once the user drags a splitter, that absolute pixel width is persisted in sessionStorage and used on subsequent mounts."

### Problem statement

Before this task, ThreePaneLayout used fixed pixel defaults (340 left + 400 right + flex-1 center). On a typical 2000px viewport that distributes panes ~17/50/33, NOT the desired 25/50/25. The fix had to be surgical:

- ✅ First cold load (empty sessionStorage) → 25/50/25 of viewport
- ✅ After the user drags a splitter, the persisted pixel value wins
- ✅ Subsequent reloads honor the persisted pixel value (no override by frac)
- ✅ Existing minimum-width floors (240/240/320) still clamp the result
- ✅ Backwards compatible — any consumer not opting into the new frac props keeps legacy behavior

### Files modified

| File | Change |
|---|---|
| `src/client/shared/Spaarke.UI.Components/src/components/ThreePaneLayout/ThreePaneLayout.types.ts` | Added `defaultLeftWidthFrac?: number` and `defaultRightWidthFrac?: number` to `ThreePaneLayoutProps` (JSDoc-documented precedence) |
| `src/client/shared/Spaarke.UI.Components/src/components/ThreePaneLayout/useThreePaneLayout.ts` | Added matching options to `UseThreePaneLayoutOptions`; replaced `loadPersistedWidth` with `resolveInitialWidth` (three-tier precedence: stored > frac × `window.innerWidth` > legacy pixel); wired into `useState` lazy initializers |
| `src/client/shared/Spaarke.UI.Components/src/components/ThreePaneLayout/ThreePaneLayout.tsx` | Forwarded the two new props from component into the hook |
| `src/solutions/SpaarkeAi/src/components/shell/ThreePaneShell.tsx` | Passed `defaultLeftWidthFrac={0.25}` + `defaultRightWidthFrac={0.25}` to `<ThreePaneLayout>` alongside the existing pixel defaults (which now serve as the legacy fallback layer in the precedence chain) |

### API shape (Option A — confirmed)

Two new optional props on `ThreePaneLayoutProps`:

```ts
defaultLeftWidthFrac?: number;   // e.g. 0.25 for 25%
defaultRightWidthFrac?: number;
```

Backwards-compatible: omitting the props preserves the pre-task-117 `loadPersistedWidth` path verbatim.

### Precedence implementation (`resolveInitialWidth`)

```
1. sessionStorage stored pixel width (user-dragged value persists)
2. frac × window.innerWidth (NEW — percentage default)
3. defaultLeftWidthPx (legacy pixel default; also serves as SSR fallback)
```

`window.innerWidth` is used as the viewport reference because the layout's own bounding rect is not yet measurable at first mount (`containerRef` is populated post-mount). The SpaarkeAi shell fills the viewport, so this is an accurate proxy. The computed value is clamped to at least `min` (240/200/...) so narrow viewports still respect the minimum floor.

### SpaarkeAi vs LegalWorkspace call-site differentiation (FR-25)

- **SpaarkeAi** passes the new frac props → 25/50/25 on first cold load.
- **LegalWorkspace** does NOT consume `ThreePaneLayout` at all (confirmed via grep — no `ThreePaneLayout` imports anywhere under `src/solutions/LegalWorkspace/`). It uses `WorkspaceGrid`-based section rendering. FR-25 trivially preserved.
- Any future consumer that imports `@spaarke/ui-components.ThreePaneLayout` without passing the new frac props will continue to see the legacy pixel-default behavior.

### Build verification (Step 6)

All three packages clean:

| Package | Command | Result | Bundle (gzip) | Baseline | Δ |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| `@spaarke/ui-components` | `tsc` | ✅ 0 errors | n/a (library) | n/a | n/a |
| `SpaarkeAi` | `vite build` | ✅ 0 errors | **916.69 KB** | 916.60 KB (task 115) | +0.09 KB (trivial) |
| `LegalWorkspace` | `vite build` | ✅ 0 errors | **587.34 KB** | 587.31 KB (task 115) | +0.03 KB (source-map noise; LegalWorkspace does NOT consume ThreePaneLayout so no semantic change) |

The +0.09 KB delta on SpaarkeAi exactly matches the addition of two optional props + the three-branch `resolveInitialWidth` function (a few hundred bytes minified + gzipped — about right). The LegalWorkspace delta is purely module-hash variation; the underlying code is byte-identical relative to ThreePaneLayout.

### Smoke check (mental walkthrough)

The UI cannot be opened from here, but the expected behavior is:

| Scenario | Expected |
|---|---|
| Fresh session, viewport = 1600px | Left ≈ 400px (25%), Center ≈ 800px (50%), Right ≈ 400px (25%) |
| Fresh session, viewport = 800px | Left = 240px (clamped to min), Center = 320px (clamped to min), Right = 240px (clamped to min) — exactly fits |
| User drags left to 320px and reloads | Left = 320px (sessionStorage value wins over frac default) |
| User drags right to 500px and reloads | Right = 500px (sessionStorage value wins) |
| `sessionStorage.clear()` and reload | Returns to 25/50/25 of current viewport |
| LegalWorkspace standalone | UNCHANGED — does not consume ThreePaneLayout |


## Task 116 — Calendar widget polish (horizontal layout, responsive count, ◀ ▶ navigation, collapse, height) — 2026-05-22

**Wave**: R10 (parallel-safe with task 117 — different files)
**Branch**: `work/spaarke-ai-platform-unification-r3`
**Parent task**: 115 (Calendar workspace widget — initial vertical implementation)
**Operator feedback round**: Round 10 (2026-05-22 smoke)

### 1. Operator feedback addressed

1. **Horizontal calendar strip** (was vertical stacking) — operator: "The
   calendar horizontal not stacked vertical; showing the number of
   calendars based on the screen width (responsive)."
2. **Reduced strip height** so the grid below isn't pushed too low —
   operator: "Height (size) of calendar should allow the bottom grid to
   show more (currently too low in the workspace view port)."
3. **External ◀ ▶ arrow navigation** instead of internal scroll —
   operator: "Use arrows left and right to scroll calendars, not scroll
   bar."
4. **Unbounded month/year navigation** — operator: "Needs to show all
   months/years not just 2."
5. **Collapsible calendar strip** with persistence — operator: "Allow the
   CalendarSection to be collapsed; right side expand/collapse icon."
   Operator Q&A clarification: collapse target = **just the calendar
   strip** (date filter, toolbar, view selector, grid remain visible
   when collapsed).

### 2. Composition decisions

Task 115 flagged composition-over-modification as the posture for the
shared `CalendarSection` — external arrows would require lifting
`viewDate` to a prop. Operator's Round 10 feedback made the four
shared-component touch points load-bearing, so we extended
`CalendarSection` with **three optional, backwards-compatible props**:

| Prop | Default | Effect when omitted |
|---|---|---|
| `viewDate?: Date` | (internal state, `today`) | UNCONTROLLED — internal `setInternalViewDate` retained |
| `monthsToShow?: number` | `3` | Prior behavior (current + 2 ahead) |
| `layout?: 'vertical' \| 'horizontal'` | `'vertical'` | Prior CSS (`flex-direction: column; overflow-y: auto`) |

Standalone EventsPage's `CalendarDrawer` does NOT pass any of the new
props, so it renders byte-identically. The new horizontal layout uses a
separate `calendarContentHorizontal` style class (flex row, `gap: 16px`,
`overflow: hidden`) and each month container gets `monthContainerHorizontal`
(`flex: 1 1 0; min-width: 240px; margin-bottom: 0`) when layout === 'horizontal'.

### 3. CalendarWorkspaceWidget rewrite

**State now owned by the widget**:
- `viewDate` — initialized to `startOfMonth(new Date())`; unbounded (◀ /
  ▶ shift ±1 month via `addMonths`).
- `monthsToShow` — initialized to 2 (matches default 25/50/25 ~600px
  Workspace pane after task 117); overridden by `ResizeObserver` on the
  strip container ref. `computeMonthsForWidth()` maps width to count:
  - `< 380px` → 1 month
  - `< 720px` → 2 months
  - `< 1060px` → 3 months
  - `< 1400px` → 4 months
  - `≥ 1400px` → 5 months (capped — each month renders 42 day cells)
- `calendarCollapsed` — initialized from `localStorage["spaarke:calendar:collapsed"]`
  via try/catch-wrapped accessors (mirrors `pinnedWorkspaces.ts` task-092
  pattern; degrades silently on private browsing / quota / corrupt storage).

**Layout (when expanded)**:

```
+---------------------------------------------------------------+
| <  |  CalendarSection (horizontal, monthsToShow)  |  >  | ^/v |
+---------------------------------------------------------------+
```

- Outer `calendarRow` has `flex-shrink: 0; min-height: 280px` (one-month
  grid baseline) so the strip is bounded.
- Middle `calendarStrip` has `flex: 1 1 auto; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0`.
- ◀ / ▶ Buttons (`ChevronLeft/Right20Regular`) are `appearance="subtle"`,
  Tooltip-wrapped (label="Previous/Next month (Shift+click: jump by
  window)"), `aria-label`-tagged. **Step**: 1 month per click;
  **Shift+click**: jump by `monthsToShow` for power users.
- Collapse toggle (`ChevronUp20Regular` when expanded) lives in a
  bordered slot to the right of ▶ — same row.

**Layout (when collapsed)**:

```
+---------------------------------------------------------------+
| Calendar (collapsed)                                        v |
+---------------------------------------------------------------+
```

- The whole `calendarRow` is replaced by a slim `collapsedBar` (label +
  expand chevron). CalendarSection unmounts (state lives in widget — no
  re-mount cost beyond CSS).
- Grid container retains `flex: 1 1 auto; min-height: 320px`, so it
  expands to fill the freed vertical space.

### 4. New util module

Added `src/client/shared/Spaarke.Events.Components/src/utils/dateMath.ts`:
- `addMonths(date: Date, months: number): Date` — uses Date.setMonth;
  preserves day-of-month with natural JS roll-over (e.g. Jan 31 + 1mo →
  Mar 3) which is acceptable because the widget anchors via
  `startOfMonth(viewDate)` before computing the month list.
- `startOfMonth(date: Date): Date` — returns `new Date(year, month, 1)`.

**Why inline instead of `date-fns`**: events-components currently has
ZERO runtime dependencies beyond React + Fluent v9 (peer-deps only).
Adding date-fns would inflate bundle-size attribution and break the
clean baseline. Two trivial helpers don't justify a new peer.

Barrel updates:
- `src/utils/index.ts` (NEW) re-exports `./dateMath`.
- Top-level `src/index.ts` adds `export * from "./utils"`.
- `package.json` adds `"./utils": "./src/utils/index.ts"` exports entry.

### 5. Build verification

| Package | Result | Modules | Gzip | Baseline (task 115) | Delta |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| `@spaarke/events-components` | tsc clean | N/A | — | — | — |
| EventsPage (standalone) | Vite 0 errors | 3,283 | **330.24 KB** | 329.92 KB | **+0.32 KB** (near-zero — confirms backwards-compat) |
| LegalWorkspace | Vite 0 errors | 3,245 | **588.32 KB** | 587.31 KB | **+1.01 KB** (ResizeObserver + arrow nav + collapse state + util) |
| SpaarkeAi | Vite 0 errors | 3,438 | **917.48 KB** | 916.60 KB | **+0.88 KB** (same — alias-resolved from shared lib) |

3 pre-existing AppInsights `/*#__PURE__*/` warnings unchanged.

**EventsPage standalone parity**: +0.32 KB delta on a 329.92 KB baseline
is consistent with adding 3 optional prop slots to the typed component
surface (no runtime cost when omitted — `viewDate` prop is undefined,
internal state path retained byte-for-byte). EventsPage's
`CalendarDrawer.tsx` call site is unchanged.

### 6. Files changed

### 8. Operator smoke flow (verifiable steps)

1. Open SpaarkeAi → Workspaces dropdown → select **Calendar** workspace.
2. Confirm the calendar strip renders **horizontally** (months side-by-side,
   not stacked top-to-bottom).
3. Confirm month count adapts to width:
   - Default 25/50/25 layout (~600px Workspace pane) → **2 months**.
   - Collapse Context pane (or Assistant) so Workspace widens → **3-4
     months** appear automatically (no reload needed).
4. Click ◀ — calendar shifts left by **1 month**; verify can scroll back
   to **any past month/year** (e.g. 2020). Click ▶ to advance forward
   beyond the original "+2 ahead" cap.
5. **Shift+click** ◀ or ▶ — calendar jumps by the visible-window count
   (e.g. 2 months at default width).
6. Click the right-side **collapse chevron (^)** — strip disappears, slim
   "Calendar (collapsed)" bar remains; grid below expands to fill.
7. Reload the page — collapse state **persists** (localStorage).
8. Click the expand chevron (v) on the collapsed bar — strip re-appears
   with the same `viewDate` (state retained on widget level; CalendarSection
   re-mounts with the same `viewDate` prop).
9. Confirm internal scrollbar on the strip is **absent** — arrows are
   the only navigation.

  shape).
- (c) `CalendarDrawer`'s `eventDates: string[]` mismatch with
  `IEventDateInfo[]` API drift is unaffected by this task — bridged
  with existing cast at the call site.
- (d) Standalone EventsPage + standalone LegalWorkspace code pages NOT
  redeployed in this task — operator focus is SpaarkeAi.

### 10. ADR compliance

  preserved via optional props with prior-behavior defaults; EventsPage
  byte-identical (+0.32 KB delta is typed-surface-only). The horizontal
  layout + responsive count is shared-lib-resident, not widget-local —
  reusable by any future consumer.
- **ADR-021** (Fluent v9 tokens): all colors / spacing via `tokens.*`
  and `shorthands.*`. Zero hex / rgba literals introduced.
- **ADR-022** (React 19): `useState` lazy initializers (`viewDate`,
  `calendarCollapsed`), `useRef` for ResizeObserver target, `useCallback`

  disconnect. No React-16 fallbacks.
- **ADR-028** (auth via `Xrm.WebApi`): unchanged from task 115 — all
  Dataverse access flows through `Xrm.WebApi` exclusively. ZERO BFF

## Task 118 — Calendar widget Round 11 polish

**Date**: 2026-05-22
**Branch**: `work/spaarke-ai-platform-unification-r3`
**Resource GUID**: `5206a442-3451-f111-bec7-7ced8d1dc988`
**Bundle**: SpaarkeAi 917.85 KB gzip (vs 917.48 baseline = +0.37 KB).
EventsPage parity confirmed: 330.23 KB gzip (vs 330.24 = -0.01 KB,
within rounding).

### 1. Six operator refinements (Round 11)

#### Fix 1 — Collapse chevron moves to the filter row

The chevron previously sat at the right end of the calendar strip (inside
the strip row). It now lives at the right edge of the **filter row**
(Filter by Date Field, From, To, spacer, chevron). When collapsed,
the filter row remains fully interactive and continues to drive grid
filtering — only the calendar strip itself hides. The flex-spacer
right-justifies the chevron at any viewport width without media queries.

#### Fix 2 — New collapse icon

`ChevronUp20Regular` / `ChevronDown20Regular` are replaced with
`CaretUp24Regular` / `CaretDown24Regular`. The caret triangles are
visually distinct from the month-navigation chevrons and clearly
convey vertical collapse direction. Both confirmed present in the
installed `@fluentui/react-icons` version.

#### Fix 3 — Calendar header + separator removed

The internal CalendarSection rendered a header row with the calendar
icon, the text "Calendar", and a bottom border. In `layout='horizontal'`
mode (Calendar widget), this header is now suppressed entirely. The
selectionInfo banner and the footer (clear + version) are also
suppressed in horizontal mode because the widget owns those
affordances on its own toolbar / filter rows. The `layout='vertical'`
branch (EventsPage CalendarDrawer) is unchanged.

#### Fix 4 — Month grid spacing

`CalendarSection.calendarContentHorizontal` gap bumped from `16px`
to `tokens.spacingHorizontalXL` (~20px) on the column axis. Visual
breathing room between adjacent months without sacrificing the
visible month count at typical workspace widths. Vertical layout
retained `marginBottom: 16px` from `monthContainer`.

#### Fix 5 — Event-day highlight + click-to-filter

Investigation: CalendarSection already tracked `hasEvents` per day
and rendered a 4×4px dot at the bottom of the cell. At calendar-cell
density, the dot was easy to miss on SpaarkeAi's smaller embedded
view.

Added: a `dayWithEvents` Griffel style applied to in-month days that
have associated events. Tokens used: `colorBrandBackground2`,
`colorBrandForeground1`, `fontWeightSemibold`,
`colorBrandBackground2Hover`. Stacking priority: selected > in-range
> has-events > today > other-month base. Other-month days are not
tinted because they would compete visually. The original 4×4px dot
remains for stacking inside selected/in-range cells.

Controlled mode: `CalendarSection` gained two optional props (both
backwards-compat — omitting them preserves the prior internal
selection behavior used by EventsPage CalendarDrawer):

```ts
selectedDate?: Date | null;
onSelectDate?: (date: Date | null) => void;
```

When `onSelectDate` is provided, the parent owns the selection. Day
clicks emit through `onSelectDate` only; `onFilterChange` continues
to fire for Shift+click range selections and footer-clear.

Widget wiring: the Calendar widget owns `selectedDate: Date | null`
state. `onDaySelect` callback:

1. Updates local `selectedDate` for the visual highlight.
2. Dispatches a single-day range filter through
   `EventsPageContext.setCalendarFilter({ type: 'range', start: iso,
   end: iso, dateFields: [dateField] })`.
3. On toggle-off (CalendarSection emits `null`), clears via
   `{ type: 'clear' }`.

Filter-divergence effect: a `useEffect` watches
`filters.calendarFilter`. If the active filter no longer matches the
local `selectedDate` (because the user changed From/To, hit Clear, or
another component dispatched), `selectedDate` is reset to `null`.
Day-click takes precedence over From/To; manually editing From/To
clears the day selection via this effect.

#### Fix 6 — Grid open-in-full icon

In the view-selector row: `ViewSelectorDropdown` + flex spacer +
`<Button icon={<Open24Regular />} />` with tooltip "Open Events
list". Click dispatches `Xrm.Navigation.navigateTo({pageType:
'entitylist', entityName: 'sprk_event'}, {target: 2, 80% × 80%,
position: 1})` — the standard SpaarkeAi modal-launch pattern (same
`Open24Regular` icon and 80% sizing used by task 111 Documents
Expand and FilePreview "Open Record").

### 2. Files modified

- `src/client/shared/Spaarke.Events.Components/src/widgets/CalendarWorkspaceWidget/CalendarWorkspaceWidget.tsx`
- `src/client/shared/Spaarke.Events.Components/src/components/CalendarSection/CalendarSection.tsx`
  (VERSION bumped 1.0.0 → 1.1.0)

### 3. NOT modified

- `src/solutions/EventsPage/src/App.tsx` (standalone; CalendarSection
  backwards-compat keeps it byte-identical within rounding)
- `src/solutions/CalendarSidePane/` (separate CalendarSection copy —
  unaffected)
- BFF (zero new endpoints — `Xrm.Navigation.navigateTo` is the seam)

### 4. Bundle deltas

| Package | Before | After | Delta |
|---|---|---|---|
| @spaarke/events-components | tsc clean | tsc clean | — |
| EventsPage | 330.24 KB | 330.23 KB | -0.01 KB (parity) |
| LegalWorkspace | 588.32 KB | 588.72 KB | +0.40 KB |
| SpaarkeAi | 917.48 KB | 917.85 KB | +0.37 KB |

### 5. Operator-verifiable test flow

1. Load LegalWorkspace in SpaarkeAi. Click the Calendar workspace tab.
   The widget renders with: filter row at top (Filter by Date Field +
   From + To + spacer + caret-up chevron at far right), then the
   horizontal calendar strip (no Calendar sub-heading row, no
   separator line), then the toolbar (New / Delete / ... / Refresh /
   Calendar), then the view selector row (ViewSelectorDropdown +
   spacer + Open icon at far right), then the grid.
2. Confirm visible spacing between adjacent month grids (~20px gap).
3. Click a day with events on it (brand-blue tint). The grid below
   filters to that single day. The clicked day visually escalates
   to the "selected" state.
4. Click the same day again — selection toggles off; grid clears the
   date filter (other filters remain).
5. Click a different event-day — grid filter moves to the new day.
6. Manually set From/To to a multi-day range — grid filters to the
   range; previously-selected day-highlight clears
   (filter-divergence effect).
7. Click the caret-up chevron at the right edge of the filter row —
   calendar strip collapses; chevron flips to caret-down. The
   filter row stays visible (operator-critical) and From/To still
   drive the grid.
8. Reload the page — collapse state persists (localStorage). Click
   caret-down — strip re-appears with the same `viewDate`.
9. Click the Open icon at the right of the view-selector row — a
   modal opens at 80% × 80% showing the sprk_event entitylist.
10. EventsPage standalone code page: navigate to it directly, confirm
    the Calendar drawer (right-side overlay) still renders with its
    Calendar header + footer (vertical layout unchanged —
    backwards-compat verified).

### 6. ADR compliance

- **ADR-012** (shared lib reuse): both new CalendarSection props are

  byte-identical within rounding (-0.01 KB). Horizontal-layout
  header/footer suppression and event-day tint live in the shared

  `colorBrandBackground2Hover`, `colorBrandForeground1`,
  `fontWeightSemibold`). Zero hex / rgba literals introduced.
- **ADR-022** (React 19): all hooks remain React-19-compatible.
- **ADR-028** (auth via `Xrm.WebApi`): unchanged. The new entitylist
  modal uses `Xrm.Navigation.navigateTo` (Power Apps Client API), not a
  BFF call.

- ZERO new BFF endpoints / services / DI / NuGet / publish-size delta.
